### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Análise de Arquitetura e Plano de Refatoração

## 1. Análise da Arquitetura V11

```javascript
// src/analysis/v11-architecture-analysis.js
/**
 * Análise Técnica da Arquitetura V11
 * Data: 2024-01-15
 * Status: Em análise
 */

class V11ArchitectureAnalyzer {
  constructor() {
    this.findings = {
      acoplamento: [],
      resiliência: [],
      performance: [],
      débitoTécnico: []
    };
  }

  async analyzeCurrentCodebase() {
    // Análise de acoplamento
    this.findings.acoplamento = [
      {
        id: 'ACP-001',
        severity: 'HIGH',
        description: 'Serviço de WhatsApp acoplado diretamente ao core de negócios',
        location: 'src/services/whatsapp-core.js',
        impact: 'Falha no WhatsApp derruba todo o sistema',
        recommendation: 'Extrair para microserviço independente com circuit breaker'
      },
      {
        id: 'ACP-002',
        severity: 'MEDIUM',
        description: 'Banco de dados compartilhado entre múltiplos contextos',
        location: 'src/database/models.js',
        impact: 'Mudanças em um modelo afetam contextos não relacionados',
        recommendation: 'Implementar Database per Service pattern'
      },
      {
        id: 'ACP-003',
        severity: 'HIGH',
        description: 'LLM Agent com dependências diretas de UI',
        location: 'src/agents/llm-orchestrator.js',
        impact: 'Mudanças na UI requerem modificações no agente',
        recommendation: 'Introduzir camada de abstração com eventos'
      }
    ];

    // Análise de resiliência
    this.findings.resiliência = [
      {
        id: 'RES-001',
        severity: 'CRITICAL',
        description: 'Falta de circuit breaker em chamadas externas',
        location: 'src/integrations/*',
        impact: 'Falha em API externa causa cascata de erros',
        recommendation: 'Implementar resilience4j ou similar'
      },
      {
        id: 'RES-002',
        severity: 'HIGH',
        description: 'Sem retry com backoff exponencial',
        location: 'src/services/api-client.js',
        impact: 'Tentativas imediatas sobrecarregam serviços em recuperação',
        recommendation: 'Implementar política de retry inteligente'
      },
      {
        id: 'RES-003',
        severity: 'MEDIUM',
        description: 'Cache sem estratégia de invalidation',
        location: 'src/cache/manager.js',
        impact: 'Dados stale causam inconsistências',
        recommendation: 'Implementar TTL e cache-aside pattern'
      }
    ];

    // Análise de performance
    this.findings.performance = [
      {
        id: 'PERF-001',
        severity: 'HIGH',
        description: 'N+1 queries em loops de processamento',
        location: 'src/processors/batch-processor.js:47',
        impact: 'Degradação exponencial com volume',
        recommendation: 'Implementar eager loading ou batch queries'
      },
      {
        id: 'PERF-002',
        severity: 'MEDIUM',
        description: 'Serialização/deserialização redundante',
        location: 'src/middleware/json-parser.js',
        impact: 'CPU overhead desnecessário',
        recommendation: 'Usar binary protocols ou otimizar JSON handling'
      }
    ];

    // Débito técnico identificado
    this.findings.débitoTécnico = [
      {
        id: 'DT-001',
        effort: 'M',
        description: 'Refatorar monólito para arquitetura baseada em eventos',
        businessValue: 'Alta resiliência e escalabilidade',
        deadline: 'Sprint 3'
      },
      {
        id: 'DT-002',
        effort: 'S',
        description: 'Implementar health checks distribuídos',
        businessValue: 'Melhor observabilidade',
        deadline: 'Sprint 1'
      },
      {
        id: 'DT-003',
        effort: 'L',
        description: 'Migrar para message broker (RabbitMQ/Kafka)',
        businessValue: 'Desacoplamento assíncrono',
        deadline: 'Sprint 4'
      }
    ];

    return this.generateReport();
  }

  generateReport() {
    return {
      summary: {
        totalFindings: this.findings.acoplamento.length + 
                      this.findings.resiliência.length + 
                      this.findings.performance.length,
        criticalIssues: this.findings.resiliência.filter(f => f.severity === 'CRITICAL').length,
        highPriority: this.findings.acoplamento.filter(f => f.severity === 'HIGH').length +
                     this.findings.resiliência.filter(f => f.severity === 'HIGH').length
      },
      findings: this.findings,
      recommendations: this.generateMigrationPlan()
    };
  }

  generateMigrationPlan() {
    return {
      phase1: {
        name: 'Foundation & Observability',
        sprint: 'Sprint 1-2',
        tasks: [
          'Implementar logging estruturado (Pino/Winston)',
          'Configurar métricas com Prometheus',
          'Implementar health checks endpoints',
          'Setup de tracing distribuído (Jaeger)',
          'Criar dashboard básico de monitoramento'
        ],
        successCriteria: [
          '100% dos serviços com health checks',
          'Logs centralizados e pesquisáveis',
          'Métricas básicas coletadas'
        ]
      },
      phase2: {
        name: 'Resilience Patterns',
        sprint: 'Sprint 3-4',
        tasks: [
          'Implementar circuit breaker pattern',
          'Adicionar retry com backoff exponencial',
          'Configurar bulkhead isolation',
          'Implementar fallback strategies',
          'Criar chaos testing framework'
        ],
        successCriteria: [
          'Circuit breaker ativo em todas chamadas externas',
          'Retry policies configuradas',
          'Fallback handlers implementados'
        ]
      },
      phase3: {
        name: 'Decoupling & Events',
        sprint: 'Sprint 5-6',
        tasks: [
          'Extrair WhatsApp para microserviço',
          'Implementar message broker',
          'Migrar para event-driven architecture',
          'Criar API Gateway',
          'Implementar CQRS para queries complexas'
        ],
        successCriteria: [
          'WhatsApp service isolado e resiliente',
          'Eventos substituindo chamadas síncronas',
          'API Gateway roteando tráfego'
        ]
      },
      phase4: {
        name: 'Performance & Scalability',
        sprint: 'Sprint 7-8',
        tasks: [
          'Otimizar queries N+1',
          'Implementar cache distribuído (Redis)',
          'Configurar auto-scaling',
          'Otimizar serialização',
          'Implementar connection pooling'
        ],
        successCriteria: [
          'Latência reduzida em 50%',
          'Cache hit ratio > 80%',
          'Auto-scaling funcionando'
        ]
      }
    };
  }
}

module.exports = V11ArchitectureAnalyzer;
```

## 2. ADR: Arquitetura V12 - Event-Driven com Circuit Breaker

```markdown
# ADR-001: Migração para Arquitetura Baseada em Eventos com Circuit Breaker

Data: 2024-01-15
Status: Aceita
Autores: Tech Lead, Especialista Infra, Especialista LLM

## CONTEXTO:
A arquitetura atual (V11) apresenta alto acoplamento entre componentes, resultando em:
1. Falhas em cascata quando um serviço depende de outro
2. Dificuldade de escalar componentes individualmente
3. Complexidade no deployment e manutenção
4. Baixa resiliência em chamadas externas (WhatsApp API, LLM providers)

## DECISÃO:
Migrar para arquitetura baseada em eventos com os seguintes padrões:
1. **Event-Driven Architecture**: Comunicação assíncrona via message broker
2. **Circuit Breaker Pattern**: Isolamento de falhas em chamadas externas
3. **Database per Service**: Isolamento de dados por domínio
4. **API Gateway**: Ponto único de entrada com rate limiting e auth

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:

### Opção A: Refatoração incremental (Strangler Pattern)
- **Prós**: Baixo risco, migração gradual, negócio continua funcionando
- **Contras**: Custo de manutenção dupla, timeline estendida
- **Complexidade**: Média

### Opção B: Rewrite completo
- **Prós**: Arquitetura limpa, sem débito técnico herdado
- **Contras**: Alto risco, downtime prolongado, custo alto
- **Complexidade**: Alta

### Opção C: Híbrido com Modo Hive (ESCOLHIDA)
- **Prós**: Refatoração paralela com squad dedicada, risco controlado
- **Contras**: Coordenação necessária entre squads
- **Complexidade**: Média-Alta

## ARQUITETURA PROPOSTA V12:

```yaml
components:
  - api-gateway:
      tech: Express.js + Kong
      responsibility: Routing, rate limiting, authentication
      
  - whatsapp-service:
      tech: Node.js + Baileys
      responsibility: Comunicação WhatsApp isolada
      resilience: Circuit breaker + retry + fallback
      
  - llm-orchestrator:
      tech: Python/FastAPI
      responsibility: Roteamento inteligente entre modelos LLM
      features: Load balancing, fallback, cost optimization
      
  - event-bus:
      tech: RabbitMQ + Kafka para diferentes volumes
      patterns: Pub/Sub, Event Sourcing
      
  - database-layer:
      pattern: Database per service
      stores:
        - user-service: PostgreSQL
        - conversation-service: MongoDB
        - analytics-service: ClickHouse
```

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:

### Positivas:
1. **Resiliência**: Falhas isoladas não derrubam sistema
2. **Escalabilidade**: Componentes escalam independentemente
3. **Manutenibilidade**: Times podem trabalhar em serviços diferentes
4. **Observabilidade**: Melhor monitoramento por serviço

### Negativas:
1. **Complexidade**: Distributed systems challenges
2. **Latência**: Comunicação assíncrona adiciona overhead
3. **Custo**: Infraestrutura mais complexa
4. **Debugging**: Tracing distribuído necessário

### Riscos e Mitigações:
1. **Risco**: Perda de eventos durante migração
   **Mitigação**: Dual-write durante transição, DLQ (Dead Letter Queue)
   
2. **Risco**: Performance degradation
   **Mitigação**: Load testing antes de produção, gradual rollout
   
3. **Risco**: Data consistency
   **Mitigação**: Saga pattern, compensação transactions

## REVISÃO:
Reavaliar em 3 meses (2024-04-15) após implementação do Phase 2.
```

## 3. Plano de Refatoração com Modo Hive

```javascript
// src/refactoring/hive-mode-plan.js
/**
 * Plano de Refatoração V12 - Modo Hive
 * Duas squads trabalhando em paralelo:
 * 1. Hive Squad: Refatora componentes para nova arquitetura
 * 2. Core Squad: Mantém sistema atual funcionando
 */

class HiveModeRefactoringPlan {
  constructor() {
    this.phases = this.definePhases();
    this.coordination = this.setupCoordination();
    this.qualityGates = this.defineQualityGates();
  }

  definePhases() {
    return {
      preparation: {
        duration: '1 semana',
        tasks: [
          {
            id: 'PREP-001',
            description: 'Setup ambiente isolado para Hive Squad',
            owner: 'Infra Specialist',
            deliverables: ['K8s namespace', 'CI/CD pipeline separado']
          },
          {
            id: 'PREP-002',
            description: 'Definir contratos de interface entre squads',
            owner: 'Tech Lead',
            deliverables: ['API contracts', 'Event schemas']
          },
          {
            id: 'PREP-003',
            description: 'Implementar feature flags para gradual rollout',
            owner: 'Backend Dev',
            deliverables: ['LaunchDarkly config', 'Toggle endpoints']
          }
        ]
      },
      
      parallelDevelopment: {
        duration: '6 semanas',
        hiveSquad: {
          focus: 'Novos serviços desacoplados',
          milestones: [
            {
              week: 1,
              goal: 'WhatsApp Service com circuit breaker',
              integration: 'Feature flag para 1% do tráfego'
            },
            {
              week: 2,
              goal: 'Event Bus básico (RabbitMQ)',
              integration: 'Eventos de teste apenas'
            },
            {
              week: 3,
              goal: 'LLM Orchestrator com fallback',
              integration: 'Shadow mode - log only'
            },
            {
              week: 4,
              goal: 'API Gateway com rate limiting',
              integration: '10% do tráfego via gateway'
            },
            {
              week: 5,
              goal: 'Database separation proof-of-concept',
              integration: 'Read-only replicas'
            },
            {
              week: 6,
              goal: 'Full integration test',
              integration: 'Canary deployment ready'
            }
          ]
        },
        coreSquad: {
          focus: 'Manter V11 funcionando + bug fixes',
          constraints: [
            'Nenhuma nova feature complexa',
            'Apenas hotfixes críticos',
            'Preparar data migration scripts'
          ]
        }
      },
      
      integration: {
        duration: '2 semanas',
        tasks: [
          {
            id: 'INT-001',
            description: 'Canary deployment gradual',
            strategy: '5% → 25% → 50% → 100% do tráfego',
            rollbackPlan: 'Automático se error rate > 5%'
          },
          {
            id: 'INT-002',
            description: 'Data migration em batches',
            strategy: 'Dual-write durante 48h, then cutover',
            validation: 'Consistency checks automáticos'
          },
          {
            id: 'INT-003',
            description: 'Performance benchmarking',
            metrics: ['P99 latency', 'error rate', 'throughput'],
            acceptance: 'Melhoria ou igual à V11'
          }
        ]
      }
    };
  }

  setupCoordination() {
    return {
      dailySync: {
        time: '10:00 AM',
        duration: '15min',
        participants: ['Tech Leads de ambas squads', 'Squad Leaders'],
        agenda: ['Blockers', 'Integration points', 'Contract changes']
      },
      sharedArtifacts: {
        contractRegistry: 'https://github.com/diyapp/contracts',
        eventSchemaRepo: 'https://github.com/diyapp/events',
        deploymentDashboard: 'https://grafana.diyapp.com/hive-mode'
      },
      conflictResolution: {
        escalationPath: ['Tech Leads → Architecture Review Board → CTO'],
        timeToResolve: '4 horas máximo',
        fallback: 'Manter contrato anterior até resolução'
      }
    };
  }

  defineQualityGates() {
    return {
      preIntegration: [
        {
          gate: 'Test Coverage',
          requirement: '≥ 85% coverage por serviço',
          validation: 'CI pipeline bloqueia se abaixo'
        },
        {
          gate: 'Performance Tests',
          requirement: 'P95 latency < 200ms em carga esperada',
          validation: 'Load test automatizado'
        },
        {
          gate: 'Resilience Tests',
          requirement: 'Circuit breaker ativa após 5 falhas',
          validation: 'Chaos engineering tests'
        }
      ],
      preProduction: [
        {
          gate: 'Canary Metrics',
          requirement: 'Error rate < 1% por 24h',
          validation: 'Prometheus + Grafana alerts'
        },
        {
          gate: 'Business Metrics',
          requirement: 'Conversation completion rate mantido',
          validation: 'A/B test estatisticamente significativo'
        },
        {
          gate: 'Rollback Tested',
          requirement: 'Rollback completo em < 15min',
          validation: 'Disaster recovery drill'
        }
      ]
    };
  }

  generateMigrationChecklist() {
    return `
# Checklist de Migração V11 → V12

## Pré-requisitos
- [ ] Backup completo de banco de dados
- [ ] Snapshots de todos volumes
- [ ] Rollback plan documentado e testado
- [ ] Equipe de plantão 24/7 durante migração

## Fase 1: Read-Only Mode (00:00-01:00)
- [ ] Colocar sistema em modo manutenção
- [ ] Bloquear novas conversas
- [ ] Exportar estado atual para novo formato
- [ ] Validar consistência dos dados

## Fase 2: Dual-Write (01:00-48:00)
- [ ] Ativar dual-write para novos dados
- [ ] Monitorar latência em ambos sistemas
- [ ] Validar consistência em tempo real
- [ ] Coletar métricas de performance

## Fase 3: Cutover (48:00-49:00)
- [ ] Direcionar 100% do tráfego para V12
- [ ] Desativar writes na V11
- [ ] Executar migration final batch
- [ ] Validar completude

## Fase 4: Observação (49:00-72:00)
- [ ] Monitorar métricas críticas
- [ ] Equipe em alerta máximo
- [ ] Rollback automático se error rate > 5%
- [ ] Documentar lições aprendidas
    `;
  }
}

module.exports = HiveModeRefactoringPlan;
```

## 4. Dashboard de Monitoramento da Migração

```html
<!-- public/dashboard/migration-monitor.html -->
<!DOCTYPE

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Design System

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes visuais premium e suporte a dark/light mode. O sistema será 100% autônomo e seguirá os princípios de WCAG AA.

```html

            --transition-base: 250ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);

            --z-index-modal: 40;
            --z-index-popover: 50;
            --z-index-toast: 60;
            --z-index-tooltip: 70;
        }

        /* ============================================
           DARK MODE TOKENS
        ============================================ */
        [data-theme="dark"] {
            /* Cores primárias (ajustadas para contraste no dark mode) */
            --color-primary-50: #082f49;
            --color-primary-100: #0c4a6e;
            --color-primary-200: #075985;
            --color-primary-300: #0369a1;
            --color-primary-400: #0284c7;
            --color-primary-500: #0ea5e9;
            --color-primary-600: #38bdf8;
            --color-primary-700: #7dd3fc;
            --color-primary-800: #bae6fd;
            --color-primary-900: #e0f2fe;
            --color-primary-950: #f0f9ff;
            
            /* Cores neutras (invertidas para dark mode) */
            --color-neutral-50: #0a0a0a;
            --color-neutral-100: #171717;
            --color-neutral-200: #262626;
            --color-neutral-300: #404040;

```python
# src/core/api/graphql/schema.py
"""
GraphQL schema definition for DIYAPP Evolution V12 Core
Hybrid GraphQL/REST architecture with circuit breaker and service layer caching
"""
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime
import graphene
from graphene import ObjectType, String, Int, Float, Boolean, List as GrapheneList, Field
from graphene.relay import Node, Connection
from graphql import GraphQLError

# Service layer imports
from src.core.services.circuit_breaker import CircuitBreakerRegistry
from src.core.services.cache_service import DistributedCache
from src.core.monitoring.metrics import APIMetricsCollector

class UserNode(ObjectType):
    """User type with GraphQL Node interface"""
    class Meta:
        interfaces = (Node,)
    
    id = graphene.ID(required=True)
    email = String(required=True)
    username = String(required=True)
    created_at = String(required=True)
    last_login = String()
    
    @classmethod
    def get_node(cls, info, id):
        """Resolve single user by ID with circuit breaker protection"""
        user_service = info.context["user_service"]
        cache_key = f"user:{id}"
        
        # Try cache first
        cached = user_service.cache.get(cache_key)
        if cached:
            APIMetricsCollector.record_cache_hit("user")
            return cls(**cached)
        
        # Use circuit breaker for DB call
        with user_service.circuit_breaker("user_db"):
            user = user_service.get_user_by_id(id)
            if not user:
                raise GraphQLError(f"User {id} not found")
            
            # Cache for 5 minutes
            user_service.cache.set(cache_key, user.to_dict(), ttl=300)
            APIMetricsCollector.record_cache_miss("user")
            
            return cls(**user.to_dict())

class ProductNode(ObjectType):
    """Product type with inventory and pricing"""
    class Meta:
        interfaces = (Node,)
    
    id = graphene.ID(required=True)
    name = String(required=True)
    sku = String(required=True)
    price = Float(required=True)
    inventory = Int(required=True)
    category = String()
    tags = GrapheneList(String)
    
    # Computed field with caching
    is_available = Boolean()
    
    def resolve_is_available(self, info):
        """Resolve availability with business logic"""
        product_service = info.context["product_service"]
        cache_key = f"product_availability:{self.id}"
        
        # Check cache for availability status
        cached = product_service.cache.get(cache_key)
        if cached is not None:
            return cached
        
        # Compute availability (business logic)
        available = self.inventory > 0
        
        # Cache with shorter TTL for dynamic data
        product_service.cache.set(cache_key, available, ttl=30)
        
        return available

class OrderNode(ObjectType):
    """Order type with relationships"""
    class Meta:
        interfaces = (Node,)
    
    id = graphene.ID(required=True)
    user_id = String(required=True)
    status = String(required=True)
    total_amount = Float(required=True)
    created_at = String(required=True)
    items = GrapheneList(lambda: OrderItemNode)
    
    # Resolve user relationship
    user = Field(UserNode)
    
    def resolve_user(self, info):
        """Resolve user with DataLoader for N+1 prevention"""
        return info.context["user_loader"].load(self.user_id)
    
    def resolve_items(self, info):
        """Resolve order items"""
        order_service = info.context["order_service"]
        cache_key = f"order_items:{self.id}"
        
        # Batch loading with caching
        items = order_service.get_order_items_batch([self.id], cache_key)
        return [OrderItemNode(**item) for item in items]

class OrderItemNode(ObjectType):
    """Order item type"""
    id = graphene.ID(required=True)
    order_id = String(required=True)
    product_id = String(required=True)
    quantity = Int(required=True)
    unit_price = Float(required=True)
    
    # Resolve product
    product = Field(ProductNode)
    
    def resolve_product(self, info):
        """Resolve product with circuit breaker"""
        product_service = info.context["product_service"]
        
        # Use circuit breaker for product service
        with product_service.circuit_breaker("product_service"):
            return product_service.get_product(self.product_id)

class Query(ObjectType):
    """Root GraphQL query with hybrid REST fallback support"""
    
    # Single entity queries
    user = Field(UserNode, id=graphene.ID(required=True))
    product = Field(ProductNode, id=graphene.ID(required=True))
    order = Field(OrderNode, id=graphene.ID(required=True))
    
    # List queries with pagination
    users = GrapheneList(
        UserNode,
        limit=Int(default_value=20),
        offset=Int(default_value=0)
    )
    
    products = GrapheneList(
        ProductNode,
        category=String(),
        in_stock=Boolean(),
        limit=Int(default_value=50),
        offset=Int(default_value=0)
    )
    
    # Resolvers with circuit breaker and caching
    def resolve_user(self, info, id):
        """Resolve user query"""
        return UserNode.get_node(info, id)
    
    def resolve_product(self, info, id):
        """Resolve product with fallback to REST if GraphQL fails"""
        product_service = info.context["product_service"]
        
        try:
            # Try GraphQL resolution first
            return ProductNode.get_node(info, id)
        except Exception as e:
            APIMetricsCollector.record_error("graphql_product_resolution")
            
            # Fallback to REST endpoint
            with product_service.circuit_breaker("product_fallback"):
                rest_data = product_service.get_product_rest(id)
                return ProductNode(**rest_data)
    
    def resolve_products(self, info, category=None, in_stock=None, limit=50, offset=0):
        """Resolve products list with advanced caching"""
        product_service = info.context["product_service"]
        cache_key = f"products:{category}:{in_stock}:{limit}:{offset}"
        
        # Check cache for product lists
        cached = product_service.cache.get(cache_key)
        if cached:
            APIMetricsCollector.record_cache_hit("products_list")
            return [ProductNode(**p) for p in cached]
        
        # Use circuit breaker for DB query
        with product_service.circuit_breaker("products_db"):
            products = product_service.get_products(
                category=category,
                in_stock=in_stock,
                limit=limit,
                offset=offset
            )
            
            # Cache with invalidation tags
            product_service.cache.set(
                cache_key, 
                [p.to_dict() for p in products],
                ttl=60,
                tags=[f"category:{category}" if category else "all_products"]
            )
            
            APIMetricsCollector.record_cache_miss("products_list")
            return [ProductNode(**p.to_dict()) for p in products]

class Mutation(ObjectType):
    """GraphQL mutations with transactional integrity"""
    
    class CreateOrder(graphene.Mutation):
        """Create order mutation with inventory check"""
        class Arguments:
            user_id = graphene.ID(required=True)
            items = graphene.List(graphene.NonNull(
                graphene.InputField(
                    type=graphene.InputObjectType(
                        "OrderItemInput",
                        product_id=graphene.ID(required=True),
                        quantity=graphene.Int(required=True, min_value=1)
                    )
                )
            ))
        
        order = Field(OrderNode)
        success = Boolean()
        errors = GrapheneList(String)
        
        @staticmethod
        def mutate(root, info, user_id, items):
            """Execute order creation with circuit breakers"""
            order_service = info.context["order_service"]
            product_service = info.context["product_service"]
            
            errors = []
            
            # Validate user exists with circuit breaker
            try:
                with order_service.circuit_breaker("user_validation"):
                    if not order_service.user_exists(user_id):
                        errors.append(f"User {user_id} not found")
            except Exception as e:
                errors.append("User service temporarily unavailable")
                APIMetricsCollector.record_circuit_open("user_validation")
            
            # Check inventory for all items
            for item in items:
                try:
                    with product_service.circuit_breaker("inventory_check"):
                        available = product_service.check_inventory(
                            item["product_id"], 
                            item["quantity"]
                        )
                        if not available:
                            errors.append(
                                f"Insufficient inventory for product {item['product_id']}"
                            )
                except Exception as e:
                    errors.append(
                        f"Inventory service unavailable for product {item['product_id']}"
                    )
                    APIMetricsCollector.record_circuit_open("inventory_check")
            
            if errors:
                return CreateOrder(success=False, errors=errors, order=None)
            
            # Create order with transaction
            try:
                with order_service.circuit_breaker("order_creation"):
                    order = order_service.create_order(user_id, items)
                    
                    # Invalidate relevant caches
                    order_service.cache.invalidate_tags([f"user_orders:{user_id}"])
                    for item in items:
                        product_service.cache.delete(f"product:{item['product_id']}")
                    
                    return CreateOrder(
                        success=True,
                        errors=[],
                        order=OrderNode(**order.to_dict())
                    )
            except Exception as e:
                APIMetricsCollector.record_error("order_creation")
                return CreateOrder(
                    success=False,
                    errors=["Order creation failed"],
                    order=None
                )
    
    class UpdateProductInventory(graphene.Mutation):
        """Update product inventory with cache invalidation"""
        class Arguments:
            product_id = graphene.ID(required=True)
            delta = graphene.Int(required=True)  # Positive to add, negative to remove
        
        product = Field(ProductNode)
        success = Boolean()
        new_inventory = Int()
        
        @staticmethod
        def mutate(root, info, product_id, delta):
            product_service = info.context["product_service"]
            
            try:
                with product_service.circuit_breaker("inventory_update"):
                    # Update inventory
                    product = product_service.update_inventory(product_id, delta)
                    
                    # Invalidate all caches for this product
                    cache_keys = [
                        f"product:{product_id}",
                        f"product_availability:{product_id}",
                        "products:*"  # Wildcard for all product lists
                    ]
                    product_service.cache.delete_many(cache_keys)
                    
                    # Also invalidate by tags
                    product_service.cache.invalidate_tags([
                        f"product:{product_id}",
                        "all_products"
                    ])
                    
                    return UpdateProductInventory(
                        success=True,
                        product=ProductNode(**product.to_dict()),
                        new_inventory=product.inventory
                    )
            except Exception as e:
                APIMetricsCollector.record_error("inventory_update")
                return UpdateProductInventory(
                    success=False,
                    product=None,
                    new_inventory=None
                )
    
    # Register mutations
    create_order = CreateOrder.Field()
    update_product_inventory = UpdateProductInventory.Field()

# Create GraphQL schema
schema = graphene.Schema(query=Query, mutation=Mutation)
```

```python
# src/core/services/circuit_breaker.py
"""
Circuit breaker implementation for service resilience
Based on Netflix Hystrix patterns
"""
import time
from enum import Enum
from typing import Callable, Optional, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass
from threading import Lock
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class CircuitState(Enum):
    """Circuit breaker states"""
    CLOSED = "CLOSED"      # Normal operation
    OPEN = "OPEN"          # Circuit open, failing fast
    HALF_OPEN = "HALF_OPEN" # Testing if service recovered

@dataclass
class CircuitBreakerConfig:
    """Configuration for circuit breaker"""
    failure_threshold: int = 5        # Failures before opening
    reset_timeout: int = 30           # Seconds before half-open
    half_open_max_calls: int = 3      # Max calls in half-open state
    sliding_window_size: int = 10     # Window for failure rate calculation
    min_number_of_calls: int = 5      # Min calls before calculating failure rate

class CircuitBreaker:
    """Circuit breaker implementation"""
    
    def __init__(
        self, 
        name: str,
        config: Optional[CircuitBreakerConfig] = None
    ):
        self.name = name
        self.config = config or CircuitBreakerConfig()
        self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.last_failure_time = 0
        self.half_open_success_count = 0
        self.lock = Lock()
        
        # Metrics
        self.total_calls = 0
        self.failed_calls = 0
        self.circuit_opened_count = 0
        
        logger.info(f"CircuitBreaker '{name}' initialized")
    
    def execute(self, func: Callable, *args, **kwargs) -> Any:
        """Execute function with circuit breaker protection"""
        with self.lock:
            self.total_calls += 1
            
            # Check if circuit is open
            if self.state == CircuitState.OPEN:
                # Check if reset timeout has passed
                if time.time() - self.last_failure_time > self.config.reset_timeout:
                    self.state = CircuitState.HALF_OPEN
                    self.half_open_success_count = 0
                    logger.info(f"Circuit '{self.name}' moved to HALF_OPEN")
                else:
                    self.failed_calls += 1
                    raise CircuitBreakerOpenError(
                        f"Circuit '{self.name}' is OPEN. "
                        f"Last failure: {self.last_failure_time}"
                    )
            
            # Execute the function
            try:
                result = func(*args, **kwargs)
                
                # Handle success
                if self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
                    self.half_open_success_count += 1
                    if self.half_open_success_count >= self.config.half_open_max_calls:
                        self._reset_circuit()
                        logger.info(f"Circuit '{self.name}' reset to CLOSED")
                
                return result
                
            except Exception as e:
                self._handle_failure(e)
                raise
    
    def _handle_failure(self, error: Exception):
        """Handle function failure"""
        self.failure_count += 1
        self.failed_calls += 1
        self.last_failure_time = time.time()
        
        logger.warning(
            f"Circuit '{self.name}' failure {self.failure_count}/"
            f"{self.config.failure_threshold}: {error}"
        )
        
        # Check if we should open the circuit
        if (self.state == CircuitState.CLOSED and 
            self.failure_count >= self.config.failure_threshold):
            
            self.state = CircuitState.OPEN
            self.circuit_opened_count += 1
            
            logger.error(
                f"Circuit '{self.name}' opened due to {self.failure_count} failures"
            )
        
        elif self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
            # Half-open call failed, back to OPEN
            self.state = CircuitState.OPEN
            logger.warning(f"Circuit '{self.name}' re-opened from HALF_OPEN")
    
    def _reset_circuit(self):
        """Reset circuit to closed state"""
        self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.half_open_success_count = 0
    
    def get_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get circuit breaker metrics"""
        failure_rate = (
            (self.failed_calls / self.total_calls * 100) 
            if self.total_calls > 0 else 0
        )
        
        return {
            "name": self.name,
            "state": self.state.value,
            "failure_count": self.failure_count,
            "total_calls": self.total_calls,
            "failed_calls": self.failed_calls,
            "failure_rate_percent": round(failure_rate, 2),
            "circuit_opened_count": self.circuit_opened_count,
            "last_failure_time": self.last_failure_time,
            "is_healthy": self.state != CircuitState.OPEN
        }

class CircuitBreakerOpenError(Exception):
    """Exception raised when circuit breaker is open"""
    pass

class CircuitBreakerRegistry:
    """Registry for managing multiple circuit breakers"""
    
    _instance = None
    _breakers: Dict[str, CircuitBreaker] = {}
    _registry_lock = Lock()
    
    def __new__(cls):
        if cls._instance is None:
            cls._instance = super().__new__(cls)
        return cls._instance
    
    @classmethod
    def get_breaker(
        cls, 
        name: str,
        config: Optional[CircuitBreakerConfig] = None
    ) -> CircuitBreaker:
        """Get or create a circuit breaker"""
        with cls._registry_lock:
            if name not in cls._breakers:
                cls._breakers[name] = CircuitBreaker(name, config)
            return cls._breakers[name]
    
    @classmethod
    def get_all_metrics(cls) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Get metrics for all circuit breakers"""
        return [breaker.get_metrics() for breaker in cls._breakers.values()]
    
    @classmethod
    def reset_breaker(cls, name: str):
        """Reset a specific circuit breaker"""
        with cls._registry_lock:
            if name in cls._breakers:
                breaker = cls._breakers[name]
                breaker.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
                breaker.failure_count = 0
                logger.info(f"Circuit breaker '{name}' manually reset")
```

"""
Distributed cache service with Redis backend and local L1 cache
"""
import json
import pickle
from typing import Any, Optional, List, Dict

from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import redis

import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class CacheLayer:
    """Abstract cache layer interface"""
    
    def get(self, key: str) -> Optional[Any]:
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def set(self, key: str, value: Any, ttl: Optional[int] = None, **kwargs):
        raise NotImplementedError
    
    def delete(self, key: str

```typescript
// src/App.tsx - Ponto de entrada principal com lazy loading e estado global otimizado
import React, { Suspense, lazy, useEffect } from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { ErrorBoundary } from 'react-error-boundary';
import { Provider } from 'react-redux';
import { configureStore } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import { ThemeProvider } from 'styled-components';

// Estado global otimizado com Redux Toolkit
import rootReducer from './store/rootReducer';
import { initializeApp } from './store/slices/appSlice';

// Componentes de UI
import { GlobalStyles } from './styles/GlobalStyles';
import { theme } from './styles/theme';
import LoadingSpinner from './components/ui/LoadingSpinner';
import ErrorFallback from './components/ui/ErrorFallback';
import Layout from './components/layout/Layout';

// Lazy loading de rotas principais
const Dashboard = lazy(() => import('./pages/Dashboard'));
const Analytics = lazy(() => import('./pages/Analytics'));
const Settings = lazy(() => import('./pages/Settings'));
const AIStudio = lazy(() => import('./pages/AIStudio'));
const AgentManager = lazy(() => import('./pages/AgentManager'));

// Configuração do store Redux com middleware otimizado
const store = configureStore({
  reducer: rootReducer,
  middleware: (getDefaultMiddleware) =>
    getDefaultMiddleware({
      serializableCheck: false,
      immutableCheck: { warnAfter: 128 },
    }),
  devTools: process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production',
});

// Componente principal da aplicação
const App: React.FC = () => {
  useEffect(() => {
    // Inicialização da aplicação
    store.dispatch(initializeApp());
    
    // Monitoramento de performance
    if ('performance' in window) {
      const perfObserver = new PerformanceObserver((list) => {
        for (const entry of list.getEntries()) {
          if (entry.entryType === 'largest-contentful-paint') {
            console.log('LCP:', entry.startTime);
          }
        }
      });
      perfObserver.observe({ entryTypes: ['largest-contentful-paint', 'layout-shift'] });
    }
  }, []);

  return (
    <ErrorBoundary FallbackComponent={ErrorFallback}>
      <Provider store={store}>
        <ThemeProvider theme={theme}>
          <GlobalStyles />
          <Router>
            <Layout>
              <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner fullScreen />}>
                <Routes>
                  <Route path="/" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
                  <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
                  <Route path="/analytics" element={<Analytics />} />
                  <Route path="/settings" element={<Settings />} />
                  <Route path="/ai-studio" element={<AIStudio />} />
                  <Route path="/agent-manager" element={<AgentManager />} />
                  <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
                </Routes>
              </Suspense>
            </Layout>
          </Router>
        </ThemeProvider>
      </Provider>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
};

export default App;
```

```typescript
// src/store/rootReducer.ts - Estado global otimizado
import { combineReducers } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import { persistReducer } from 'redux-persist';
import storage from 'redux-persist/lib/storage';

// Slices
import appReducer from './slices/appSlice';
import uiReducer from './slices/uiSlice';
import agentsReducer from './slices/agentsSlice';
import aiReducer from './slices/aiSlice';

// Configuração de persistência seletiva
const persistConfig = {
  key: 'diyapp-root',
  storage,
  whitelist: ['ui', 'agents'], // Apenas estados que precisam persistir
  version: 1,
  migrate: (state: any) => {
    // Migração de versões anteriores
    if (!state?._persist?.version || state._persist.version < 1) {
      return Promise.resolve({
        ...state,
        _persist: { version: 1, rehydrated: false },
      });
    }
    return Promise.resolve(state);
  },
};

const rootReducer = combineReducers({
  app: appReducer,
  ui: uiReducer,
  agents: agentsReducer,
  ai: aiReducer,
});

export default persistReducer(persistConfig, rootReducer);
```

```typescript
// src/store/slices/agentsSlice.ts - Slice otimizado para gerenciamento de agentes
import { createSlice, createAsyncThunk, createEntityAdapter } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import type { PayloadAction } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';

interface Agent {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: 'frontend' | 'backend' | 'ai' | 'qa';
  status: 'active' | 'idle' | 'error';
  performance: number;
  lastActive: string;
  config: Record<string, any>;
}

// Entity adapter para otimização de updates
const agentsAdapter = createEntityAdapter<Agent>({
  selectId: (agent) => agent.id,
  sortComparer: (a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name),
});

// Thunks assíncronos
export const fetchAgents = createAsyncThunk(
  'agents/fetchAll',
  async (_, { rejectWithValue }) => {
    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/agents');
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch agents');
      return await response.json();
    } catch (error) {
      return rejectWithValue(error.message);
    }
  }
);

export const updateAgentConfig = createAsyncThunk(
  'agents/updateConfig',
  async ({ id, config }: { id: string; config: Record<string, any> }, { rejectWithValue }) => {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`/api/agents/${id}/config`, {
        method: 'PATCH',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(config),
      });
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to update agent');
      return await response.json();
    } catch (error) {
      return rejectWithValue(error.message);
    }
  }
);

const agentsSlice = createSlice({
  name: 'agents',
  initialState: agentsAdapter.getInitialState({
    loading: false,
    error: null as string | null,
    lastUpdated: null as string | null,
  }),
  reducers: {
    agentStatusUpdated: agentsAdapter.updateOne,
    agentAdded: agentsAdapter.addOne,
    agentRemoved: agentsAdapter.removeOne,
    clearError: (state) => {
      state.error = null;
    },
  },
  extraReducers: (builder) => {
    builder
      .addCase(fetchAgents.pending, (state) => {
        state.loading = true;
        state.error = null;
      })
      .addCase(fetchAgents.fulfilled, (state, action: PayloadAction<Agent[]>) => {
        agentsAdapter.setAll(state, action.payload);
        state.loading = false;
        state.lastUpdated = new Date().toISOString();
      })
      .addCase(fetchAgents.rejected, (state, action) => {
        state.loading = false;
        state.error = action.payload as string;
      })
      .addCase(updateAgentConfig.fulfilled, (state, action: PayloadAction<Agent>) => {
        agentsAdapter.updateOne(state, {
          id: action.payload.id,
          changes: action.payload,
        });
      });
  },
});

export const { selectAll: selectAllAgents, selectById: selectAgentById } =
  agentsAdapter.getSelectors((state: any) => state.agents);

export const { agentStatusUpdated, agentAdded, agentRemoved, clearError } = agentsSlice.actions;
export default agentsSlice.reducer;
```

```typescript
// src/components/layout/Layout.tsx - Layout otimizado com React.memo
import React, { memo, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useSelector, useDispatch } from 'react-redux';
import styled from 'styled-components';
import { selectSidebarCollapsed, toggleSidebar } from '../../store/slices/uiSlice';
import Sidebar from './Sidebar';
import Header from './Header';

const LayoutContainer = styled.div`
  display: flex;
  min-height: 100vh;
  background: ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.background.primary};
`;

const MainContent = styled.main<{ $sidebarCollapsed: boolean }>`
  flex: 1;
  margin-left: ${({ $sidebarCollapsed, theme }) =>
    $sidebarCollapsed ? theme.spacing.sidebar.collapsed : theme.spacing.sidebar.expanded};
  transition: margin-left ${({ theme }) => theme.transitions.normal};
  padding: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.lg};
  overflow-y: auto;
  max-height: 100vh;

  @media (max-width: ${({ theme }) => theme.breakpoints.md}) {
    margin-left: 0;
    padding: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.md};
  }
`;

const Layout: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = memo(({ children }) => {
  const dispatch = useDispatch();
  const sidebarCollapsed = useSelector(selectSidebarCollapsed);
  const [mobileMenuOpen, setMobileMenuOpen] = useState(false);

  const handleSidebarToggle = useCallback(() => {
    dispatch(toggleSidebar());
  }, [dispatch]);

  const handleMobileMenuToggle = useCallback(() => {
    setMobileMenuOpen((prev) => !prev);
  }, []);

  return (
    <LayoutContainer>
      <Sidebar
        collapsed={sidebarCollapsed}
        mobileOpen={mobileMenuOpen}
        onMobileClose={() => setMobileMenuOpen(false)}
      />
      <MainContent $sidebarCollapsed={sidebarCollapsed}>
        <Header
          onMenuToggle={handleSidebarToggle}
          onMobileMenuToggle={handleMobileMenuToggle}
        />
        {children}
      </MainContent>
    </LayoutContainer>
  );
});

Layout.displayName = 'Layout';

export default Layout;
```

```typescript
// src/components/AgentCard.tsx - Componente otimizado com React.memo e useMemo
import React, { memo, useMemo, useCallback } from 'react';
import styled from 'styled-components';
import { Agent } from '../store/slices/agentsSlice';
import PerformanceIndicator from './ui/PerformanceIndicator';
import StatusBadge from './ui/StatusBadge';

interface AgentCardProps {
  agent: Agent;
  onSelect: (id: string) => void;
  onConfigUpdate: (id: string, config: Record<string, any>) => void;
}

const Card = styled.div`
  background: ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.background.card};
  border-radius: ${({ theme }) => theme.borderRadius.lg};
  padding: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.lg};
  box-shadow: ${({ theme }) => theme.shadows.sm};
  transition: all ${({ theme }) => theme.transitions.fast};
  border: 1px solid ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.border.default};
  
  &:hover {
    box-shadow: ${({ theme }) => theme.shadows.md};
    transform: translateY(-2px);
    border-color: ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.primary.main};
  }
  
  &:focus-within {
    outline: 2px solid ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.primary.main};
    outline-offset: 2px;
  }
`;

const CardHeader = styled.div`
  display: flex;
  justify-content: space-between;
  align-items: center;
  margin-bottom: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.md};
`;

const AgentName = styled.h3`
  margin: 0;
  color: ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.text.primary};
  font-size: ${({ theme }) => theme.typography.fontSizes.lg};
  font-weight: ${({ theme }) => theme.typography.fontWeights.semibold};
`;

const AgentType = styled.span`
  color: ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.text.secondary};
  font-size: ${({ theme }) => theme.typography.fontSizes.sm};
  text-transform: uppercase;
  letter-spacing: 0.5px;
`;

const CardBody = styled.div`
  display: grid;
  grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr;
  gap: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.md};
  margin-bottom: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.lg};
`;

const StatItem = styled.div`
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
`;

const StatLabel = styled.span`
  color: ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.text.secondary};
  font-size: ${({ theme }) => theme.typography.fontSizes.xs};
  margin-bottom: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.xs};
`;

const StatValue = styled.span`
  color: ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.text.primary};
  font-size: ${({ theme }) => theme.typography.fontSizes.md};
  font-weight: ${({ theme }) => theme.typography.fontWeights.medium};
`;

const CardFooter = styled.div`
  display: flex;
  justify-content: space-between;
  align-items: center;
  padding-top: ${({ theme }) => theme.spacing.md};
  border-top: 1px solid ${({ theme }) => theme.colors.border.subtle};
`;

const AgentCard: React.FC<AgentCardProps> = memo(({ agent, onSelect, onConfigUpdate }) => {
  const handleSelect = useCallback(() => {
    onSelect(agent.id);
  }, [agent.id, onSelect]);

  const handleKeyDown = useCallback((e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleSelect();
    }
  }, [handleSelect]);

  // Memoize derived values
  const lastActiveFormatted = useMemo(() => {
    const date = new Date(agent.lastActive);
    return date.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', {
      day: '2-digit',
      month: 'short',
      hour: '2-digit',
      minute: '2-digit',
    });
  }, [agent.lastActive]);

  const performanceColor = useMemo(() => {
    if (agent.performance >= 90) return 'success';
    if (agent.performance >= 70) return 'warning';
    return 'error';
  }, [agent.performance]);

  return (
    <Card
      role="button"
      tabIndex={0}
      onClick={handleSelect}
      onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
      aria-label={`Agente ${agent.name}, ${agent.type}, performance ${agent.performance}%`}
    >
      <CardHeader>
        <div>
          <AgentName>{agent.name}</AgentName>
          <AgentType>{agent.type}</AgentType>
        </div>
        <StatusBadge status={agent.status} />
      </CardHeader>
      
      <CardBody>
        <StatItem>
          <StatLabel>Performance</StatLabel>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '8px' }}>
            <StatValue>{agent.performance}%</StatValue>
            <PerformanceIndicator value={agent.performance} color={performanceColor} />
          </div>
        </StatItem>
        
        <StatItem>
          <StatLabel>Última Atividade</StatLabel>
          <StatValue>{lastActiveFormatted}</StatValue>
        </StatItem>
      </CardBody>
      
      <CardFooter>
        <button
          onClick={(e) => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            onConfigUpdate(agent.id, agent.config);
          }}
          aria-label={`Configurar agente ${agent.name}`}
        >
          Configurar
        </button>
        <span aria-hidden="true">→</span>
      </CardFooter>
    </Card>
  );
});

AgentCard.displayName = 'AgentCard';

export default AgentCard;
```

```typescript
// src/hooks/useOptimizedFetch.ts - Hook customizado para fetch otimizado
import { useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useDispatch } from 'react-redux';

interface UseOptimizedFetchOptions {
  maxRetries?: number;
  retryDelay?: number;
  cacheTime?: number;
}

export const useOptimizedFetch = <T>(
  url: string,
  options: UseOptimizedFetchOptions = {}
) => {
  const {
    maxRetries = 3,
    retryDelay = 1000,
    cacheTime = 30000, // 30 segundos
  } = options;

  const dispatch = useDispatch();
  const cacheRef = useRef<Map<string, { data: T; timestamp: number }>>(new Map());
  const abortControllerRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);

  const fetchWithRetry = useCallback(
    async (retryCount = 0): Promise<T> => {
      // Verificar cache primeiro
      const cached = cacheRef.current.get(url);
      if (cached && Date.now() - cached.timestamp < cacheTime) {
        return cached.data;
      }

      // Cancelar request anterior
      if (abortControllerRef.current) {
        abortControllerRef.current.abort();
      }

      abortControllerRef.current = new AbortController();

      try {
        const response = await fetch(url, {
          signal: abortControllerRef.current.signal,
          headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          },
        });

        if (!response.ok) {
          throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}: ${response.statusText}`);
        }

        const data = await response.json();
        
        // Armazenar em cache
        cacheRef.current.set(url, { data, timestamp: Date.now() });
        
        return data;
      } catch (error) {
        if (error.name === 'AbortError') {
          throw error;
        }

        if (retryCount < maxRetries) {
          await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, retryDelay * (2 ** retryCount)));
          return fetchWithRetry(retryCount + 1);
        }

        throw error;
      }
    },
    [url, maxRetries, retryDelay, cacheTime]
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (abortControllerRef.current) {
        abortControllerRef.current.abort();
      }
    };
  }, []);

  const

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infraestrutura como Código e CI/CD

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-core/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   ├── outputs.tf
│   ├── providers.tf
│   ├── modules/

## 1. Terraform - Infraestrutura como Código

### `terraform/main.tf`

```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
  }

  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key            = "v12-core/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "terraform-locks"
  }
}

# Módulo VPC
module "vpc" {
  source = "./modules/vpc"

  environment = var.environment
  vpc_cidr    = var.vpc_cidr
  azs         = var.availability_zones
}

# Módulo ECS (Fargate)
module "ecs" {
  source = "./modules/ecs"

  environment     = var.environment
  vpc_id         = module.vpc.vpc_id
  private_subnets = module.vpc.private_subnets
  public_subnets  = module.vpc.public_subnets

  container_image = var.container_image
  container_port  = var.container_port
  cpu             = var.container_cpu
  memory          = var.container_memory

  desired_count   = var.desired_count
  min_capacity    = var.min_capacity
  max_capacity    = var.max_capacity

  health_check_path = var.health_check_path
}

# Módulo RDS (PostgreSQL)
module "rds" {
  source = "./modules/rds"

  environment    = var.environment
  vpc_id        = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids    = module.vpc.database_subnets

  db_name       = var.db_name
  db_username   = var.db_username
  db_password   = var.db_password
  db_instance_class = var.db_instance_class
}

# Módulo de Monitoramento
module "monitoring" {
  source = "./modules/monitoring"

  environment    = var.environment
  ecs_cluster_name = module.ecs.cluster_name
  ecs_service_name = module.ecs.service_name
  alb_arn_suffix  = module.ecs.alb_arn_suffix

  # SLOs configurados
  availability_slo    = 99.9  # 99.9%
  latency_slo_p95    = 300   # 300ms
  error_rate_slo     = 0.1   # 0.1%
}
```

### `terraform/modules/ecs/main.tf`

```hcl
resource "aws_ecs_cluster" "main" {
  name = "diyapp-${var.environment}-cluster"

  setting {
    name  = "containerInsights"
    value = "enabled"
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

resource "aws_ecs_task_definition" "main" {
  family                   = "diyapp-${var.environment}-task"
  network_mode             = "awsvpc"
  requires_compatibilities = ["FARGATE"]
  cpu                      = var.cpu
  memory                   = var.memory
  execution_role_arn       = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_execution_role.arn
  task_role_arn           = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_role.arn

  container_definitions = jsonencode([
    {
      name      = "diyapp-container"
      image     = var.container_image
      cpu       = var.cpu
      memory    = var.memory
      essential = true
      portMappings = [
        {
          containerPort = var.container_port
          hostPort      = var.container_port
          protocol      = "tcp"
        }
      ]
      environment = [
        {
          name  = "NODE_ENV"
          value = var.environment
        },
        {
          name  = "PORT"
          value = tostring(var.container_port)
        }
      ]
      logConfiguration = {
        logDriver = "awslogs"
        options = {
          awslogs-group         = aws_cloudwatch_log_group.main.name
          awslogs-region        = data.aws_region.current.name
          awslogs-stream-prefix = "ecs"
        }
      }
      healthCheck = {
        command     = ["CMD-SHELL", "curl -f http://localhost:${var.container_port}${var.health_check_path} || exit 1"]
        interval    = 30
        timeout     = 5
        retries     = 3
        startPeriod = 60
      }
    }
  ])

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

resource "aws_ecs_service" "main" {
  name            = "diyapp-${var.environment}-service"
  cluster         = aws_ecs_cluster.main.id
  task_definition = aws_ecs_task_definition.main.arn
  desired_count   = var.desired_count
  launch_type     = "FARGATE"

  network_configuration {
    subnets          = var.private_subnets
    security_groups  = [aws_security_group.ecs_tasks.id]
    assign_public_ip = false
  }

  load_balancer {
    target_group_arn = aws_lb_target_group.main.arn
    container_name   = "diyapp-container"
    container_port   = var.container_port
  }

  deployment_controller {
    type = "CODE_DEPLOY"
  }

  deployment_circuit_breaker {
    enable   = true
    rollback = true
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

# Application Load Balancer
resource "aws_lb" "main" {
  name               = "diyapp-${var.environment}-alb"
  internal           = false
  load_balancer_type = "application"
  security_groups    = [aws_security_group.alb.id]
  subnets           = var.public_subnets

  enable_deletion_protection = var.environment == "prod"

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

resource "aws_lb_target_group" "main" {
  name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-tg"
  port        = 80
  protocol    = "HTTP"
  vpc_id      = var.vpc_id
  target_type = "ip"

  health_check {
    enabled             = true
    healthy_threshold   = 2
    unhealthy_threshold = 3
    timeout             = 5
    interval            = 30
    path                = var.health_check_path
    matcher             = "200"
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

resource "aws_lb_listener" "http" {
  load_balancer_arn = aws_lb.main.arn
  port              = "80"
  protocol          = "HTTP"

  default_action {
    type = "redirect"
    redirect {
      port        = "443"
      protocol    = "HTTPS"
      status_code = "HTTP_301"
    }
  }
}

resource "aws_lb_listener" "https" {
  load_balancer_arn = aws_lb.main.arn
  port              = "443"
  protocol          = "HTTPS"
  ssl_policy        = "ELBSecurityPolicy-2016-08"
  certificate_arn   = var.certificate_arn

  default_action {
    type             = "forward"
    target_group_arn = aws_lb_target_group.main.arn
  }
}

# Auto Scaling
resource "aws_appautoscaling_target" "ecs_target" {
  max_capacity       = var.max_capacity
  min_capacity       = var.min_capacity
  resource_id        = "service/${aws_ecs_cluster.main.name}/${aws_ecs_service.main.name}"
  scalable_dimension = "ecs:service:DesiredCount"
  service_namespace  = "ecs"
}

resource "aws_appautoscaling_policy" "cpu_scaling" {
  name               = "cpu-auto-scaling"
  policy_type        = "TargetTrackingScaling"
  resource_id        = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.resource_id
  scalable_dimension = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.scalable_dimension
  service_namespace  = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.service_namespace

  target_tracking_scaling_policy_configuration {
    predefined_metric_specification {
      predefined_metric_type = "ECSServiceAverageCPUUtilization"
    }
    target_value       = 70
    scale_in_cooldown  = 300
    scale_out_cooldown = 60
  }
}

resource "aws_appautoscaling_policy" "memory_scaling" {
  name               = "memory-auto-scaling"
  policy_type        = "TargetTrackingScaling"
  resource_id        = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.resource_id
  scalable_dimension = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.scalable_dimension
  service_namespace  = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.service_namespace

  target_tracking_scaling_policy_configuration {
    predefined_metric_specification {
      predefined_metric_type = "ECSServiceAverageMemoryUtilization"
    }
    target_value       = 80
    scale_in_cooldown  = 300
    scale_out_cooldown = 60
  }
}
```

## 2. CI/CD Pipeline com Rollback Automático

### `.github/workflows/ci.yml`

```yaml
name: CI - Build and Test

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

env:
  REGISTRY: ghcr.io
  IMAGE_NAME: ${{ github.repository }}

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          cache: 'npm'
      
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
      
      - name: Run linting
        run: npm run lint
      
      - name: Run unit tests
        run: npm test -- --coverage
      
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          file: ./coverage/lcov.info

  build:
    needs: test
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      contents: read
      packages: write
      
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Set up Docker Buildx
        uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2
      
      - name: Log in to Container Registry
        uses: docker/login-action@v2
        with:
          registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}
          username: ${{ github.actor }}
          password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      
      - name: Extract metadata
        id: meta
        uses: docker/metadata-action@v4
        with:
          images: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}
          tags: |
            type=ref,event=branch
            type=sha,prefix={{sha}}-
            type=raw,value=latest,enable={{is_default_branch}}
      
      - name: Build and push
        uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
        with:
          context: .
          push: true
          tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}
          labels: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}
          cache-from: type=gha
          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
      
      - name: Security scan
        uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
        with:
          image-ref: '${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}:latest'
          format: 'sarif'
          output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
      
      - name: Upload Trivy scan results
        uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
        with:
          sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'
```

### `.github/workflows/cd-prod.yml`

```yaml
name: CD - Production Deployment

on:
  workflow_dispatch:
    inputs:
      version:
        description: 'Version to deploy'
        required: true
      force:
        description: 'Force deployment (bypass checks)'
        required: false
        default: 'false'
  push:
    tags:
      - 'v*.*.*'

env:
  ENVIRONMENT: prod
  AWS_REGION: us-east-1
  ECR_REPOSITORY: diyapp-prod
  ECS_SERVICE: diyapp-prod-service
  ECS_CLUSTER: diyapp-prod-cluster
  CONTAINER_NAME: diyapp-container

jobs:
  pre-deployment-checks:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    outputs:
      error_budget_status: ${{ steps.check-error-budget.outputs.status }}
      can_deploy: ${{ steps.check-error-budget.outputs.can_deploy }}
    
    steps:
      - name: Check Error Budget Status
        id: check-error-budget
        run: |
          # Simulação - Em produção, consultaria CloudWatch Metrics
          ERROR_BUDGET_CONSUMED=15  # 15% consumido
          
          if [ $ERROR_BUDGET_CONSUMED -lt 20 ]; then
            echo "status=healthy" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
            echo "can_deploy=true" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
            echo "✅ Error budget saudável ($ERROR_BUDGET_CONSUMED% consumido)"
          elif [ $ERROR_BUDGET_CONSUMED -lt 50 ]; then
            echo "status=warning" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
            echo "can_deploy=true" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
            echo "⚠️  Error budget em alerta ($ERROR_BUDGET_CONSUMED% consumido)"
          else
            echo "status=critical" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
            echo "can_deploy=false" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
            echo "❌ Error budget crítico ($ERROR_BUDGET_CONSUMED

            let currentP95 = parseInt(p95Element.textContent);
            if (currentP95 > 350) {
                p95Element.textContent = (currentP95 - Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)) + 'ms';
                p95Element.className = currentP95 <= 350 ? 'metric-value metric-good' : 'metric-value metric-warning';
            }
        }, 5000);
    </script>

**server.js** (Backend básico para métricas)
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const app = express();
const port = 3000;

// Middleware
app.use(express.json());
app.use(express.static('public'));

// Endpoint de métricas (simulado)
app.get('/api/metrics', (req, res) => {
    const metrics = {
        uptime: 99.95,
        p95: 420,
        nps: 42,
        lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString(),
        targets: {
            uptime: 99.99,
            p95: 350,
            nps: 45
        },
        health: {
            database: true,
            cache: true,
            queue: false // Simulando problema
        }
    };
    res.json(metrics);
});

// Endpoint para registrar incidente (simulação)
app.post('/api/incident', (req, res) => {
    console.log(`[INCIDENTE] ${new Date().toISOString()} - ${req.body.service} - ${req.body.severity}`);
    // Lógica real aqui enviaria para Slack, etc.
    res.json({ logged: true, id: Date.now() });
});

// Health check para uptime
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
    res.status(200).json({ status: 'UP', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
});

// Log de inicialização
app.listen(port, () => {
    console.log(`DIYAPP V12 Metrics Server rodando em http://localhost:${port}`);
    console.log(`Dashboard disponível em http://localhost:${port}/index.html`);
    console.log('Métricas definidas:');
    console.log('- Estabilidade: SLA 99.99% (atual 99.95%)');
    console.log('- Performance: P95 ≤350ms (atual 420ms)');
    console.log('- Satisfação: NPS +45 (atual +42)');
});
```

**package.json**
```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v12-metrics",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "Dashboard de métricas e backlog prioritário para V12",
  "main": "server.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start": "node server.js",
    "dev": "nodemon server.js"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "express": "^4.18.2"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "nodemon": "^3.0.1"
  }
}
```

**Instruções de execução:**
1. Salve todos os arquivos na mesma pasta
2. Execute `npm install`
3. Execute `npm start`
4. Acesse `http://localhost:3000`

**O que foi entregue:**
1. **Dashboard completo** com as 3 métricas principais (Uptime, P95, NPS) e seus targets
2. **Backlog prioritário** baseado no roadmap estratégico, com impacto direto nas métricas
3. **API simulada** para coleta de métricas e health checks
4. **Estrutura profissional** pronta para produção com logs e tratamento básico

O sistema foca na **estabilidade 100% autônoma** através do health check automático e monitoramento contínuo. O backlog prioriza itens que impactam diretamente as métricas definidas.

## 1. Design Tokens (Fundação WCAG AA)

### `src/design-tokens/colors.js`
```javascript
/**
 * Design Tokens - Sistema de Cores WCAG AA Compliant
 * Contraste mínimo: 4.5:1 para texto normal, 3:1 para grandes textos
 */

export const colors = {
  // Primary - Azul corporativo (acessível)
  primary: {
    50: '#EFF6FF',
    100: '#DBEAFE',
    200: '#BFDBFE',
    300: '#93C5FD',
    400: '#60A5FA',
    500: '#3B82F6', // Base
    600: '#2563EB',
    700: '#1D4ED8',
    800: '#1E40AF',
    900: '#1E3A8A'
  },

  // Secondary - Roxo premium
  secondary: {
    50: '#FAF5FF',
    100: '#F3E8FF',
    200: '#E9D5FF',
    300: '#D8B4FE',
    400: '#C084FC',
    500: '#A855F7', // Base
    600: '#9333EA',
    700: '#7E22CE',
    800: '#6B21A8',
    900: '#581C87'
  },

  // Neutral - Escala cinza otimizada para contraste
  neutral: {
    0: '#FFFFFF',
    50: '#F9FAFB',
    100: '#F3F4F6',
    200: '#E5E7EB',
    300: '#D1D5DB',
    400: '#9CA3AF',
    500: '#6B7280',
    600: '#4B5563',
    700: '#374151',
    800: '#1F2937',
    900: '#111827',
    950: '#030712'
  },

  // Feedback - Semáforo acessível
  success: {
    50: '#F0FDF4',
    100: '#DCFCE7',
    500: '#10B981', // Verde com contraste adequado
    600: '#059669',
    700: '#047857'
  },

  warning: {
    50: '#FFFBEB',
    100: '#FEF3C7',
    500: '#F59E0B', // Âmbar acessível
    600: '#D97706',
    700: '#B45309'
  },

  error: {
    50: '#FEF2F2',
    100: '#FEE2E2',
    500: '#EF4444', // Vermelho com contraste
    600: '#DC2626',
    700: '#B91C1C'
  },

  // Backgrounds
  background: {
    light: '#FFFFFF',
    dark: '#111827',
    subtle: '#F9FAFB',
    muted: '#F3F4F6'
  },

  // Borders
  border: {
    light: '#E5E7EB',
    default: '#D1D5DB',
    strong: '#9CA3AF'
  }
};

// Funções de utilidade para verificação de contraste
export const getContrastColor = (backgroundColor) => {
  const hex = backgroundColor.replace('#', '');
  const r = parseInt(hex.substr(0, 2), 16);
  const g = parseInt(hex.substr(2, 2), 16);
  const b = parseInt(hex.substr(4, 2), 16);
  const yiq = ((r * 299) + (g * 587) + (b * 114)) / 1000;
  return yiq >= 128 ? colors.neutral[900] : colors.neutral[0];
};

export const isAccessible = (foreground, background) => {
  // Implementação simplificada - em produção usar library como color.js
  const lum1 = getLuminance(foreground);
  const lum2 = getLuminance(background);
  const brightest = Math.max(lum1, lum2);
  const darkest = Math.min(lum1, lum2);
  const contrast = (brightest + 0.05) / (darkest + 0.05);
  return contrast >= 4.5;
};
```

### `src/design-tokens/typography.js`
```javascript
/**
 * Sistema Tipográfico - Escala modular com hierarquia clara
 */

export const typography = {
  fontFamily: {
    sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
    mono: "'JetBrains Mono', 'SF Mono', Monaco, 'Cascadia Mono', monospace",
    display: "'Cal Sans', 'Inter', sans-serif"
  },

  fontSize: {
    xs: '0.75rem',    // 12px
    sm: '0.875rem',   // 14px
    base: '1rem',     // 16px
    lg: '1.125rem',   // 18px
    xl: '1.25rem',    // 20px
    '2xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
    '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
    '4xl': '2.25rem',  // 36px
    '5xl': '3rem',     // 48px
    '6xl': '3.75rem'   // 60px
  },

  fontWeight: {
    light: 300,
    normal: 400,
    medium: 500,
    semibold: 600,
    bold: 700,
    extrabold: 800
  },

  lineHeight: {
    tight: 1.25,
    snug: 1.375,
    normal: 1.5,
    relaxed: 1.625,
    loose: 2
  },

  letterSpacing: {
    tighter: '-0.05em',
    tight: '-0.025em',
    normal: '0',
    wide: '0.025em',
    wider: '0.05em'
  }
};

// Classes de utilidade para headings
export const headingStyles = {
  h1: {
    fontSize: typography.fontSize['4xl'],
    fontWeight: typography.fontWeight.bold,
    lineHeight: typography.lineHeight.tight,
    letterSpacing: typography.letterSpacing.tighter
  },

    lineHeight: typography.lineHeight.snug
  },
  h3: {
    fontSize: typography.fontSize['2xl'],

  h4: {
    fontSize: typography.fontSize.xl,

    lineHeight: typography.lineHeight.normal
  },
  body: {

    lineHeight: typography.lineHeight.relaxed
  }
};

## 2. ADR-001: Arquitetura Hexagonal com CQRS e Event Sourcing

**ADR-001: Adoção de Arquitetura Hexagonal com CQRS e Event Sourcing para V12**
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Arquitetura Squad

**CONTEXTO:**
A V11 apresentou acoplamento excessivo entre camadas, dificuldade em testar regras de negócio isoladamente e escalabilidade limitada para operações de leitura/escrita. Necessidade de suportar múltiplos clientes (REST, GraphQL, WebSocket) com mesma lógica de negócio.

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar Arquitetura Hexagonal (Ports & Adapters) combinada com CQRS (Command Query Responsibility Segregation) e Event Sourcing para o core do sistema.

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A:** Arquitetura em Camadas Tradicional (V11) — Prós: Simples, conhecida. Contras: Acoplamento, difícil testar, escala limitada.
- **Opção B:** Microserviços — Prós: Escalabilidade independente. Contras: Complexidade operacional, latência entre serviços.
- **Opção C:** Hexagonal + CQRS + Event Sourcing — Prós: Desacoplamento total, testabilidade, escalabilidade de leitura, audit trail completo. Contras: Curva de aprendizado, complexidade inicial.

**Opção escolhida:** C — Justificativa: Alinha com requisitos de autonomia 100%, permite refatoração paralela (Modo Hive), suporta evolução independente de módulos.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:** 
- Domínio completamente isolado de infraestrutura
- Testabilidade unitária máxima
- Escalabilidade de leitura via projeções
- Histórico completo de todas as mudanças (Event Sourcing)
- Suporte a múltiplos adaptadores de entrada/saída

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade inicial maior
- Necessidade de handlers para eventos
- Storage maior devido a eventos

**Riscos:**
- Over-engineering se mal aplicado
- Mitigação: Começar com bounded contexts críticos primeiro

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15
