## 4. Estratégia de Cache Multi-layer

```typescript
// src/core/infrastructure/cache/multi-layer-cache.ts
import Redis from 'ioredis';
import NodeCache from 'node-cache';

export interface CacheLayer {
  get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null>;
  set<T>(key: string, value: T, ttl?: number): Promise<void>;
  delete(key: string): Promise<void>;
  clear(): Promise<void>;
}

export class MultiLayerCache implements CacheLayer {
  private localCache: NodeCache;
  private redisClient: Redis;
  private readonly defaultTTL = 300; // 5 minutos

  constructor(redisConfig?: Redis.RedisOptions) {
    this.localCache = new NodeCache({
      stdTTL: 60,
      checkperiod: 120,
      useClones: false
    });
    
    this.redisClient = new Redis({
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT || '6379'),
      ...redisConfig
    });
  }

  async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    // 1. Tentar local cache (L1)
    const localValue = this.localCache.get<T>(key);
    if (localValue !== undefined) {
      return localValue;
    }

    // 2. Tentar Redis (L2)
    try {
      const redisValue = await this.redisClient.get(key);
      if (redisValue) {
        const parsedValue = JSON.parse(redisValue) as T;
        
        // Popular local cache
        this.localCache.set(key, parsedValue);
        
        return parsedValue;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn(`Redis cache miss for key ${key}:`, error);
    }

    return null;
  }

  async set<T>(key: string, value: T, ttl?: number): Promise<void> {
    const cacheTTL = ttl || this.defaultTTL;
    
    // 1. Setar local cache
    this.localCache.set(key, value, cacheTTL);
    
    // 2. Setar Redis async (fire and forget)
    this.redisClient
      .setex(key, cacheTTL, JSON.stringify(value))
      .catch(err => console.error(`Redis set error for key ${key}:`, err));
  }

  async delete(key: string): Promise<void> {
    this.localCache.del(key);
    await this.redisClient.del(key);
  }

  async clear(): Promise<void> {
    this.localCache.flushAll();
    await this.redisClient.flushall();
  }

  // Pattern-based invalidation para CQRS
  async invalidatePattern(pattern: string): Promise<void> {
    const keys = await this.redisClient.keys(pattern);
    if (keys.length > 0) {
      await this.redisClient.del(...keys);
    }
    
    // Invalidação local por pattern
    const localKeys = this.localCache.keys();
    const matchingKeys = localKeys.filter(key => key.includes(pattern));
    matchingKeys.forEach(key => this.localCache.del(key));
  }
}

// Estratégias de cache específicas
export class CacheStrategies {
  static readonly USER_SESSION = {
    ttl: 3600, // 1 hora
    pattern: 'user:session:*'
  };

  static readonly LLM_RESPONSE = {
    ttl: 300, // 5 minutos
    pattern: 'llm:response:*'
  };

  static readonly WORKFLOW_STATE = {
    ttl: 1800, // 30 minutos
    pattern: 'workflow:state:*'
  };
}
```

## 5. Stack de Monitoramento (APM)

```typescript
// src/core/infrastructure/monitoring/apm-setup.ts
import * as Sentry from '@sentry/node';
import * as Tracing from '@sentry/tracing';
import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-grpc';
import { Resource } from '@opentelemetry/resources';
import { SemanticResourceAttributes } from '@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions';
import Prometheus from 'prom-client';
import express from 'express';

export class APMManager {
  private static instance: APMManager;
  private metricsApp: express.Application;
  private prometheusRegistry: Prometheus.Registry;

  private constructor() {
    this.prometheusRegistry = new Prometheus.Registry();
    this.prometheusRegistry.setDefaultLabels({
      app: 'diyapp-v12',
      version: process.env.npm_package_version || '1.0.0'
    });

    this.metricsApp = express();
    this.setupMetricsEndpoint();
  }

  static getInstance(): APMManager {
    if (!APMManager.instance) {
      APMManager.instance = new APMManager();
    }
    return APMManager.instance;
  }

  async initialize(): Promise<void> {
    // 1. Sentry para error tracking
    if (process.env.SENTRY_DSN) {
      Sentry.init({
        dsn: process.env.SENTRY_DSN,
        environment: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
        tracesSampleRate: parseFloat(process.env.SENTRY_TRACES_SAMPLE_RATE || '0.1'),
        integrations: [
          new Sentry.Integrations.Http({ tracing: true }),
          new Tracing.Integrations.Express({ app: this.metricsApp }),
        ],
      });
    }

    // 2. OpenTelemetry para distributed tracing
    if (process.env.OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT) {
      const sdk = new NodeSDK({
        resource: new Resource({
          [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: 'diyapp-v12',
          [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_VERSION]: process.env.npm_package_version || '1.0.0',
        }),
        traceExporter: new OTLPTraceExporter(),
        instrumentations: [getNodeAutoInstrumentations()],
      });

      sdk.start();
    }

    // 3. Métricas customizadas
    this.registerDefaultMetrics();
  }

  private setupMetricsEndpoint(): void {
    this.metricsApp.get('/metrics', async (req, res) => {
      res.set('Content-Type', this.prometheusRegistry.contentType);
      res.end(await this.prometheusRegistry.metrics());
    });

    this.metricsApp.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      res.json({
        status: 'healthy',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        uptime: process.uptime(),
        memory: process.memoryUsage(),
      });
    });
  }

  private registerDefaultMetrics(): void {
    // Coletor de métricas padrão do Node.js
    Prometheus.collectDefaultMetrics({ register: this.prometheusRegistry });

    // Métricas customizadas
    const httpRequestDuration = new Prometheus.Histogram({
      name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
      help: 'Duration of HTTP requests in seconds',
      labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code'],
      buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
    });

    const llmRequestsCounter = new Prometheus.Counter({
      name: 'llm_requests_total',
      help: 'Total number of LLM requests',
      labelNames: ['model', 'status']
    });

    const workflowExecutionTime = new Prometheus.Histogram({
      name: 'workflow_execution_time_seconds',
      help: 'Workflow execution time in seconds',
      labelNames: ['workflow_type', 'status'],
      buckets: [1, 5, 10, 30, 60]
    });

    this.prometheusRegistry.registerMetric(httpRequestDuration);
    this.prometheusRegistry.registerMetric(llmRequestsCounter);
    this.prometheusRegistry.registerMetric(workflowExecutionTime);
  }

  getMetricsApp(): express.Application {
    return this.metricsApp;
  }

  // Decorator para monitorar métodos
  static monitor(metricName: string, labels?: Record<string, string>) {
    return function (
      target: any,
      propertyKey: string,
      descriptor: PropertyDescriptor
    ) {
      const originalMethod = descriptor.value;
      
      descriptor.value = async function (...args: any[]) {
        const start = Date.now();
        try {
          const result = await originalMethod.apply(this, args);
          const duration = Date.now() - start;
          
          // Registrar métrica
          const histogram = APMManager.getInstance().prometheusRegistry.getSingleMetric(
            `${metricName}_duration_seconds`
          ) as Prometheus.Histogram;
          
          if (histogram) {
            histogram.observe(labels || {}, duration / 1000);
          }
          
          return result;
        } catch (error) {
          const duration = Date.now() - start;
          
          // Registrar erro
          const counter = APMManager.getInstance().prometheusRegistry.getSingleMetric(
            `${metricName}_errors_total`
          ) as Prometheus.Counter;
          
          if (counter) {
            counter.inc(labels || {}, 1);
          }
          
          throw error;
        }
      };
      
      return descriptor;
    };
  }
}
```

```python

# src/core/config.py
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings
from typing import Optional
import os

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # API
    API_V1_STR: str = "/api/v1"
    API_V2_STR: str = "/api/v2"
    PROJECT_NAME: str = "DIYAPP Evolution V12"
    
    # Database
    POSTGRES_SERVER: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_SERVER", "localhost")
    POSTGRES_USER: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_USER", "postgres")
    POSTGRES_PASSWORD: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_PASSWORD", "")
    POSTGRES_DB: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_DB", "diyapp")
    DATABASE_URL: Optional[str] = None
    
    # Redis for Celery and caching
    REDIS_URL: str = os.getenv("REDIS_URL", "redis://localhost:6379/0")
    
    # External Services with timeouts
    PAYMENT_SERVICE_URL: str = os.getenv("PAYMENT_SERVICE_URL", "https://api.payment.com")
    PAYMENT_SERVICE_TIMEOUT: int = 10  # seconds
    EMAIL_SERVICE_URL: str = os.getenv("EMAIL_SERVICE_URL", "https://api.email.com")
    EMAIL_SERVICE_TIMEOUT: int = 5
    
    # Circuit Breaker settings
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD: int = 5
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT: int = 60
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_EXPECTED_EXCEPTION: tuple = (Exception,)
    
    # Retry Policy
    MAX_RETRIES: int = 3
    RETRY_BACKOFF_MULTIPLIER: float = 2.0
    RETRY_BACKOFF_MAX: int = 60
    
    # Security
    SECRET_KEY: str = os.getenv("SECRET_KEY", "your-secret-key-change-in-production")
    ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30
    
    # Logging
    LOG_LEVEL: str = "INFO"
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
    
    def __post_init__(self):
        if not self.DATABASE_URL:
            self.DATABASE_URL = f"postgresql://{self.POSTGRES_USER}:{self.POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@{self.POSTGRES_SERVER}/{self.POSTGRES_DB}"

settings = Settings()

# src/core/database.py
from sqlalchemy import create_engine, text
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker, Session
from sqlalchemy.pool import QueuePool
from contextlib import contextmanager
from typing import Generator
import structlog
from .config import settings

logger = structlog.get_logger()

# Connection pool configuration
engine = create_engine(
    settings.DATABASE_URL,
    poolclass=QueuePool,
    pool_size=20,  # Maximum number of connections
    max_overflow=10,  # Additional connections beyond pool_size
    pool_timeout=30,  # Seconds to wait for a connection
    pool_recycle=1800,  # Recycle connections after 30 minutes
    pool_pre_ping=True,  # Verify connection before using
    echo=False,  # Set to True for SQL logging in development
)

SessionLocal = sessionmaker(autocommit=False, autoflush=False, bind=engine)
Base = declarative_base()

@contextmanager
def get_db() -> Generator[Session, None, None]:
    """Database session context manager with proper error handling"""
    db = SessionLocal()
    try:
        yield db
        db.commit()
    except Exception as e:
        db.rollback()
        logger.error("database_transaction_failed", error=str(e), error_type=type(e).__name__)
        raise
    finally:
        db.close()

def init_db():
    """Initialize database and create tables"""
    Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)
    
    # Test connection with timeout
    try:
        with engine.connect() as conn:
            conn.execute(text("SELECT 1"))
        logger.info("database_connection_successful")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("database_connection_failed", error=str(e))
        raise

# src/utils/retry_policy.py
from tenacity import (
    retry,
    stop_after_attempt,
    wait_exponential,
    retry_if_exception_type,
    before_sleep_log,
    after_log
)
import structlog
from typing import Type, Tuple, Any
import httpx

logger = structlog.get_logger()

def create_retry_policy(
    max_retries: int = 3,
    wait_multiplier: float = 2.0,
    wait_max: int = 60,
    retry_on_exceptions: Tuple[Type[Exception], ...] = (Exception,)
):
    """Create a retry policy with exponential backoff"""
    
    @retry(
        stop=stop_after_attempt(max_retries),
        wait=wait_exponential(multiplier=wait_multiplier, max=wait_max),
        retry=retry_if_exception_type(retry_on_exceptions),
        before_sleep=before_sleep_log(logger, "WARNING"),
        after=after_log(logger, "INFO"),
        reraise=True
    )
    def retry_decorator(func):
        async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            return await func(*args, **kwargs)
        return wrapper
    
    return retry_decorator

# Common retry policies
retry_external_service = create_retry_policy(
    max_retries=3,
    wait_multiplier=2.0,
    wait_max=60,
    retry_on_exceptions=(httpx.TimeoutException, httpx.NetworkError)
)

retry_database = create_retry_policy(
    max_retries=2,
    wait_multiplier=1.5,
    wait_max=30,
    retry_on_exceptions=(Exception,)  # Database exceptions
)

# src/services/circuit_breaker.py
from circuitbreaker import circuit
import structlog
from typing import Callable, Any
import time
from functools import wraps
from ..core.config import settings

logger = structlog.get_logger()

class CircuitBreaker:
    """Enhanced circuit breaker with monitoring"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        failure_threshold: int = 5,
        recovery_timeout: int = 60,
        expected_exception: tuple = (Exception,),
        name: str = "default"
    ):
        self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold
        self.recovery_timeout = recovery_timeout
        self.expected_exception = expected_exception
        self.name = name
        self.state = "CLOSED"
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.last_failure_time = None
        
    def __call__(self, func: Callable) -> Callable:
        @wraps(func)
        async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            if self.state == "OPEN":
                if time.time() - self.last_failure_time > self.recovery_timeout:
                    self.state = "HALF_OPEN"
                    logger.warning("circuit_half_open", breaker=self.name)
                else:
                    logger.warning("circuit_open", breaker=self.name)
                    raise CircuitOpenException(f"Circuit breaker {self.name} is OPEN")
            
            try:
                result = await func(*args, **kwargs)
                if self.state == "HALF_OPEN":
                    self.state = "CLOSED"
                    self.failure_count = 0
                    logger.info("circuit_closed", breaker=self.name)
                return result
            except self.expected_exception as e:
                self.failure_count += 1
                self.last_failure_time = time.time()
                
                if self.failure_count >= self.failure_threshold:
                    self.state = "OPEN"
                    logger.error("circuit_opened", 
                                breaker=self.name, 
                                error=str(e),
                                failure_count=self.failure_count)
                
                logger.warning("circuit_failure", 
                              breaker=self.name, 
                              failure_count=self.failure_count,
                              error=str(e))
                raise
        
        return wrapper

class CircuitOpenException(Exception):
    """Exception raised when circuit breaker is open"""
    pass

# Circuit breaker instances for different services
payment_circuit_breaker = CircuitBreaker(
    failure_threshold=settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD,
    recovery_timeout=settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT,
    name="payment_service"
)

email_circuit_breaker = CircuitBreaker(
    failure_threshold=settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD,
    recovery_timeout=settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT,
    name="email_service"
)

# src/services/background.py
from celery import Celery
from celery.schedules import crontab
import structlog
from typing import Dict, Any
from ..core.config import settings

logger = structlog.get_logger()

# Initialize Celery
celery_app = Celery(
    "diyapp_background",
    broker=settings.REDIS_URL,
    backend=settings.REDIS_URL,
    include=["src.services.background_tasks"]
)

# Celery configuration
celery_app.conf.update(
    task_serializer="json",
    accept_content=["json"],
    result_serializer="json",
    timezone="UTC",
    enable_utc=True,
    task_track_started=True,
    task_time_limit=30 * 60,  # 30 minutes
    task_soft_time_limit=25 * 60,  # 25 minutes
    worker_max_tasks_per_child=1000,  # Prevent memory leaks
    worker_prefetch_multiplier=1,  # Fair task distribution
)

# Periodic tasks schedule
celery_app.conf.beat_schedule = {
    "cleanup-expired-sessions": {
        "task": "src.services.background_tasks.cleanup_expired_sessions",
        "schedule": crontab(hour=2, minute=0),  # Daily at 2 AM
    },
    "send-daily-reports": {
        "task": "src.services.background_tasks.send_daily_reports",
        "schedule": crontab(hour=9, minute=0),  # Daily at 9 AM
    },
    "process-pending-payments": {
        "task": "src.services.background_tasks.process_pending_payments",
        "schedule": 300.0,  # Every 5 minutes
    },
    "backup-database": {
        "task": "src.services.background_tasks.backup_database",
        "schedule": crontab(hour=0, minute=0),  # Daily at midnight
    },
}

# src/services/background_tasks.py
from .background import celery_app
from ..core.database import get_db
from ..services.email_service import EmailService
from ..services.payment_service import PaymentService
import structlog
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from sqlalchemy import text

logger = structlog.get_logger()

@celery_app.task(bind=True, max_retries=3)
def cleanup_expired_sessions(self):
    """Clean up expired user sessions"""
    try:
        with get_db() as db:
            # Delete sessions older than 30 days
            result = db.execute(
                text("""
                    DELETE FROM user_sessions 
                    WHERE last_activity < NOW() - INTERVAL '30 days'
                """)
            )
            db.commit()
            logger.info("expired_sessions_cleaned", count=result.rowcount)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("session_cleanup_failed", error=str(e))
        raise self.retry(exc=e, countdown=60)

@celery_app.task(bind=True, max_retries=3)
def send_daily_reports(self):
    """Send daily activity reports to admin"""
    try:
        email_service = EmailService()
        
        with get_db() as db:
            # Get daily statistics
            stats = db.execute(
                text("""
                    SELECT 
                        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as active_users,
                        COUNT(*) as total_actions,
                        COUNT(DISTINCT DATE(created_at)) as active_days
                    FROM user_activities 
                    WHERE created_at >= NOW() - INTERVAL '1 day'
                """)
            ).fetchone()
        
        report = f"""
        Daily Report - {datetime.now().date()}
        
        Active Users: {stats.active_users or 0}
        Total Actions: {stats.total_actions or 0}
        Active Days: {stats.active_days or 0}
        """
        
        email_service.send_email(
            to="admin@diyapp.com",
            subject=f"DIYAPP Daily Report - {datetime.now().date()}",
            body=report
        )
        
        logger.info("daily_report_sent")
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("daily_report_failed", error=str(e))
        raise self.retry(exc=e, countdown=300)

@celery_app.task(bind=True, max_retries=5, time_limit=300)
def process_pending_payments(self):
    """Process pending payments with retry logic"""
    try:
        payment_service = PaymentService()
        
        with get_db() as db:
            # Get pending payments
            pending_payments = db.execute(
                text("""
                    SELECT id, user_id, amount, payment_data
                    FROM payments 
                    WHERE status = 'pending'
                    AND created_at >= NOW() - INTERVAL '7 days'
                    LIMIT 100
                """)
            ).fetchall()
        
        for payment in pending_payments:
            try:
                result = payment_service.process_payment(
                    user_id=payment.user_id,
                    amount=payment.amount,
                    payment_data=payment.payment_data
                )
                
                # Update payment status
                db.execute(
                    text("""
                        UPDATE payments 
                        SET status = :status, 
                            processed_at = NOW(),
                            transaction_id = :transaction_id
                        WHERE id = :id
                    """),
                    {
                        "status": "completed",
                        "transaction_id": result.transaction_id,
                        "id": payment.id
                    }
                )
                db.commit()
                
                logger.info("payment_processed", 
                           payment_id=payment.id,
                           transaction_id=result.transaction_id)
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error("payment_processing_failed",
                            payment_id=payment.id,
                            error=str(e))
                # Mark as failed after 3 attempts
                db.execute(
                    text("""
                        UPDATE payments 
                        SET status = 'failed',
                            error_message = :error
                        WHERE id = :id
                        AND attempts >= 3
                    """),
                    {"error": str(e), "id": payment.id}
                )
                db.commit()
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("batch_payment_processing_failed", error=str(e))
        raise self.retry(exc=e, countdown=600)

@celery_app.task(bind=True, max_retries=2, time_limit=3600)
def backup_database(self):
    """Create database backup"""
    try:
        import subprocess
        import os
        from datetime import datetime
        
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
        backup_file = f"/backups/diyapp_backup_{timestamp}.sql"
        
        # Create backup using pg_dump
        subprocess.run([
            "pg_dump",
            f"--dbname={settings.DATABASE_URL}",
            f"--file={backup_file}",
            "--format=custom",
            "--verbose"
        ], check=True)
        
        # Compress backup
        subprocess.run(["gzip", backup_file], check=True)
        
        # Keep only last 7 days of backups
        subprocess.run([
            "find", "/backups",
            "-name", "*.sql.gz",

```typescript
// src/components/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { Spinner } from '../Spinner/Spinner';
import { useButtonStyles } from './useButtonStyles';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  loading?: boolean;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      loading = false,
      fullWidth = false,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      children,
      disabled,
      className,
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const { buttonClasses, spinnerColor } = useButtonStyles({
      variant,
      size,
      loading,
      fullWidth,
      disabled,
      className,
    });

    return (
      <button
        ref={ref}
        className={buttonClasses}
        disabled={disabled || loading}
        aria-busy={loading}
        {...props}
      >
        {loading && (
          <span className="mr-2" aria-hidden="true">
            <Spinner size={size === 'sm' ? 'xs' : 'sm'} color={spinnerColor} />
          </span>
        )}
        {!loading && leftIcon && (
          <span className="mr-2" aria-hidden="true">
            {leftIcon}
          </span>
        )}
        <span className="flex items-center justify-center">{children}</span>
        {!loading && rightIcon && (
          <span className="ml-2" aria-hidden="true">
            {rightIcon}
          </span>
        )}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';
```

```typescript
// src/components/Button/useButtonStyles.ts
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { ButtonVariant, ButtonSize } from './Button';

interface UseButtonStylesProps {
  variant: ButtonVariant;
  size: ButtonSize;
  loading: boolean;
  fullWidth: boolean;
  disabled?: boolean;
  className?: string;
}

export const useButtonStyles = ({
  variant,
  size,
  loading,
  fullWidth,
  disabled,
  className = '',
}: UseButtonStylesProps) => {
  const baseClasses = [
    'inline-flex items-center justify-center',
    'font-medium',
    'rounded-md',
    'transition-all duration-200',
    'focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2',
    'disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed',
    fullWidth ? 'w-full' : '',
  ];

  const variantClasses = {
    primary: [
      'bg-primary-600 text-white',
      'hover:bg-primary-700',
      'active:bg-primary-800',
      'focus:ring-primary-500',
      disabled ? '' : 'shadow-sm',
    ],
    secondary: [
      'bg-neutral-100 text-neutral-900',
      'hover:bg-neutral-200',
      'active:bg-neutral-300',
      'focus:ring-neutral-500',
      disabled ? '' : 'shadow-sm',
    ],
    outline: [
      'border border-neutral-300 text-neutral-700',
      'hover:bg-neutral-50',
      'active:bg-neutral-100',
      'focus:ring-primary-500',
      'bg-transparent',
    ],
    ghost: [
      'text-neutral-700',
      'hover:bg-neutral-100',
      'active:bg-neutral-200',
      'focus:ring-primary-500',
      'bg-transparent',
    ],
  };

  const sizeClasses = {
    sm: ['text-sm', 'py-1.5', 'px-3', 'gap-1'],
    md: ['text-base', 'py-2', 'px-4', 'gap-2'],
    lg: ['text-lg', 'py-3', 'px-6', 'gap-3'],
  };

  const buttonClasses = [
    ...baseClasses,
    ...variantClasses[variant],
    ...sizeClasses[size],
    className,
  ]
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join(' ');

  const spinnerColor = variant === 'primary' || variant === 'secondary' 
    ? 'currentColor' 
    : tokens.colors.neutral[500];

  return { buttonClasses, spinnerColor };
};
```

```typescript
// src/components/Button/Button.test.tsx
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import { Button } from './Button';

describe('Button', () => {
  it('renders with default props', () => {
    render(<Button>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(button).toHaveClass('bg-primary-600');
  });

  it('renders with secondary variant', () => {
    render(<Button variant="secondary">Secondary</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toHaveClass('bg-neutral-100');
  });

  it('shows loading state', () => {
    render(<Button loading>Loading</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
    expect(screen.getByRole('status')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn();
    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click</Button>);
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button'));
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  it('renders with left and right icons', () => {
    render(
      <Button
        leftIcon={<span data-testid="left-icon">←</span>}
        rightIcon={<span data-testid="right-icon">→</span>}
      >
        Icons
      </Button>
    );
    expect(screen.getByTestId('left-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByTestId('right-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('has proper accessibility attributes when disabled', () => {
    render(<Button disabled>Disabled</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
    expect(button).toHaveClass('disabled:opacity-50');
  });
});
```

```typescript
// src/components/Card/Card.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, HTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export interface CardProps extends HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  variant?: 'elevated' | 'outline' | 'filled';
  padding?: 'none' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export const Card = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, CardProps>(
  ({ variant = 'elevated', padding = 'md', children, className = '', ...props }, ref) => {
    const baseClasses = [
      'rounded-lg',
      'transition-all duration-200',
    ];

    const variantClasses = {
      elevated: ['bg-white', 'shadow-md', 'border border-neutral-100'],
      outline: ['bg-transparent', 'border border-neutral-200'],
      filled: ['bg-neutral-50', 'border border-neutral-100'],
    };

    const paddingClasses = {
      none: 'p-0',
      sm: 'p-4',
      md: 'p-6',
      lg: 'p-8',
    };

    const cardClasses = [
      ...baseClasses,
      ...variantClasses[variant],
      paddingClasses[padding],
      className,
    ].join(' ');

    return (
      <div ref={ref} className={cardClasses} {...props}>
        {children}
      </div>
    );
  }
);

Card.displayName = 'Card';
```

```typescript
// src/components/Spinner/Spinner.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export type SpinnerSize = 'xs' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
export type SpinnerColor = 'primary' | 'neutral' | 'white' | 'currentColor';

interface SpinnerProps {
  size?: SpinnerSize;
  color?: SpinnerColor;
  className?: string;
}

export const Spinner: React.FC<SpinnerProps> = ({
  size = 'md',
  color = 'primary',
  className = '',
}) => {
  const sizeClasses = {
    xs: 'w-4 h-4',
    sm: 'w-5 h-5',
    md: 'w-6 h-6',
    lg: 'w-8 h-8',
  };

  const colorClasses = {
    primary: 'text-primary-600',
    neutral: 'text-neutral-600',
    white: 'text-white',
    currentColor: 'text-current',
  };

  return (
    <div
      role="status"
      className={`inline-block animate-spin ${sizeClasses[size]} ${colorClasses[color]} ${className}`}
      aria-label="Loading"
    >
      <svg
        className="w-full h-full"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        fill="none"
        viewBox="0 0 24 24"
        aria-hidden="true"
      >
        <circle
          className="opacity-25"
          cx="12"
          cy="12"
          r="10"
          stroke="currentColor"
          strokeWidth="4"
        />
        <path
          className="opacity-75"
          fill="currentColor"
          d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
        />
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
};
```

```typescript
// src/components/DataTable/DataTable.tsx
import React, { useState, useMemo } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { Spinner } from '../Spinner/Spinner';
import { Button } from '../Button/Button';

export interface Column<T> {
  key: keyof T | string;
  header: string;
  width?: string;
  sortable?: boolean;
  render?: (value: any, row: T) => React.ReactNode;
}

export interface DataTableProps<T> {
  columns: Column<T>[];
  data: T[];
  loading?: boolean;
  error?: string | null;
  onRowClick?: (row: T) => void;
  onSort?: (key: keyof T, direction: 'asc' | 'desc') => void;
  emptyState?: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
}

export function DataTable<T extends Record<string, any>>({
  columns,
  data,
  loading = false,
  error = null,
  onRowClick,
  onSort,
  emptyState,
  className = '',
}: DataTableProps<T>) {
  const [sortConfig, setSortConfig] = useState<{
    key: keyof T | string;
    direction: 'asc' | 'desc';
  } | null>(null);

  const handleSort = (key: keyof T | string) => {
    if (!columns.find(col => col.key === key)?.sortable) return;

    let direction: 'asc' | 'desc' = 'asc';
    if (sortConfig && sortConfig.key === key && sortConfig.direction === 'asc') {
      direction = 'desc';
    }

    const newSortConfig = { key, direction };
    setSortConfig(newSortConfig);
    onSort?.(key as keyof T, direction);
  };

  const sortedData = useMemo(() => {
    if (!sortConfig || !sortConfig.key) return data;

    return [...data].sort((a, b) => {
      const aValue = a[sortConfig.key as keyof T];
      const bValue = b[sortConfig.key as keyof T];

      if (aValue < bValue) return sortConfig.direction === 'asc' ? -1 : 1;
      if (aValue > bValue) return sortConfig.direction === 'asc' ? 1 : -1;
      return 0;
    });
  }, [data, sortConfig]);

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center p-12">
        <Spinner size="lg" />
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (error) {
    return (
      <div className="text-center p-8">
        <div className="text-error-600 mb-2">Error loading data</div>
        <div className="text-neutral-600">{error}</div>
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          className="mt-4"
          onClick={() => window.location.reload()}
        >
          Retry
        </Button>
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (data.length === 0) {
    return (
      emptyState || (
        <div className="text-center p-12">
          <div className="text-neutral-500">No data available</div>
        </div>
      )
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className={`overflow-x-auto ${className}`}>
      <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-neutral-200">
        <thead className="bg-neutral-50">
          <tr>
            {columns.map((column) => (
              <th
                key={String(column.key)}
                scope="col"
                className={`px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-neutral-500 uppercase tracking-wider ${
                  column.sortable ? 'cursor-pointer hover:bg-neutral-100' : ''
                }`}
                style={{ width: column.width }}
                onClick={() => column.sortable && handleSort(column.key)}
              >
                <div className="flex items-center

### [Sessão Paralela: PM]

## 1. Design Tokens (design-tokens.js)

```javascript
// design-tokens.js
// Sistema de tokens de design baseado em evidências de usabilidade

class DesignTokens {
  constructor() {
    this.tokens = {
      // Cores baseadas em contraste WCAG AA
      colors: {
        primary: {
          50: '#f0f9ff',
          100: '#e0f2fe',
          200: '#bae6fd',
          300: '#7dd3fc',
          400: '#38bdf8',
          500: '#0ea5e9',
          600: '#0284c7',
          700: '#0369a1',
          800: '#075985',
          900: '#0c4a6e',
          950: '#082f49'
        },
        secondary: {
          50: '#fdf4ff',
          100: '#fae8ff',
          200: '#f5d0fe',
          300: '#f0abfc',
          400: '#e879f9',
          500: '#d946ef',
          600: '#c026d3',
          700: '#a21caf',
          800: '#86198f',
          900: '#701a75',
          950: '#4a044e'
        },
        neutral: {
          0: '#ffffff',
          50: '#f8fafc',
          100: '#f1f5f9',
          200: '#e2e8f0',
          300: '#cbd5e1',
          400: '#94a3b8',
          500: '#64748b',
          600: '#475569',
          700: '#334155',
          800: '#1e293b',
          900: '#0f172a',
          950: '#020617'
        },
        feedback: {
          success: {
            light: '#d1fae5',
            base: '#10b981',
            dark: '#047857'
          },
          warning: {
            light: '#fef3c7',
            base: '#f59e0b',
            dark: '#d97706'
          },
          error: {
            light: '#fee2e2',
            base: '#ef4444',
            dark: '#dc2626'
          },
          info: {
            light: '#dbeafe',
            base: '#3b82f6',
            dark: '#1d4ed8'
          }
        },
        // Cores para estados de IA
        ai: {
          processing: '#8b5cf6',
          streaming: '#06b6d4',
          confidence: {
            high: '#10b981',
            medium: '#f59e0b',
            low: '#ef4444'
          }
        }
      },
      
      // Tipografia com hierarquia de headings acessível
      typography: {
        fontFamily: {
          sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
          mono: "'JetBrains Mono', 'Courier New', monospace"
        },
        fontSize: {
          xs: '0.75rem',    // 12px
          sm: '0.875rem',   // 14px
          base: '1rem',     // 16px
          lg: '1.125rem',   // 18px
          xl: '1.25rem',    // 20px
          '2xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
          '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
          '4xl': '2.25rem',  // 36px
          '5xl': '3rem'      // 48px
        },
        fontWeight: {
          normal: '400',
          medium: '500',
          semibold: '600',
          bold: '700'
        },
        lineHeight: {
          tight: '1.25',
          snug: '1.375',
          normal: '1.5',
          relaxed: '1.625',
          loose: '2'
        }
      },
      
      // Espaçamento baseado em escala 8px
      spacing: {
        px: '1px',
        0: '0',
        0.5: '0.125rem',   // 2px
        1: '0.25rem',      // 4px
        1.5: '0.375rem',   // 6px
        2: '0.5rem',       // 8px
        2.5: '0.625rem',   // 10px
        3: '0.75rem',      // 12px
        3.5: '0.875rem',   // 14px
        4: '1rem',         // 16px
        5: '1.25rem',      // 20px
        6: '1.5rem',       // 24px
        7: '1.75rem',      // 28px
        8: '2rem',         // 32px
        9: '2.25rem',      // 36px
        10: '2.5rem',      // 40px
        12: '3rem',        // 48px
        14: '3.5rem',      // 56px
        16: '4rem',        // 64px
        20: '5rem',        // 80px
        24: '6rem',        // 96px
        28: '7rem',        // 112px
        32: '8rem'         // 128px
      },
      
      // Border radius consistente
      borderRadius: {
        none: '0',
        sm: '0.125rem',    // 2px
        base: '0.25rem',   // 4px
        md: '0.375rem',    // 6px
        lg: '0.5rem',      // 8px
        xl: '0.75rem',     // 12px
        '2xl': '1rem',     // 16px
        '3xl': '1.5rem',   // 24px
        full: '9999px'
      },
      
      // Elevação (box-shadow) para hierarquia visual
      elevation: {
        0: 'none',
        1: '0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
        2: '0 1px 3px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
        3: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
        4: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
        5: '0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04)'
      },
      
      // Animações e transições
      transitions: {
        duration: {
          fast: '150ms',
          normal: '300ms',
          slow: '500ms'
        },
        easing: {
          linear: 'linear',
          in: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)',
          out: 'cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)',
          inOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)'
        }
      },
      
      // Breakpoints responsivos
      breakpoints: {
        sm: '640px',
        md: '768px',
        lg: '1024px',
        xl: '1280px',
        '2xl': '1536px'
      }
    };
  }
  
  // Validação de contraste WCAG AA
  validateContrast(foreground, background) {
    // Implementação simplificada - em produção usar biblioteca como chroma.js
    const luminance = (color) => {
      const rgb = this.hexToRgb(color);
      const [r, g, b] = rgb.map(c => {
        c = c / 255;
        return c <= 0.03928 ? c / 12.92 : Math.pow((c + 0.055) / 1.055, 2.4);
      });
      return 0.2126 * r + 0.7152 * g + 0.0722 * b;
    };
    
    const l1 = luminance(foreground);
    const l2 = luminance(background);
    const contrast = (Math.max(l1, l2) + 0.05) / (Math.min(l1, l2) + 0.05);
    
    return {
      ratio: contrast.toFixed(2),
      aa: contrast >= 4.5,
      aaLarge: contrast >= 3,
      aaa: contrast >= 7
    };
  }
  
  hexToRgb(hex) {
    const result = /^#?([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})$/i.exec(hex);
    return result ? [
      parseInt(result[1], 16),
      parseInt(result[2], 16),
      parseInt(result[3], 16)
    ] : [0, 0, 0];
  }
  
  // Gera CSS custom properties
  generateCSS() {
    let css = ':root {\n';
    
    // Cores
    Object.entries(this.tokens.colors).forEach(([category, values]) => {
      Object.entries(values).forEach(([shade, color]) => {
        if (typeof color === 'object') {
          Object.entries(color).forEach(([subShade, subColor]) => {
            css += `  --color-${category}-${shade}-${subShade}: ${subColor};\n`;
          });
        } else {
          css += `  --color-${category}-${shade}: ${color};\n`;
        }
      });
    });
    
    // Tipografia
    Object.entries(this.tokens.typography.fontSize).forEach(([size, value]) => {
      css += `  --font-size-${size}: ${value};\n`;
    });
    
    // Espaçamento
    Object.entries(this.tokens.spacing).forEach(([size, value]) => {
      css += `  --spacing-${size}: ${value};\n`;
    });
    
    // Border radius
    Object.entries(this.tokens.borderRadius).forEach(([size, value]) => {
      css += `  --radius-${size}: ${value};\n`;
    });
    
    // Elevação
    Object.entries(this.tokens.elevation).forEach(([level, value]) => {
      css += `  --elevation-${level}: ${value};\n`;
    });
    
    css += '}\n';
    return css;
  }
}

// Export para uso global
window.DesignTokens = DesignTokens;
```

## 2. Componente Premium Button (components/premium-button.js)

```javascript
// components/premium-button.js
// Botão premium com todos os estados especificados

class PremiumButton extends HTMLElement {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.attachShadow({ mode: 'open' });
    this.tokens = new DesignTokens();
  }
  
  static get observedAttributes() {
    return ['variant', 'size', 'state', 'loading', 'disabled', 'icon'];
  }
  
  connectedCallback() {
    this.render();
    this.setupEventListeners();
  }
  
  attributeChangedCallback(name, oldValue, newValue) {
    if (oldValue !== newValue) {
      this.render();
    }
  }
  
  get variant() {
    return this.getAttribute('variant') || 'primary';
  }
  
  get size() {
    return this.getAttribute('size') || 'medium';
  }
  
  get state() {
    return this.getAttribute('state') || 'default';
  }
  
  get loading() {
    return this.hasAttribute('loading');
  }
  
  get disabled() {
    return this.hasAttribute('disabled');
  }
  
  get icon() {
    return this.getAttribute('icon');
  }
  
  render() {
    const variant = this.variant;
    const size = this.size;
    const state = this.state;
    const loading = this.loading;
    const disabled = this.disabled;
    const icon = this.icon;
    
    const styles = this.getStyles();
    const buttonContent = this.getButtonContent();
    
    this.shadowRoot.innerHTML = `
      <style>${styles}</style>
      <button
        class="premium-button ${variant} ${size} ${state}"
        ?disabled="${disabled || loading}"
        aria-busy="${loading}"
        aria-label="${this.getAttribute('aria-label') || this.textContent}"
      >
        ${buttonContent}
      </button>
    `;
  }
  
  getStyles() {
    return `
      :host {
        display: inline-block;
      }
      
      .premium-button {
        font-family: var(--font-family-sans, 'Inter', sans-serif);
        font-weight: 600;
        border: none;
        border-radius: var(--radius-lg, 0.5rem);
        cursor: pointer;
        transition: all var(--transition-duration-normal, 300ms) var(--transition-easing-inOut, cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1));

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura Técnica

## Estrutura do Repositório Base

```

## ADR-001: Arquitetura Técnica V12

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

### CONTEXTO:
A V12 do DIYAPP precisa suportar:
1. Escalabilidade para 100k usuários simultâneos
2. 99.99% de disponibilidade
3. Desenvolvimento paralelo com Modo Hive
4. Monitoramento completo em tempo real
5. Testes automatizados em todos os níveis

### DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura hexagonal com separação clara de responsabilidades, cache distribuído com Redis, monitoramento com Elastic APM, e stack de testes completa com Jest, Supertest e Playwright.

### OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A:** Monolito tradicional com cache em memória
  - Prós: Simples, rápido desenvolvimento
  - Contras: Não escala, acoplamento alto, difícil manutenção
- **Opção B:** Microserviços completos
  - Prós: Escalabilidade máxima, isolamento de falhas
  - Contras: Complexidade operacional alta, overhead de comunicação
- **Opção C:** Arquitetura hexagonal com módulos independentes
  - Prós: Balance entre simplicidade e escalabilidade, fácil refatoração paralela
  - Contras: Requer disciplina de desenvolvimento

**Opção escolhida:** C - Justificativa: Permite desenvolvimento paralelo (Modo Hive) enquanto mantém coesão do sistema.

### CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Desacoplamento permite refatoração paralela
- Testabilidade aumentada
- Escalabilidade modular
- Manutenção simplificada

**Negativas:**
- Curva de aprendizado para novos devs
- Overhead inicial de configuração

**Riscos:**
- Complexidade excessiva se não seguirmos padrões
- Mitigação: Code reviews rigorosos e ADRs

## Engineering Standards

### 2. Estratégia de Cache

```typescript
// src/core/infrastructure/cache/RedisCacheService.ts
import Redis from 'ioredis';
import { logger } from '../../shared/utils/logger';

export interface CacheService {
  get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null>;
  set(key: string, value: any, ttl?: number): Promise<void>;
  delete(key: string): Promise<void>;
  invalidatePattern(pattern: string): Promise<void>;
}

export class RedisCacheService implements CacheService {
  private client: Redis;
  private readonly defaultTTL = 3600; // 1 hora

  constructor() {
    this.client = new Redis({
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT || '6379'),
      retryStrategy: (times) => Math.min(times * 50, 2000)
    });

    this.client.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Redis connection error:', err);
    });
  }

  async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    try {
      const data = await this.client.get(key);
      return data ? JSON.parse(data) : null;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache get error for key ${key}:`, error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  async set(key: string, value: any, ttl?: number): Promise<void> {
    try {
      const serialized = JSON.stringify(value);
      await this.client.setex(key, ttl || this.defaultTTL, serialized);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache set error for key ${key}:`, error);
    }
  }

  async delete(key: string): Promise<void> {
    await this.client.del(key);
  }

  async invalidatePattern(pattern: string): Promise<void> {
    const keys = await this.client.keys(pattern);
    if (keys.length > 0) {
      await this.client.del(...keys);
    }
  }
}

// Padrões de chave de cache
export const CacheKeys = {
  USER: (id: string) => `user:${id}`,
  SESSION: (token: string) => `session:${token}`,
  RATE_LIMIT: (ip: string, endpoint: string) => `ratelimit:${ip}:${endpoint}`,
  API_RESPONSE: (path: string, params: string) => `api:${path}:${params}`
} as const;
```

### 3. Monitoramento (APM)

```typescript
// config/apm/elastic-apm.ts
import * as apm from 'elastic-apm-node';

export const initializeAPM = () => {
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    apm.start({
      serviceName: 'diyapp-v12',
      secretToken: process.env.ELASTIC_APM_SECRET_TOKEN,
      serverUrl: process.env.ELASTIC_APM_SERVER_URL,
      environment: process.env.NODE_ENV,
      active: true,
      captureBody: 'all',
      errorOnAbortedRequests: true,
      captureExceptions: true,
      metricsInterval: '30s'
    });
  }
};

// src/shared/utils/logger.ts
import winston from 'winston';
import { ElasticsearchTransport } from 'winston-elasticsearch';

const esTransport = new ElasticsearchTransport({
  level: 'info',
  clientOpts: { node: process.env.ELASTICSEARCH_URL },
  indexPrefix: 'diyapp-logs'
});

export const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.simple()
    }),
    esTransport
  ]
});

// Middleware de monitoramento
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';

export const monitoringMiddleware = (
  req: Request,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
) => {
  const start = Date.now();
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    const span = apm.startSpan(`${req.method} ${req.path}`);
    
    if (span) {
      span.setLabel('http.status_code', res.statusCode.toString());
      span.setLabel('http.method', req.method);
      span.setLabel('http.url', req.url);
      span.setLabel('duration', duration);
      span.end();
    }

    logger.info('HTTP Request', {
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      status: res.statusCode,
      duration,
      userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
      ip: req.ip
    });
  });

  next();
};
```

### 4. Stack de Testes

```javascript
// jest.config.js
module.exports = {
  preset: 'ts-jest',
  testEnvironment: 'node',
  roots: ['<rootDir>/src', '<rootDir>/tests'],
  collectCoverageFrom: [
    'src/**/*.{ts,js}',
    '!src/**/*.d.ts',
    '!src/index.ts',
    '!src/**/index.ts'
  ],
  coverageThreshold: {
    global: {
      branches: 80,
      functions: 80,
      lines: 80,
      statements: 80
    }
  },
  testMatch: [
    '<rootDir>/tests/unit/**/*.test.ts',
    '<rootDir>/tests/integration/**/*.test.ts'
  ],
  setupFilesAfterEnv: ['<rootDir>/tests/setup.ts'],
  globalTeardown: '<rootDir>/tests/teardown.ts'
};

// tests/setup.ts
import { initializeAPM } from '../config/apm/elastic-apm';
import { TestDatabase } from './fixtures/TestDatabase';
import { RedisMock } from './fixtures/RedisMock';

// Inicializa APM para testes
if (process.env.ENABLE_APM_IN_TESTS === 'true') {
  initializeAPM();
}

// Banco de dados de teste
export const testDB = new TestDatabase();

// Mock do Redis
export const redisMock = new RedisMock();

beforeAll(async () => {
  await testDB.connect();
});

afterAll(async () => {
  await testDB.disconnect();
  redisMock.disconnect();
});

beforeEach(async () => {
  await testDB.clear();
  redisMock.clear();
});

// Exemplo de teste unitário
// tests/unit/core/domain/User.test.ts
import { User } from '../../../src/core/domain/User';

describe('User Entity', () => {
  it('should create a valid user', () => {
    const user = User.create({
      email: 'test@example.com',
      name: 'Test User'
    });

    expect(user.id).toBeDefined();
    expect(user.email).toBe('test@example.com');
    expect(user.isActive).toBe(true);
  });

  it('should validate email format', () => {
    expect(() => {
      User.create({
        email: 'invalid-email',
        name: 'Test User'
      });
    }).toThrow('Invalid email format');
  });
});

// Exemplo de teste de integração
// tests/integration/api/auth.test.ts
import request from 'supertest';
import { app } from '../../../src/api/rest/server';

describe('Auth API', () => {
  it('should register a new user', async () => {
    const response = await request(app)
      .post('/api/v1/auth/register')
      .send({
        email: 'test@example.com',
        password: 'SecurePass123!',
        name: 'Test User'
      })
      .expect(201);

    expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('token');
    expect(response.body.user.email).toBe('test@example.com');
  });

  it('should reject weak password', async () => {
    await request(app)
      .post('/api/v1/auth/register')
      .send({
        email: 'test@example.com',
        password: '123',
        name: 'Test User'
      })
      .expect(400);
  });
});

// Configuração E2E com Playwright
// tests/e2e/playwright.config.ts
import { PlaywrightTestConfig } from '@playwright/test';

const config: PlaywrightTestConfig = {
  testDir: './tests/e2e',
  timeout: 30000,
  retries: process.env.CI ? 2 : 0,
  workers: process.env.CI ? 1 : undefined,
  use: {
    baseURL: process.env.E2E_BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
    screenshot: 'only-on-failure',
    trace: 'retain-on-failure'
  },
  projects: [
    {
      name: 'chromium',
      use: { browserName: 'chromium' }
    }
  ],
  reporter: [
    ['html', { outputFolder: 'playwright-report' }],
    ['json', { outputFile: 'playwright-results.json' }]
  ]
};

export default config;

// Exemplo de teste E2E
// tests/e2e/user-flow.spec.ts
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';

test('complete user registration flow', async ({ page }) => {
  await page.goto('/');
  
  // Navega para registro
  await page.click('text=Sign Up');
  await expect(page).toHaveURL('/register');
  
  // Preenche formulário
  await page.fill('#email', 'test@example.com');
  await page.fill('#password', 'SecurePass123!');
  await page.fill('#name', 'Test User');
  
  // Submete
  await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
  
  // Verifica redirecionamento
  await expect(page).toHaveURL('/dashboard');
  await expect(page.locator('text=Welcome Test User')).toBeVisible();
});
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO:
# diyapp-v12-core/
# ├── src/
# │   ├── api/

# ├── requirements.txt
# ├── docker-compose.yml
# ├── Dockerfile
# └── main.py

# requirements.txt
"""
fastapi==0.104.1
uvicorn[standard]==0.24.0
sqlalchemy==2.0.23
asyncpg==0.29.0
psycopg2-binary==2.9.9
redis==5.0.1
celery==5.3.4
tenacity==8.2.3

pytest-cov==4.1.0
alembic==1.13.0

# src/core/config.py
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings
from typing import Optional
import os

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # API
    API_V1_STR: str = "/api/v1"
    API_V2_STR: str = "/api/v2"
    PROJECT_NAME: str = "DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core"
    
    # Database
    DATABASE_URL: str = os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "postgresql+asyncpg://user:pass@localhost:5432/diyapp")
    DATABASE_POOL_SIZE: int = 20
    DATABASE_MAX_OVERFLOW: int = 10
    DATABASE_POOL_TIMEOUT: int = 30
    DATABASE_POOL_RECYCLE: int = 3600
    
    # Redis (for Celery and caching)
    REDIS_URL: str = os.getenv("REDIS_URL", "redis://localhost:6379/0")
    
    # Security
    SECRET_KEY: str = os.getenv("SECRET_KEY", "your-secret-key-change-in-production")
    ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30
    
    # Resilience
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD: int = 5
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT: int = 60
    HTTP_TIMEOUT: int = 10
    HTTP_MAX_RETRIES: int = 3
    HTTP_RETRY_BACKOFF: float = 0.5
    
    # Background Tasks
    CELERY_BROKER_URL: str = REDIS_URL
    CELERY_RESULT_BACKEND: str = REDIS_URL
    
    # Monitoring
    ENABLE_METRICS: bool = True
    ENABLE_TRACING: bool = True
    LOG_LEVEL: str = "INFO"
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"

settings = Settings()

# src/core/database.py
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession, create_async_engine, async_sessionmaker
from sqlalchemy.orm import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.pool import AsyncAdaptedQueuePool
import logging
from .config import settings

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

Base = declarative_base()

class DatabaseManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self._engine = None
        self._session_factory = None
        
    async def initialize(self):
        """Initialize database connection with optimized pool settings"""
        try:
            self._engine = create_async_engine(
                settings.DATABASE_URL,
                echo=False,
                poolclass=AsyncAdaptedQueuePool,
                pool_size=settings.DATABASE_POOL_SIZE,
                max_overflow=settings.DATABASE_MAX_OVERFLOW,
                pool_timeout=settings.DATABASE_POOL_TIMEOUT,
                pool_recycle=settings.DATABASE_POOL_RECYCLE,
                pool_pre_ping=True,  # Verify connections before using
                connect_args={
                    "command_timeout": 60,
                    "server_settings": {
                        "jit": "off",
                        "statement_timeout": "30000"
                    }
                }
            )
            
            self._session_factory = async_sessionmaker(
                self._engine,
                class_=AsyncSession,
                expire_on_commit=False,
                autocommit=False,
                autoflush=False
            )
            
            logger.info("Database connection pool initialized successfully")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to initialize database: {str(e)}")
            raise
    
    async def get_session(self) -> AsyncSession:
        """Get database session with automatic cleanup"""
        if not self._session_factory:
            await self.initialize()
        
        session = self._session_factory()
        try:
            yield session
        finally:
            await session.close()
    
    async def close(self):
        """Close database connections"""
        if self._engine:
            await self._engine.dispose()
            logger.info("Database connections closed")

db_manager = DatabaseManager()

# src/core/resilience.py
from circuitbreaker import circuit
from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_exponential, retry_if_exception_type
import httpx
import asyncio
from typing import Any, Callable, Type, Optional
import logging
from functools import wraps
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class ResilienceManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.circuit_breakers = {}
        self.metrics = {
            "circuit_opens": {},
            "retry_attempts": {},
            "timeouts": {}
        }
    
    def circuit_breaker(
        self,
        failure_threshold: int = 5,
        recovery_timeout: int = 60,
        expected_exception: Type[Exception] = Exception,
        name: Optional[str] = None
    ):
        """Decorator for circuit breaker pattern"""
        def decorator(func):
            cb_name = name or func.__name__
            
            @circuit(
                failure_threshold=failure_threshold,
                recovery_timeout=recovery_timeout,
                expected_exception=expected_exception,
                name=cb_name
            )
            @wraps(func)
            async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                try:
                    return await func(*args, **kwargs)
                except expected_exception as e:
                    self._record_circuit_event(cb_name, "failure")
                    raise
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.error(f"Unexpected error in {cb_name}: {str(e)}")
                    raise
            
            return wrapper
        return decorator
    
    def retry_policy(
        self,
        max_attempts: int = 3,
        wait_multiplier: float = 1,
        wait_min: float = 1,
        wait_max: float = 10,
        retry_on: Optional[Type[Exception]] = None
    ):
        """Decorator for retry with exponential backoff"""
        def decorator(func):
            @retry(
                stop=stop_after_attempt(max_attempts),
                wait=wait_exponential(
                    multiplier=wait_multiplier,
                    min=wait_min,
                    max=wait_max
                ),
                retry=retry_if_exception_type(retry_on) if retry_on else None,
                before_sleep=lambda retry_state: logger.warning(
                    f"Retrying {func.__name__}, attempt {retry_state.attempt_number}"
                )
            )
            @wraps(func)
            async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                try:
                    return await func(*args, **kwargs)
                except Exception as e:
                    self._record_retry_event(func.__name__)
                    raise
            
            return wrapper
        return decorator
    
    def timeout(self, timeout_seconds: int = 10):
        """Decorator for function timeout"""
        def decorator(func):
            @wraps(func)
            async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                try:
                    return await asyncio.wait_for(
                        func(*args, **kwargs),
                        timeout=timeout_seconds
                    )
                except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                    self._record_timeout_event(func.__name__)
                    logger.error(f"Timeout after {timeout_seconds}s in {func.__name__}")
                    raise TimeoutError(f"Operation timed out after {timeout_seconds} seconds")
            
            return wrapper
        return decorator
    
    def _record_circuit_event(self, circuit_name: str, event: str):
        if circuit_name not in self.metrics["circuit_opens"]:
            self.metrics["circuit_opens"][circuit_name] = []
        
        if event == "open":
            self.metrics["circuit_opens"][circuit_name].append(datetime.utcnow())
    
    def _record_retry_event(self, function_name: str):
        if function_name not in self.metrics["retry_attempts"]:
            self.metrics["retry_attempts"][function_name] = 0
        self.metrics["retry_attempts"][function_name] += 1
    
    def _record_timeout_event(self, function_name: str):
        if function_name not in self.metrics["timeouts"]:
            self.metrics["timeouts"][function_name] = 0
        self.metrics["timeouts"][function_name] += 1
    
    def get_metrics(self) -> dict:
        """Get resilience metrics for monitoring"""
        return {
            "circuit_breakers": {
                name: {
                    "total_opens": len(timestamps),
                    "recent_opens": len([ts for ts in timestamps 
                                       if ts > datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(hours=1)])
                }
                for name, timestamps in self.metrics["circuit_opens"].items()
            },
            "retries": self.metrics["retry_attempts"],
            "timeouts": self.metrics["timeouts"]
        }

class ResilientHTTPClient:
    def __init__(self, timeout: int = 10, max_retries: int = 3):
        self.timeout = timeout
        self.max_retries = max_retries
        self.resilience = ResilienceManager()
        
        limits = httpx.Limits(
            max_keepalive_connections=20,
            max_connections=100,
            keepalive_expiry=30
        )
        
        self.client = httpx.AsyncClient(
            timeout=timeout,
            limits=limits,
            follow_redirects=True
        )
    
    @ResilienceManager().circuit_breaker(
        failure_threshold=3,
        recovery_timeout=30,
        expected_exception=(httpx.TimeoutException, httpx.HTTPStatusError)
    )
    @ResilienceManager().retry_policy(
        max_attempts=3,
        wait_multiplier=1,
        wait_min=1,
        wait_max=5,
        retry_on=(httpx.TimeoutException, httpx.NetworkError)
    )
    async def get(self, url: str, **kwargs) -> httpx.Response:
        """Make GET request with resilience patterns"""
        return await self.client.get(url, **kwargs)
    
    async def close(self):
        await self.client.aclose()

resilience_manager = ResilienceManager()
http_client = ResilientHTTPClient()

# src/models/database.py
from sqlalchemy import Column, Integer, String, DateTime, Boolean, Text, ForeignKey, JSON
from sqlalchemy.sql import func
from sqlalchemy.orm import relationship
from src.core.database import Base

class User(Base):
    __tablename__ = "users"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)
    email = Column(String(255), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    username = Column(String(100), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    hashed_password = Column(String(255), nullable=False)
    full_name = Column(String(255))
    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    is_superuser = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
    
    tasks = relationship("Task", back_populates="owner", cascade="all, delete-orphan")

class Task(Base):
    __tablename__ = "tasks"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)
    title = Column(String(255), nullable=False)
    description = Column(Text)
    status = Column(String(50), default="pending", index=True)
    priority = Column(String(20), default="medium")
    due_date = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))
    metadata = Column(JSON, default=dict)
    owner_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"), nullable=False)
    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
    completed_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))
    
    owner = relationship("User", back_populates="tasks")

# src/models/schemas.py
from pydantic import BaseModel, EmailStr, Field, validator
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime
from enum import Enum

class TaskStatus(str, Enum):
    PENDING = "pending"
    IN_PROGRESS = "in_progress"
    COMPLETED = "completed"
    FAILED = "failed"

class TaskPriority(str, Enum):
    LOW = "low"
    MEDIUM = "medium"
    HIGH = "high"
    CRITICAL = "critical"

# User Schemas
class UserBase(BaseModel):
    email: EmailStr
    username: str = Field(..., min_length=3, max_length=50)
    full_name: Optional[str] = None

class UserCreate(UserBase):
    password: str = Field(..., min_length=8)

class UserUpdate(BaseModel):
    email: Optional[EmailStr] = None
    username: Optional[str] = Field(None, min_length=3, max_length=50)
    full_name: Optional[str] = None
    password: Optional[str] = Field(None, min_length=8)

class UserInDB(UserBase):
    id: int
    is_active: bool
    is_superuser: bool
    created_at: datetime
    updated_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    
    class Config:
        from_attributes = True

class UserResponse(UserInDB):
    pass

# Task Schemas
class TaskBase(BaseModel):
    title: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=255)
    description: Optional[str] = None
    status: TaskStatus = TaskStatus.PENDING
    priority: TaskPriority = TaskPriority.MEDIUM
    due_date: Optional[datetime] = None
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)

class TaskCreate(TaskBase):
    owner_id: int

class TaskUpdate(BaseModel):
    title: Optional[str] = Field(None, min_length=1, max_length=255)
    description: Optional[str] = None
    status: Optional[TaskStatus] = None
    priority: Optional[TaskPriority] = None
    due_date: Optional[datetime] = None
    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None

class TaskInDB(TaskBase):
    id: int
    owner_id: int
    created_at: datetime
    updated_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    completed_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    
    class Config:
        from_attributes = True

class TaskResponse(TaskInDB):
    owner: Optional[UserResponse] = None

# API Response Schemas
class PaginatedResponse(BaseModel):
    items: List[Any]
    total: int
    page: int
    size: int
    pages: int

class ErrorResponse(BaseModel):
    detail: str
    error_code: Optional[str] = None
    correlation_id: Optional[str] = None

```typescript
// src/components/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { Spinner } from '../Spinner/Spinner';
import { useButtonStyles } from './useButtonStyles';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  loading?: boolean;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
}

export const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      loading = false,
      disabled = false,
      fullWidth = false,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      className = '',
      onClick,
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const isDisabled = disabled || loading;
    const styles = useButtonStyles({ variant, size, fullWidth, isDisabled });

    const handleClick = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLButtonElement>) => {
      if (!isDisabled && onClick) {
        onClick(e);
      }
    };

    const getIconSize = () => {
      switch (size) {
        case 'sm': return tokens.typography.fontSize.sm;
        case 'lg': return tokens.typography.fontSize.lg;
        default: return tokens.typography.fontSize.base;
      }
    };

    return (
      <button
        ref={ref}
        className={`${styles.base} ${className}`}
        disabled={isDisabled}
        onClick={handleClick}
        aria-busy={loading}
        {...props}
      >
        {loading && (
          <span className={styles.spinnerContainer}>
            <Spinner size={size} />
          </span>
        )}
        
        {!loading && leftIcon && (
          <span 
            className={styles.iconContainer}
            style={{ fontSize: getIconSize() }}
            aria-hidden="true"
          >
            {leftIcon}
          </span>
        )}
        
        <span className={styles.content}>
          {children}
        </span>
        
        {!loading && rightIcon && (
          <span 
            className={styles.iconContainer}
            style={{ fontSize: getIconSize() }}
            aria-hidden="true"
          >
            {rightIcon}
          </span>
        )}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';
```

```typescript
// src/components/Button/useButtonStyles.ts
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { ButtonVariant, ButtonSize } from './Button';

interface UseButtonStylesProps {
  variant: ButtonVariant;
  size: ButtonSize;
  fullWidth: boolean;
  isDisabled: boolean;
}

export const useButtonStyles = ({
  variant,
  size,
  fullWidth,
  isDisabled,
}: UseButtonStylesProps) => {
  const baseStyles = {
    base: [
      'inline-flex items-center justify-center',
      'font-medium whitespace-nowrap',
      'transition-colors duration-200',
      'focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2',
      'disabled:cursor-not-allowed',
      fullWidth ? 'w-full' : '',
    ].join(' '),
    spinnerContainer: 'absolute',
    iconContainer: 'flex items-center',
    content: '',
  };

  const variantStyles = {
    primary: {
      base: [
        'text-white',
        `bg-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`,
        `hover:bg-${tokens.colors.primary[600]}`,
        `focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`,
        isDisabled ? `bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}` : '',
      ].join(' '),
    },
    secondary: {
      base: [
        `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]}`,
        `bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]}`,
        `hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}`,
        `focus:ring-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}`,
        isDisabled ? `bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[400]}` : '',
      ].join(' '),
    },
    outline: {
      base: [
        `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]}`,
        'bg-transparent',
        `border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}`,
        `hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[50]}`,
        `focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`,
        isDisabled ? `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[400]} border-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}` : '',
      ].join(' '),
    },
    ghost: {
      base: [
        `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]}`,
        'bg-transparent',
        `hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]}`,
        `focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`,
        isDisabled ? `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[400]}` : '',
      ].join(' '),
    },
  };

  const sizeStyles = {
    sm: {
      base: [
        `text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm}`,
        `px-${tokens.spacing.sm}`,
        `py-${tokens.spacing.xs}`,
        `rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.md}`,
      ].join(' '),
      iconContainer: `mr-${tokens.spacing.xs}`,
      content: '',
    },
    md: {
      base: [
        `text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.base}`,
        `px-${tokens.spacing.md}`,
        `py-${tokens.spacing.sm}`,
        `rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.md}`,
      ].join(' '),
      iconContainer: `mr-${tokens.spacing.sm}`,
      content: '',
    },
    lg: {
      base: [
        `text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.lg}`,
        `px-${tokens.spacing.lg}`,
        `py-${tokens.spacing.md}`,
        `rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.lg}`,
      ].join(' '),
      iconContainer: `mr-${tokens.spacing.md}`,
      content: '',
    },
  };

  return {
    base: `${baseStyles.base} ${variantStyles[variant].base} ${sizeStyles[size].base}`,
    spinnerContainer: baseStyles.spinnerContainer,
    iconContainer: `${baseStyles.iconContainer} ${sizeStyles[size].iconContainer}`,
    content: baseStyles.content,
  };
};
```

```typescript
// src/components/Button/Button.test.tsx
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import { Button } from './Button';

describe('Button', () => {
  it('renders with default props', () => {
    render(<Button>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('type', 'button');
  });

  it('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn();
    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click me</Button>);
    
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    fireEvent.click(button);
    
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  it('does not call onClick when disabled', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn();
    render(
      <Button disabled onClick={handleClick}>
        Click me
      </Button>
    );
    
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    fireEvent.click(button);
    
    expect(handleClick).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  it('does not call onClick when loading', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn();
    render(
      <Button loading onClick={handleClick}>
        Click me
      </Button>
    );
    
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    fireEvent.click(button);
    
    expect(handleClick).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
  });

  it('renders with left icon', () => {
    const leftIcon = <span data-testid="left-icon">←</span>;
    render(<Button leftIcon={leftIcon}>Back</Button>);
    
    expect(screen.getByTestId('left-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveTextContent('Back');
  });

  it('renders with right icon', () => {
    const rightIcon = <span data-testid="right-icon">→</span>;
    render(<Button rightIcon={rightIcon}>Next</Button>);
    
    expect(screen.getByTestId('right-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('applies correct variant classes', () => {
    const { rerender } = render(<Button variant="primary">Primary</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('bg-primary-500');

    rerender(<Button variant="secondary">Secondary</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('bg-neutral-100');

    rerender(<Button variant="outline">Outline</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('border');

    rerender(<Button variant="ghost">Ghost</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('bg-transparent');
  });

  it('applies correct size classes', () => {
    const { rerender } = render(<Button size="sm">Small</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('text-sm');

    rerender(<Button size="md">Medium</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('text-base');

    rerender(<Button size="lg">Large</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('text-lg');
  });

  it('renders as full width when specified', () => {
    render(<Button fullWidth>Full Width</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('w-full');
  });

  it('supports keyboard navigation', () => {
    render(<Button>Accessible</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: 'Enter', code: 'Enter' });
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: ' ', code: 'Space' });
    
    expect(button).toHaveFocus();
  });
});
