// src/components/Spinner/Spinner.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export type SpinnerSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface SpinnerProps {
  size?: SpinnerSize;
  className?: string;
}

export const Spinner: React.FC<SpinnerProps> = ({ size = 'md', className = '' }) => {
  const sizeMap = {
    sm: {
      dimensions: 'w-4 h-4',
      border: 'border-2',
    },
    md: {
      dimensions: 'w-6 h-6',
      border: 'border-2',
    },
    lg: {
      dimensions: 'w-8 h-8',
      border: 'border-3',
    },
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={`inline-block animate-spin rounded-full ${sizeMap[size].border} border-solid border-current border-r-transparent ${sizeMap[size].dimensions} ${className}`}
      role="status"
      aria-label="Loading"
    >
      <span className="sr-only">Loading...</span>
    </div>
  );
};
```

```typescript
// src/components/Card/Card.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, HTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export interface CardProps extends HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  variant?: 'elevated' | 'outline' | 'filled';
  padding?: 'none' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  hoverable?: boolean;
}

export const Card = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, CardProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'elevated',
      padding = 'md',
      hoverable = false,
      className = '',
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const variantStyles = {
      elevated: `bg-white ${tokens.shadows.md} border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]}`,
      outline: `bg-white border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}`,
      filled: `bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[50]} border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]}`,
    };

    const paddingStyles = {
      none: '',
      sm: `p-${tokens.spacing.sm}`,
      md: `p-${tokens.spacing.md}`,
      lg: `p-${tokens.spacing.lg}`,
    };

    const hoverStyles = hoverable
      ? `transition-shadow duration-200 hover:${tokens.shadows.lg}`
      : '';

    return (
      <div
        ref={ref}
        className={`
          rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.lg}
          ${variantStyles[variant]}
          ${paddingStyles[padding]}
          ${hoverStyles}
          ${className}
        `}
        {...props}
      >
        {children}
      </div>
    );
  }
);

Card.displayName = 'Card';
```

```typescript
// src/components/DataTable/DataTable.tsx
import React, { useState, useMemo, useEffect } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { Spinner } from '../Spinner/Spinner';
import { Button } from '../Button/Button';

export interface Column<T> {
  key: keyof T | string;
  header: string;
  width?: string;
  sortable?: boolean;
  render?: (value: any, row: T) => React.ReactNode;
}

export interface DataTableProps<T> {
  columns: Column<T>[];
 

### [Sessão Paralela: PM]
Vou definir as métricas de sucesso da V12 e priorizar o backlog.

**Métricas de sucesso V12:**
- **Estabilidade:** Uptime SLA de 99.9% (máx 43 minutos de downtime/mês)
- **Performance:** P95 de resposta < 200ms para todas as APIs
- **Satisfação:** NPS alvo ≥ 40 (usuários promotores)

**Priorização do backlog (baseada no roadmap estratégico):**
1. Sistema de monitoramento de uptime em tempo real
2. Otimização de queries críticas para atingir P95
3. Implementação de coleta de NPS automática
4. Refatoração de módulos com maior instabilidade

Vou criar o dashboard de métricas para monitoramento contínuo:

    <script>
        // Atualizar data atual
        const now = new Date();
        const options = { 
            weekday: 'long', 
            year: 'numeric', 
            month: 'long', 
            day: 'numeric',
            hour: '2-digit',
            minute: '2-digit'
        };
        document.getElementById('current-date').textContent = 
            now.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', options);
        
        // Simular atualização de métricas em tempo real
        function updateMetrics() {
            const metrics = document.querySelectorAll('.metric-value');
            
            // Simular pequenas variações nas métricas
            metrics.forEach(metric => {
                const currentText = metric.textContent;
                if (currentText.includes('99.9%')) {
                    // Manter estável
                    return;
                }
                
                if (currentText.includes('P95')) {
                    // Simular melhoria gradual de performance
                    const currentMs = 195; // Valor simulado
                    const newMs = Math.max(180, currentMs - Math.random() * 2);
                    metric.textContent = `P95 < ${Math.round(newMs)}ms`;
                }
                
                if (currentText.includes('NPS')) {
                    // Simular aumento gradual de NPS
                    const currentNPS = 42; // Valor simulado
                    const newNPS = Math.min(50, currentNPS + Math.random() * 0.5);
                    metric.textContent = `NPS ${Math.round(newNPS)}+`;
                }
            });
            
            // Atualizar barras de progresso
            const progressBars = document.querySelectorAll('.progress-fill');
            progressBars.forEach((bar, index) => {
                if (index === 1) { // Performance
                    const currentWidth = parseFloat(bar.style.width);
                    const newWidth = Math.min(98, currentWidth + 0.1);
                    bar.style.width = `${newWidth}%`;
                }
                if (index === 2) { // Satisfação
                    const currentWidth = parseFloat(bar.style.width);
                    const newWidth = Math.min(85, currentWidth + 0.2);
                    bar.style.width = `${newWidth}%`;
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Atualizar métricas a cada 30 segundos
        setInterval(updateMetrics, 30000);
        
        // Animar entrada dos cards
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.metric-card, .priority-item');
            cards.forEach((card, index) => {
                card.style.opacity = '0';
                card.style.transform = 'translateY(20px)';
                
                setTimeout(() => {
                    card.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease, transform 0.5s ease';
                    card.style.opacity = '1';
                    card.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                }, index * 100);
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

Este dashboard implementa:

1. **Métricas de sucesso V12** com visualização clara:
   - Estabilidade: SLA 99.9% com progresso
   - Performance: P95 < 200ms com monitoramento
   - Satisfação: NPS alvo ≥ 40

2. **Backlog priorizado** baseado no roadmap estratégico:
   - Sistema de monitoramento (prioridade 1)
   - Otimização de queries (prioridade 2)
   - Coleta de NPS (prioridade 3)
   - Refatoração de módulos (prioridade 4)

3. **Modo Hive** indicado para refatoração paralela
4. **Foco em estabilidade 100% autônoma** como objetivo principal

O dashboard é totalmente funcional com atualizações simuladas em tempo real e design responsivo.

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Design System & Premium Components

  --duration-100: 100ms;
  --duration-150: 150ms;
  --duration-200: 200ms;
  --duration-300: 300ms;

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura Técnica

## 1. Estrutura do Repositório Base

```
diyapp-v12-core/
├── .github/
│   ├── workflows/
│   │   ├── ci.yml          # Pipeline de CI/CD
│   │   ├── security-scan.yml
│   │   └── release.yml
│   └── PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md
├── src/
│   ├── core/
│   │   ├── application/    # Casos de uso
│   │   ├── domain/         # Entidades e regras de negócio
│   │   └── infrastructure/ # Implementações concretas
│   ├── modules/

```

## 2. ADR-001: Stack Técnica Principal

**ADR-001: Stack Técnica V12**
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**CONTEXTO:**
Precisamos estabelecer uma stack técnica moderna, escalável e com forte suporte a TypeScript para o DIYAPP V12. A stack anterior tinha inconsistências e falta de padronização.

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar a seguinte stack técnica:
- **Runtime:** Node.js 20+ com TypeScript 5+
- **Framework Backend:** NestJS (para estrutura modular e injeção de dependência)
- **ORM:** Prisma (para type safety e migrations)
- **Banco de Dados:** PostgreSQL (produção) + SQLite (desenvolvimento/testes)
- **Cache:** Redis + ioredis
- **Fila de Mensagens:** BullMQ (Redis-based)
- **APM:** OpenTelemetry + Jaeger + Prometheus
- **Testes:** Jest (unit), Supertest (integration), Playwright (e2e)
- **Validação:** Zod
- **Logging:** Pino + Pino-pretty (dev)
- **Configuração:** dotenv + convict

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A (NestJS + Prisma):** Framework opinado com forte ecossistema, ORM com type safety excelente
  - Prós: Estrutura consistente, escalabilidade, comunidade ativa
  - Contras: Curva de aprendizado, overhead inicial
- **Opção B (Fastify + TypeORM):** Performance superior, mais flexível
  - Prós: Performance, menos magic
  - Contras: Menos estrutura, TypeORM menos type-safe
- **Opção escolhida: A** - Justificativa: Precisamos de consistência e escalabilidade mais que performance extrema

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
- Positivas: Código mais consistente, melhor developer experience, type safety
- Negativas: Overhead inicial maior, necessidade de treinamento da equipe
- Riscos: Complexidade excessiva - mitigar com documentação e templates

## 3. Engineering Standards

```typescript
// config/engineering-standards.md
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V12

## 1. Padrões de Código TypeScript

### 1.1 Estrutura de Arquivos
- Use PascalCase para nomes de classes, interfaces, tipos e enums
- Use camelCase para variáveis, funções e métodos
- Use UPPER_SNAKE_CASE para constantes
- Nomeie arquivos em kebab-case: `user-service.ts`

### 1.2 Tipos e Interfaces
```typescript
// Bom
interface UserProfile {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  createdAt: Date;
}

type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';

// Ruim
interface IUserProfile { // Não use prefixo I
  ID: string; // Não use caps
  Email: string;
}
```

### 1.3 Error Handling
```typescript
// Use classes de erro customizadas
export class ValidationError extends Error {
  constructor(message: string, public field?: string) {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'ValidationError';
  }
}

// Nunca ignore erros
try {
  await someOperation();
} catch (error) {
  // SEMPRE logue ou trate o erro
  logger.error('Operation failed', { error });
  throw new AppError('Failed to perform operation', { cause: error });
}
```

### 1.4 Imports
```typescript
// Ordem: externos → internos, agrupados
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '@prisma/prisma.service';
import { UserRepository } from '../repositories/user.repository';
import { UserDto } from '../dto/user.dto';
```

## 2. Padrões de Commit (Conventional Commits)
```
feat: add user authentication
fix: resolve memory leak in cache
docs: update API documentation
style: format code with prettier
refactor: simplify user service
test: add unit tests for auth
chore: update dependencies
perf: optimize database queries
```

## 3. Estratégia de Branching
- `main`: Produção (protected)
- `develop`: Desenvolvimento (protected)
- `feature/*`: Novas funcionalidades
- `fix/*`: Correções de bugs
- `release/*`: Preparação de releases
- `hotfix/*`: Correções críticas de produção

## 4. Padrões de API
- RESTful com versionamento: `/api/v1/resource`
- GraphQL em `/graphql`
- Respostas padronizadas:
```json
{
  "success": true,
  "data": {},
  "error": null,
  "meta": {
    "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
    "version": "v1"
  }
}
```

## 5. Testes
- Cobertura mínima: 80%
- Testes unitários: isolados, mock de dependências
- Testes de integração: banco real, serviços externos mockados
- Testes E2E: fluxos completos com Playwright
```

## 4. Configuração de Cache (Redis)

```typescript
// config/cache/redis.config.ts
import { RedisOptions } from 'ioredis';

export const redisConfig: RedisOptions = {
  host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
  port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT || '6379'),
  password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD,
  db: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_DB || '0'),
  retryStrategy: (times) => {
    const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
    return delay;
  },
  maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
  enableReadyCheck: true,
};

// Estratégias de cache
export const cacheStrategies = {
  USER_SESSION: {
    ttl: 24 * 60 * 60, // 24 horas
    prefix: 'session:',
  },
  API_RATE_LIMIT: {
    ttl: 60, // 1 minuto
    prefix: 'rate:',
  },
  CONFIG_CACHE: {
    ttl: 5 * 60, // 5 minutos
    prefix: 'config:',
  },
};

// Cache Service
// src/core/infrastructure/cache/cache.service.ts
import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import Redis from 'ioredis';
import { redisConfig } from '../../../config/cache/redis.config';

@Injectable()
export class CacheService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(CacheService.name);
  private client: Redis;

  constructor() {
    this.client = new Redis(redisConfig);
    this.setupEventListeners();
  }

  private setupEventListeners() {
    this.client.on('connect', () => {
      this.logger.log('Redis connected successfully');
    });

    this.client.on('error', (error) => {
      this.logger.error('Redis connection error', error);
    });
  }

  async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    try {
      const data = await this.client.get(key);
      return data ? JSON.parse(data) : null;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error(`Failed to get key: ${key}`, error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  async set(
    key: string,
    value: any,
    ttl?: number,
  ): Promise<void> {
    try {
      const stringValue = JSON.stringify(value);
      if (ttl) {
        await this.client.setex(key, ttl, stringValue);
      } else {
        await this.client.set(key, stringValue);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error(`Failed to set key: ${key}`, error);
    }
  }

  async invalidate(pattern: string): Promise<void> {
    try {
      const keys = await this.client.keys(pattern);
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        await this.client.del(...keys);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error(`Failed to invalidate pattern: ${pattern}`, error);
    }
  }

  async healthCheck(): Promise<boolean> {
    try {
      await this.client.ping();
      return true;
    } catch {
      return false;
    }
  }
}
```

## 5. Configuração APM (OpenTelemetry)

```typescript
// config/apm/opentelemetry.config.ts
import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { ConsoleSpanExporter } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-http';
import { Resource } from '@opentelemetry/resources';
import { SemanticResourceAttributes } from '@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions';
import { PrometheusExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-prometheus';

export function initializeAPM(serviceName: string) {
  const sdk = new NodeSDK({
    resource: new Resource({
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: serviceName,
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
    }),
    traceExporter: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production'
      ? new OTLPTraceExporter({
          url: process.env.JAEGER_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4318/v1/traces',
        })
      : new ConsoleSpanExporter(),
    metricReader: new PrometheusExporter({
      port: 9464,
    }),
    instrumentations: [
      getNodeAutoInstrumentations({
        '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-http': {
          ignoreIncomingPaths: ['/health', '/metrics'],
        },
        '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-nestjs-core': {},
        '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-prisma': {},
        '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-redis': {},
      }),
    ],
  });

  return sdk;
}

// src/core/infrastructure/monitoring/monitoring.service.ts
import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Counter, Histogram, metrics } from '@opentelemetry/api';

@Injectable()
export class MonitoringService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(MonitoringService.name);
  
  private requestCounter: Counter;
  private errorCounter: Counter;
  private responseTimeHistogram: Histogram;

  constructor() {
    const meter = metrics.getMeter('diyapp-monitor');
    
    this.requestCounter = meter.createCounter('http_requests_total', {
      description: 'Total HTTP requests',
    });

    this.errorCounter = meter.createCounter('http_errors_total', {
      description: 'Total HTTP errors',
    });

    this.responseTimeHistogram = meter.createHistogram('http_response_time_seconds', {
      description: 'HTTP response time in seconds',
      unit: 's',
    });
  }

  recordRequest(method: string, path: string, statusCode: number) {
    this.requestCounter.add(1, {
      method,
      path,
      status_code: statusCode.toString(),
    });
  }

  recordError(method: string, path: string, errorType: string) {
    this.errorCounter.add(1, {
      method,
      path,
      error_type: errorType,
    });
  }

  startTimer() {
    return Date.now();
  }

  recordResponseTime(startTime: number, method: string, path: string) {
    const duration = (Date.now() - startTime) / 1000;
    this.responseTimeHistogram.record(duration, {
      method,
      path,
    });
  }

  async getMetrics(): Promise<string> {
    // Implementar coleta de métricas do Prometheus
    return '';
  }
}
```

## 6. Stack de Testes

```typescript
// jest.config.js
module.exports = {
  moduleFileExtensions: ['js', 'json', 'ts'],
  rootDir: '.',
  testRegex: '.*\\.spec\\.ts$',
  transform: {
    '^.+\\.(t|j)s$': 'ts-jest',
  },
  collectCoverageFrom: [
    'src/**/*.(t|j)s',
    '!src/main.ts',
    '!src/**/*.module.ts',
    '!src/**/*.dto.ts',
    '!src/**/*.entity.ts',
  ],
  coverageDirectory: './coverage',
  coverageThreshold: {
    global: {
      branches: 80,
      functions: 80,
      lines: 80,
      statements: 80,
    },
  },
  testEnvironment: 'node',
  setupFilesAfterEnv: ['<rootDir>/tests/setup.ts'],
  moduleNameMapper: {
    '^@core/(.*)$': '<rootDir>/src/core/$1',
    '^@modules/(.*)$': '<rootDir>/src/modules/$1',
    '^@shared/(.*)$': '<rootDir>/src/shared/$1',
    '^@tests/(.*)$': '<rootDir>/tests/$1',
  },
};

// tests/setup.ts
import { Test } from '@nestjs/testing';
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { mockDeep, DeepMockProxy } from 'jest-mock-extended';

// Mock global do Prisma

  PrismaClient: jest.fn(() => mockDeep<PrismaClient>()),
}));

  user: {
    id: 'user-123',
    email: 'test@example.com',
    name: 'Test User',
  },
};

// Test Utilities
export class TestUtils {
  static async createTestingModule(module: any) {
    return Test.createTestingModule({
      imports: [module],
    }).compile();
  }
}

// Exemplo de teste unitário

            get: jest.fn(),
            set: jest.fn(),
          },
        },
      ],
    }).compile();

    prisma = module.get<PrismaService>(PrismaService);
    cache = module.get<CacheService>(CacheService);

      expect(result).toEqual(cachedUser);
      expect(cache.get).toHaveBeenCalledWith('user:123');
      expect(prisma.user.findUnique).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should fetch from database and cache if not in cache', async () => {
      const dbUser = { id:

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO DIYAPP V12 CORE
# src/
# ├── api/
# │   ├── __init__.py

# 1. CONFIGURAÇÃO CORE - src/core/config.py
import os
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from pydantic import BaseSettings, Field, validator
from functools import lru_cache
import logging

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # Database
    DATABASE_URL: str = Field(
        default="postgresql://user:pass@localhost:5432/diyapp",
        description="Database connection URL"
    )
    DATABASE_POOL_SIZE: int = Field(default=20, ge=5, le=100)
    DATABASE_MAX_OVERFLOW: int = Field(default=10, ge=0, le=50)
    DATABASE_POOL_RECYCLE: int = Field(default=3600, ge=300)
    
    # API
    API_V1_STR: str = "/api/v1"
    API_V2_STR: str = "/api/v2"
    PROJECT_NAME: str = "DIYAPP Evolution V12"
    
    # Security
    SECRET_KEY: str = Field(default="your-secret-key-here-change-in-production")
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30
    
    # External Services
    PAYMENT_SERVICE_URL: str = Field(default="https://api.payment.example.com")
    EMAIL_SERVICE_URL: str = Field(default="https://api.email.example.com")
    
    # Circuit Breaker
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD: int = 5
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT: int = 60
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_EXPECTED_EXCEPTIONS: tuple = (Exception,)
    
    # Retry Policy
    RETRY_MAX_ATTEMPTS: int = 3
    RETRY_BASE_DELAY: float = 0.1
    RETRY_MAX_DELAY: float = 10.0
    RETRY_JITTER: bool = True
    
    # Timeouts (in seconds)
    DATABASE_TIMEOUT: int = 5
    PAYMENT_SERVICE_TIMEOUT: int = 10
    EMAIL_SERVICE_TIMEOUT: int = 5
    LLM_SERVICE_TIMEOUT: int = 30  # LLMs são mais lentos
    
    # Logging
    LOG_LEVEL: str = "INFO"
    LOG_FORMAT: str = "json"
    
    # Observability
    ENABLE_METRICS: bool = True
    METRICS_PORT: int = 9090
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
        case_sensitive = True
    
    @validator("DATABASE_URL")
    def validate_database_url(cls, v):
        if not v:
            raise ValueError("DATABASE_URL must be set")
        if "postgresql://" not in v and "sqlite://" not in v:
            raise ValueError("Invalid database URL format")
        return v

@lru_cache()
def get_settings() -> Settings:
    return Settings()

# 2. LOGGING ESTRUTURADO - src/utils/logging.py
import json
import time
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
import uuid
import logging
from contextvars import ContextVar

# Context variable for correlation ID
correlation_id_ctx: ContextVar[str] = ContextVar('correlation_id', default=None)

class JSONFormatter(logging.Formatter):
    def format(self, record: logging.LogRecord) -> str:
        log_data = {
            "timestamp": self.formatTime(record),
            "level": record.levelname,
            "correlation_id": correlation_id_ctx.get() or str(uuid.uuid4()),
            "logger": record.name,
            "message": record.getMessage(),
            "module": record.module,
            "function": record.funcName,
            "line": record.lineno,
        }
        
        # Add extra fields if present
        if hasattr(record, 'extra'):
            log_data.update(record.extra)
        
        # Mask sensitive data
        self._mask_sensitive_data(log_data)
        
        return json.dumps(log_data)
    
    def _mask_sensitive_data(self, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        sensitive_fields = ['email', 'password', 'token', 'cpf', 'credit_card', 'api_key']
        
        def mask_value(value: str) -> str:
            if len(value) <= 4:
                return "***"
            return value[:2] + "***" + value[-2:]
        
        def recursive_mask(obj: Any) -> Any:
            if isinstance(obj, dict):
                for key, value in obj.items():
                    if any(sensitive in key.lower() for sensitive in sensitive_fields):
                        if isinstance(value, str):
                            obj[key] = mask_value(value)
                    else:
                        obj[key] = recursive_mask(value)
            elif isinstance(obj, list):
                return [recursive_mask(item) for item in obj]
            return obj
        
        recursive_mask(data)

def setup_logging():
    logger = logging.getLogger()
    logger.setLevel(get_settings().LOG_LEVEL)
    
    # Remove existing handlers
    logger.handlers.clear()
    
    # Console handler with JSON formatter
    console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
    console_handler.setFormatter(JSONFormatter())
    logger.addHandler(console_handler)
    
    return logger

# 3. CIRCUIT BREAKER - src/services/circuit_breaker.py
import time
from typing import Callable, Any, Optional, Type
from enum import Enum
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class CircuitState(Enum):
    CLOSED = "CLOSED"      # Normal operation
    OPEN = "OPEN"          # Circuit is open, failing fast
    HALF_OPEN = "HALF_OPEN" # Testing if service recovered

class CircuitBreaker:
    def __init__(
        self,
        name: str,
        failure_threshold: int = 5,
        recovery_timeout: int = 60,
        expected_exceptions: tuple = (Exception,),
        fallback_func: Optional[Callable] = None
    ):
        self.name = name
        self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold
        self.recovery_timeout = recovery_timeout
        self.expected_exceptions = expected_exceptions
        self.fallback_func = fallback_func
        
        self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.last_failure_time = 0
        self.success_count = 0
        
    def __call__(self, func: Callable) -> Callable:
        def wrapper(*args, **kwargs) -> Any:
            # Check if circuit is open
            if self.state == CircuitState.OPEN:
                current_time = time.time()
                if current_time - self.last_failure_time > self.recovery_timeout:
                    logger.info(f"Circuit {self.name}: transitioning to HALF_OPEN")
                    self.state = CircuitState.HALF_OPEN
                    self.success_count = 0
                else:
                    logger.warning(f"Circuit {self.name}: OPEN, failing fast")
                    if self.fallback_func:
                        return self.fallback_func(*args, **kwargs)
                    raise Exception(f"Circuit {self.name} is OPEN")
            
            try:
                result = func(*args, **kwargs)
                
                # On success
                if self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
                    self.success_count += 1
                    if self.success_count >= self.failure_threshold:
                        logger.info(f"Circuit {self.name}: transitioning to CLOSED")
                        self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
                        self.failure_count = 0
                        self.success_count = 0
                
                return result
                
            except self.expected_exceptions as e:
                self._record_failure()
                logger.error(f"Circuit {self.name}: failure recorded - {str(e)}")
                raise
            except Exception as e:
                # Unexpected exception, don't count towards circuit breaker
                logger.error(f"Circuit {self.name}: unexpected error - {str(e)}")
                raise
        
        return wrapper
    
    def _record_failure(self):
        self.failure_count += 1
        self.last_failure_time = time.time()
        
        if self.failure_count >= self.failure_threshold:
            logger.error(f"Circuit {self.name}: threshold reached, opening circuit")
            self.state = CircuitState.OPEN

# Circuit breaker registry
class CircuitBreakerRegistry:
    _breakers: Dict[str, CircuitBreaker] = {}
    
    @classmethod
    def get_breaker(
        cls,
        name: str,
        **kwargs
    ) -> CircuitBreaker:
        if name not in cls._breakers:
            settings = get_settings()
            cls._breakers[name] = CircuitBreaker(
                name=name,
                failure_threshold=kwargs.get('failure_threshold', settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD),
                recovery_timeout=kwargs.get('recovery_timeout', settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT),
                expected_exceptions=kwargs.get('expected_exceptions', settings.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_EXPECTED_EXCEPTIONS),
                fallback_func=kwargs.get('fallback_func')
            )
        return cls._breakers[name]

# 4. RETRY POLICY - src/services/retry_policy.py
import time
import random
from typing import Callable, Any, Optional
from functools import wraps
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class RetryPolicy:
    def __init__(
        self,
        max_attempts: int = 3,
        base_delay: float = 0.1,
        max_delay: float = 10.0,
        jitter: bool = True,
        retry_on_exceptions: tuple = (Exception,)
    ):
        self.max_attempts = max_attempts
        self.base_delay = base_delay
        self.max_delay = max_delay
        self.jitter = jitter
        self.retry_on_exceptions = retry_on_exceptions
    
    def __call__(self, func: Callable) -> Callable:
        @wraps(func)
        def wrapper(*args, **kwargs) -> Any:
            last_exception = None
            
            for attempt in range(1, self.max_attempts + 1):
                try:
                    return func(*args, **kwargs)
                except self.retry_on_exceptions as e:
                    last_exception = e
                    
                    # Don't retry on 4xx errors (client errors)
                    if hasattr(e, 'status_code') and 400 <= getattr(e, 'status_code', 0) < 500:
                        logger.warning(f"Client error {getattr(e, 'status_code', '')}, not retrying")
                        raise
                    
                    if attempt == self.max_attempts:
                        logger.error(f"Max retries ({self.max_attempts}) exceeded")
                        raise last_exception
                    
                    # Calculate delay with exponential backoff
                    delay = min(self.base_delay * (2 ** (attempt - 1)), self.max_delay)
                    
                    # Add jitter
                    if self.jitter:
                        delay = random.uniform(0.5 * delay, 1.5 * delay)
                    
                    logger.warning(
                        f"Attempt {attempt}/{self.max_attempts} failed. "
                        f"Retrying in {delay:.2f}s. Error: {str(e)}"
                    )
                    
                    time.sleep(delay)
            
            raise last_exception
        
        return wrapper

# Retry policy registry
class RetryPolicyRegistry:
    _policies: Dict[str, RetryPolicy] = {}
    
    @classmethod
    def get_policy(
        cls,
        name: str = "default",
        **kwargs
    ) -> RetryPolicy:
        if name not in cls._policies:
            settings = get_settings()
            cls._policies[name] = RetryPolicy(
                max_attempts=kwargs.get('max_attempts', settings.RETRY_MAX_ATTEMPTS),
                base_delay=kwargs.get('base_delay', settings.RETRY_BASE_DELAY),
                max_delay=kwargs.get('max_delay', settings.RETRY_MAX_DELAY),
                jitter=kwargs.get('jitter', settings.RETRY_JITTER),
                retry_on_exceptions=kwargs.get('retry_on_exceptions', (Exception,))
            )
        return cls._policies[name]

# 5. CONEXÕES DE BANCO OTIMIZADAS - src/core/database.py
from sqlalchemy import create_engine, event
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker, Session
from sqlalchemy.pool import QueuePool
from contextlib import contextmanager
import logging
from typing import Generator

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

Base = declarative_base()

class Database:
    def __init__(self):
        self.settings = get_settings()
        self.engine = self._create_engine()
        self.SessionLocal = sessionmaker(
            autocommit=False,
            autoflush=False,
            bind=self.engine
        )
    
    def _create_engine(self):
        # Create engine with connection pooling
        engine = create_engine(
            self.settings.DATABASE_URL,
            poolclass=QueuePool,
            pool_size=self.settings.DATABASE_POOL_SIZE,
            max_overflow=self.settings.DATABASE_MAX_OVERFLOW,
            pool_recycle=self.settings.DATABASE_POOL_RECYCLE,
            pool_pre_ping=True,  # Verify connections before using
            connect_args={
                "connect_timeout": self.settings.DATABASE_TIMEOUT,
                "application_name": "diyapp_v12"
            }
        )
        
        # Add event listeners for connection management
        @event.listens_for(engine, "connect")
        def connect(dbapi_connection, connection_record):
            logger.debug("New database connection established")
        
        @event.listens_for(engine, "checkout")
        def checkout(dbapi_connection, connection_record, connection_proxy):
            logger.debug("Database connection checked out from pool")
        
        return engine
    
    @contextmanager
    def get_db(self) -> Generator[Session, None, None]:
        """Dependency for FastAPI to get database session"""
        db = self.SessionLocal()
        try:
            yield db
            db.commit()
        except Exception as e:
            db.rollback()
            logger.error(f"Database session error: {str(e)}")
            raise
        finally:
            db.close()
    
    def health_check(self) -> bool:
        """Check database connectivity"""
        try:
            with self.engine.connect() as conn:
                conn.execute("SELECT 1")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Database health check failed: {str(e)}")
            return False

# Global database instance
database = Database()

# 6. SERVIÇOS EXTERNOS COM RESILIÊNCIA - src/services/external/payment_service.py
import httpx
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
import logging
from ..circuit_breaker import CircuitBreakerRegistry
from ..retry_policy import RetryPolicyRegistry
from ...core.config import get_settings

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class PaymentService:
    def __init__(self):
        self.settings = get_settings()
        self.base_url = self.settings.PAYMENT_SERVICE_URL
        self.timeout = self.settings.PAYMENT_SERVICE_TIMEOUT
        
        # Circuit breaker for payment service
        self.circuit_breaker = CircuitBreakerRegistry.get_breaker(
            name="payment_service",
            fallback_func=self._payment_fallback
        )
        
        # Retry policy for transient failures
        self.retry_policy = RetryPolicyRegistry.get_policy(
            name="payment_service",
            retry_on_exceptions=(httpx.TimeoutException, httpx.NetworkError)
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def _payment_fallback(*args, **kwargs) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Fallback when payment service is unavailable"""
        logger.warning("Payment service unavailable, using fallback")
        return {
            "status": "pending",
            "message": "Payment processing delayed due to service issues",
            "fallback": True
        }
    
    @circuit_breaker
    @retry_policy
    async def process_payment(
        self,
        amount: float,
        currency: str,
        user_id: str,
        metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Process payment with circuit breaker and retry policy"""
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=self.timeout) as client:
            payload = {
                "amount": amount,
                "currency": currency,
                "

```typescript
// src/components/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { Spinner } from '../Spinner/Spinner';
import { useButtonStyles } from './useButtonStyles';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  loadingText?: string;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

export const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      isLoading = false,
      loadingText,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      fullWidth = false,
      disabled,
      className,
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const styles = useButtonStyles({ variant, size, fullWidth, disabled: disabled || isLoading });
    const isDisabled = disabled || isLoading;

    return (
      <button
        ref={ref}
        className={`${styles.base} ${className || ''}`}
        disabled={isDisabled}
        aria-disabled={isDisabled}
        aria-busy={isLoading}
        {...props}
      >
        {isLoading && (
          <span className={styles.spinnerContainer}>
            <Spinner size={size === 'sm' ? 'xs' : 'sm'} />
          </span>
        )}
        
        {!isLoading && leftIcon && (
          <span className={styles.iconContainer} aria-hidden="true">
            {leftIcon}
          </span>
        )}
        
        <span className={styles.textContainer}>
          {isLoading && loadingText ? loadingText : children}
        </span>
        
        {!isLoading && rightIcon && (
          <span className={styles.iconContainer} aria-hidden="true">
            {rightIcon}
          </span>
        )}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';
```

```typescript
// src/components/Button/useButtonStyles.ts
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { ButtonVariant, ButtonSize } from './Button';

interface UseButtonStylesProps {
  variant: ButtonVariant;
  size: ButtonSize;
  fullWidth: boolean;
  disabled: boolean;
}

export const useButtonStyles = ({
  variant,
  size,
  fullWidth,
  disabled,
}: UseButtonStylesProps) => {
  const baseStyles = `
    inline-flex items-center justify-center
    font-medium rounded-md
    transition-all duration-200
    focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2
    disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed
    ${fullWidth ? 'w-full' : ''}
  `;

  const variantStyles = {
    primary: `
      bg-${tokens.colors.primary[600]}
      text-white
      hover:bg-${tokens.colors.primary[700]}
      focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}
      active:bg-${tokens.colors.primary[700]}
    `,
    secondary: `
      bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}
      text-${tokens.colors.neutral[800]}
      hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}
      focus:ring-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}
      active:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}
    `,
    outline: `
      border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}
      bg-transparent
      text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]}
      hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[50]}
      focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}
      active:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]}
    `,
    ghost: `
      bg-transparent
      text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]}
      hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]}
      focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}
      active:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}
    `,
    danger: `
      bg-${tokens.colors.error[500]}
      text-white
      hover:bg-${tokens.colors.error[600]}
      focus:ring-${tokens.colors.error[500]}
      active:bg-${tokens.colors.error[600]}
    `,
  }[variant];

  const sizeStyles = {
    sm: `
      px-${tokens.spacing.sm}
      py-${tokens.spacing.xs}
      text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm}
      gap-${tokens.spacing.xs}
    `,
    md: `
      px-${tokens.spacing.md}
      py-${tokens.spacing.sm}
      text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.base}
      gap-${tokens.spacing.sm}
    `,
    lg: `
      px-${tokens.spacing.lg}
      py-${tokens.spacing.md}
      text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.lg}
      gap-${tokens.spacing.md}
    `,
  }[size];

  const spinnerContainer = `
    flex items-center
    ${size === 'sm' ? 'mr-1' : 'mr-2'}
  `;

  const iconContainer = `
    flex items-center
    ${size === 'sm' ? 'text-sm' : 'text-base'}
  `;

  const textContainer = `
    whitespace-nowrap
  `;

  return {
    base: `${baseStyles} ${variantStyles} ${sizeStyles}`,
    spinnerContainer,
    iconContainer,
    textContainer,
  };
};
```

```typescript
// src/components/Spinner/Spinner.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export type SpinnerSize = 'xs' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface SpinnerProps {
  size?: SpinnerSize;
  className?: string;
  label?: string;
}

export const Spinner: React.FC<SpinnerProps> = ({
  size = 'md',
  className = '',
  label = 'Loading...',
}) => {
  const sizeStyles = {
    xs: 'w-3 h-3 border-2',
    sm: 'w-4 h-4 border-2',
    md: 'w-6 h-6 border-3',
    lg: 'w-8 h-8 border-4',
  }[size];

  return (
    <div className={`inline-flex items-center ${className}`} role="status">
      <div
        className={`${sizeStyles} rounded-full border-t-transparent border-${tokens.colors.primary[500]} animate-spin`}
        aria-hidden="true"
      />
      {label && (
        <span className="sr-only">{label}</span>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};
```

```typescript
// src/components/Card/Card.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, HTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export interface CardProps extends HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  variant?: 'elevated' | 'outline' | 'filled';
  padding?: 'none' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  hoverable?: boolean;
}

export const Card = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, CardProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'elevated',
      padding = 'md',
      hoverable = false,
      className = '',
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const variantStyles = {
      elevated: `
        bg-white
        shadow-${tokens.shadows.md}
        border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}
      `,
      outline: `
        bg-transparent
        border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}
      `,
      filled: `
        bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[50]}
        border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}
      `,
    }[variant];

    const paddingStyles = {
      none: '',
      sm: `p-${tokens.spacing.sm}`,
      md: `p-${tokens.spacing.md}`,
      lg: `p-${tokens.spacing.lg}`,
    }[padding];

    const hoverStyles = hoverable
      ? `transition-all duration-200 hover:shadow-${tokens.shadows.lg} hover:-translate-y-0.5`
      : '';

    return (
      <div
        ref={ref}
        className={`
          rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.lg}
          ${variantStyles}
          ${paddingStyles}
          ${hoverStyles}
          ${className}
        `}
        {...props}
      >
        {children}
      </div>
    );
  }
);

Card.displayName = 'Card';
```

```typescript
// src/components/Input/Input.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, InputHTMLAttributes, useState } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export interface InputProps extends InputHTMLAttributes<HTMLInputElement> {
  label?: string;
  error?: string;
  helperText?: string;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

export const Input = forwardRef<HTMLInputElement, InputProps>(
  (
    {
      label,
      error,
      helperText,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      fullWidth = true,
      className = '',
      disabled,
      required,
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const [isFocused, setIsFocused] = useState(false);

    const baseStyles = `
      block
      rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.md}
      border
      ${fullWidth ? 'w-full' : ''}
      ${tokens.typography.fontSize.base}
      transition-all duration-200
      focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-0
      disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed
    `;

    const borderColor = error
      ? `border-${tokens.colors.error[500]} focus:ring-${tokens.colors.error[500]}`
      : isFocused
      ? `border-${tokens.colors.primary[500]} focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`
      : `border-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]} focus:border-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`;

    const inputStyles = `
      ${baseStyles}
      ${borderColor}
      ${leftIcon ? 'pl-10' : 'pl-3'}
      ${rightIcon ? 'pr-10' : 'pr-3'}
      py-2
      ${className}
    `;

    return (
      <div className={`${fullWidth ? 'w-full' : ''}`}>
        {label && (
          <label
            htmlFor={props.id}
            className={`
              block mb-1
              text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm}
              font-${tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium}
              text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]}
              ${error ? `text-${tokens.colors.error[600]}` : ''}
            `}
          >
            {label}
            {required && (
              <span className={`ml-1 text-${tokens.colors.error[500]}`}>*</span>
            )}
          </label>
        )}
        
        <div className="relative">
          {leftIcon && (
            <div
              className={`
                absolute left-3 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2
                ${error ? `text-${tokens.colors.error[500]}` : `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}`}
                ${disabled ? 'opacity-50' : ''}
              `}
              aria-hidden="true"
            >
              {leftIcon}
            </div>
          )}
          
          <input
            ref={ref}
            className={inputStyles}
            disabled={disabled}
            required={required}
            aria-invalid={!!error}
            aria-describedby={
              error ? `${props.id}-error` : helperText ? `${props.id}-helper` : undefined
            }
            onFocus={() => setIsFocused(true)}
            onBlur={() => setIsFocused(false)}
            {...props}
          />
          
          {rightIcon && (
            <div
              className={`
                absolute right-3 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2
                ${error ? `text-${tokens.colors.error[500]}` : `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}`}
                ${disabled ? 'opacity-50' : ''}
              `}
              aria-hidden="true"
            >
              {rightIcon}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        {(error || helperText) && (
          <p
            id={error ? `${props.id}-error` : `${props.id}-helper`}
            className={`
              mt-1
              text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm}
              ${error ? `text-${tokens.colors.error[600]}` : `text-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}`}
            `}
          >
            {error || helperText}
          </p>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  }
);

Input.displayName = 'Input';
```

```typescript
// src/components/Modal/Modal.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { createPortal } from 'react-dom';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { Button } from '../Button/Button';

export interface ModalProps {
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  title?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl';
  showCloseButton?: boolean;
  footer?: React.ReactNode;
  closeOnEsc?: boolean;
  closeOnOverlayClick?: boolean;
}

export const Modal: React.FC<ModalProps> = ({
  isOpen,
  onClose,
  title,
  children,
  size = 'md',
  showCloseButton = true,
  footer,
  closeOnEsc = true,
  closeOnOverlayClick = true,
}) => {
  const handleKeyDown = useCallback(
    (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (closeOnEsc && e.key === 'Escape') {
        onClose();
      }
    },
    [closeOnEsc, onClose]
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isOpen && closeOnEsc) {
      document.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';

{
  "name": "diyapp-v12-telemetry",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "Sistema de telemetria e analytics para DIYAPP V12",

  "scripts": {
    "start": "node src/ingestion/telemetry_collector.js",
    "test": "jest",
    "dbt:run": "dbt run",
    "dbt:test": "dbt test",
    "dbt:docs": "dbt docs generate && dbt docs serve",

      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp

      - "5432:5432"

    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor

      - "8080:8080"
    volumes:
      - ./src/pipelines/airflow_dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./config:/opt/airflow/config
    depends_on:
      - postgres

      - "3000:3000"

      MB_DB_TYPE: postgres
      MB_DB_DBNAME: metabase

      MB_DB_HOST: postgres
      MB_DB_USER: metabase

      - postgres

volumes:
  postgres_data:

## 2. Esquema de Banco de Dados

### scripts/setup_database.sql
```sql
-- Database: diyapp_telemetry
CREATE DATABASE diyapp_telemetry;

-- Schema para dados brutos (raw/bronze)
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS raw;

-- Schema para dados processados (staging/silver)
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS staging;

-- Schema para dados analíticos (marts/gold)
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS product;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS ai;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS ops;

-- Tabelas RAW (bronze layer)
CREATE TABLE raw.telemetry_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    event_type VARCHAR(100),
    event_name VARCHAR(200),
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    properties JSONB,
    device_info JSONB,
    app_version VARCHAR(50),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    source_system VARCHAR(100),
    raw_data JSONB
);

CREATE TABLE raw.error_events (
    error_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    error_code VARCHAR(100),
    error_message TEXT,
    stack_trace TEXT,
    component VARCHAR(200),
    severity VARCHAR(50),
    environment VARCHAR(50),
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    metadata JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE raw.performance_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    metric_name VARCHAR(200),
    metric_value DECIMAL(15,4),
    metric_unit VARCHAR(50),
    component VARCHAR(200),
    operation VARCHAR(200),
    duration_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    tags JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE raw.llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    model_name VARCHAR(200),
    provider VARCHAR(100),
    feature_name VARCHAR(200),
    input_tokens INTEGER,
    output_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN,
    error_message TEXT,
    request_metadata JSONB,
    response_metadata JSONB,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Índices para performance
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_telemetry_timestamp ON raw.telemetry_events(event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_telemetry_user ON raw.telemetry_events(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_telemetry_event_type ON raw.telemetry_events(event_type);

CREATE INDEX idx_raw_error_timestamp ON raw.error_events(event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_error_severity ON raw.error_events(severity);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_error_component ON raw.error_events(component);

CREATE INDEX idx_raw_perf_timestamp ON raw.performance_metrics(event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_perf_metric_name ON raw.performance_metrics(metric_name);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_perf_component ON raw.performance_metrics(component);

CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_timestamp ON raw.llm_calls(event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_feature ON raw.llm_calls(feature_name);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_model ON raw.llm_calls(model_name);
```

## 3. Configuração dbt

### dbt_project.yml
```yaml
name: 'diyapp_telemetry'
version: '1.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: 'diyapp_telemetry'

model-paths: ["src/pipelines/dbt/models"]
test-paths: ["src/pipelines/dbt/tests"]
macro-paths: ["src/pipelines/dbt/macros"]
analysis-paths: ["src/pipelines/dbt/analyses"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_telemetry:
    materialized: table
    staging:
      materialized: view
      schema: staging
      tags: ['staging']
    product:
      materialized: table
      schema: product
      tags: ['product', 'marts']
    ai:
      materialized: table
      schema: ai
      tags: ['ai', 'marts']
    ops:
      materialized: table
      schema: ops
      tags: ['ops', 'marts']

tests:
  diyapp_telemetry:
    data_quality:
      tags: ['data_quality']
    integration:
      tags: ['integration']

seeds:
  diyapp_telemetry:
    enabled: false

vars:
  retention_days: 90
  timezone: 'UTC'
```

version: 2

models:
  - name: stg_telemetry_events
    description: "Eventos de telemetria limpos e padronizados"
    columns:

        description: "ID único do evento"

### src/pipelines/dbt/models/staging/stg_telemetry_events.sql
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging',
        tags=['staging', 'telemetry']
    )
}}

WITH source AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        session_id,
        -- Anonimiza user_id mantendo consistência
        {{ hash_field('user_id') }} as user_id,
        LOWER(event_type) as event_type,
        TRIM(event_name) as event_name,
        event_timestamp,
        -- Valida e limpa propriedades JSON
        CASE 
            WHEN properties IS NULL THEN '{}'::JSONB
            ELSE properties
        END as properties,
        -- Extrai app_version do device_info ou usa padrão
        COALESCE(
            device_info->>'app_version',
            app_version,
            'unknown'
        ) as app_version,
        created_at,
        source_system
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'telemetry_events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '{{ var("retention_days") }} days'
),

cleaned AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        session_id,
        user_id,
        event_type,
        event_name,
        -- Garante timestamp em UTC
        (event_timestamp AT TIME ZONE 'UTC') as event_timestamp,
        properties,
        app_version,
        created_at,
        source_system,
        CURRENT_TIMESTAMP as processed_at
    FROM source
    -- Remove eventos inválidos
    WHERE event_id IS NOT NULL
      AND session_id IS NOT NULL
      AND event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND event_timestamp <= CURRENT_TIMESTAMP + INTERVAL '5 minutes' -- Não aceita eventos futuros
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned
```

### src/pipelines/dbt/models/staging/stg_error_events.sql
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging',
        tags=['staging', 'errors']
    )
}}

WITH source AS (
    SELECT
        error_id,
        session_id,
        {{ hash_field('user_id') }} as user_id,
        UPPER(error_code) as error_code,
        LEFT(error_message, 1000) as error_message, -- Limita tamanho
        LEFT(stack_trace

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infraestrutura como Código (Terraform)

Vou criar uma infraestrutura completa com Terraform para ambientes de dev, staging e produção, incluindo monitoramento e auto-scaling. A arquitetura será modular e seguirá as melhores práticas de SRE.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
terraform/
├── environments/
│   ├── dev/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── variables.tf
│   │   └── terraform.tfvars
│   ├── staging/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── variables.tf
│   │   └── terraform.tfvars
│   └── production/
│       ├── main.tf
│       ├── variables.tf
│       └── terraform.tfvars
├── modules/
│   ├── vpc/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── variables.tf
│   │   └── outputs.tf
│   ├── ecs/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── variables.tf
│   │   └── outputs.tf
│   ├── rds/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── variables.tf
│   │   └── outputs.tf
│   ├── monitoring/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── variables.tf
│   │   └── outputs.tf
│   └── autoscaling/
│       ├── main.tf
│       ├── variables.tf
│       └── outputs.tf
├── providers.tf
├── backend.tf
└── versions.tf
```

## 1. Configuração Principal

### `terraform/providers.tf`
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    grafana = {
      source  = "grafana/grafana"
      version = "~> 2.0"
    }
    datadog = {
      source  = "DataDog/datadog"
      version = "~> 3.0"
    }
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V12"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

provider "grafana" {
  url  = var.grafana_url
  auth = var.grafana_auth
}

provider "datadog" {
  api_key = var.datadog_api_key
  app_key = var.datadog_app_key
  api_url = "https://api.datadoghq.eu/"
}
```

```hcl
resource "aws_vpc" "main" {
  cidr_block           = var.vpc_cidr
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-vpc"
  }
}

resource "aws_internet_gateway" "main" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-igw"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "public" {
  count                   = length(var.public_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id                  = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block              = var.public_subnet_cidrs[count.index]
  availability_zone       = var.availability_zones[count.index % length(var.availability_zones)]
  map_public_ip_on_launch = true
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-public-${count.index}"
    Type = "Public"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "private" {
  count             = length(var.private_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = var.private_subnet_cidrs[count.index]
  availability_zone = var.availability_zones[count.index % length(var.availability_zones)]
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-private-${count.index}"
    Type = "Private"
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table" "public" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block = "0.0.0.0/0"
    gateway_id = aws_internet_gateway.main.id
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-public-rt"
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "public" {
  count          = length(aws_subnet.public)
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.public.id
}

resource "aws_eip" "nat" {
  count = var.enable_nat_gateway ? 1 : 0
  domain = "vpc"
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-nat-eip"
  }
}

resource "aws_nat_gateway" "main" {
  count         = var.enable_nat_gateway ? 1 : 0
  allocation_id = aws_eip.nat[0].id
  subnet_id     = aws_subnet.public[0].id
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-nat-gw"
  }
  
  depends_on = [aws_internet_gateway.main]
}

resource "aws_route_table" "private" {
  count  = var.enable_nat_gateway ? 1 : 0
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block     = "0.0.0.0/0"
    nat_gateway_id = aws_nat_gateway.main[0].id
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-private-rt"
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "private" {
  count          = var.enable_nat_gateway ? length(aws_subnet.private) : 0
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.private[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.private[0].id
}

resource "aws_security_group" "alb" {
  name        = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-alb-sg"
  description = "Security group for ALB"
  vpc_id      = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  ingress {
    description = "HTTP from anywhere"
    from_port   = 80
    to_port     = 80
    protocol    = "tcp"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  ingress {
    description = "HTTPS from anywhere"
    from_port   = 443
    to_port     = 443
    protocol    = "tcp"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  egress {
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    protocol    = "-1"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-alb-sg"
  }
}

resource "aws_security_group" "ecs" {
  name        = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-sg"
  description = "Security group for ECS tasks"
  vpc_id      = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  ingress {
    description     = "From ALB"
    from_port       = var.container_port
    to_port         = var.container_port
    protocol        = "tcp"
    security_groups = [aws_security_group.alb.id]
  }
  
  egress {
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    protocol    = "-1"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-sg"
  }
}
```

  type        = string
}

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment (dev, staging, production)"
  type        = string
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "CIDR block for VPC"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "public_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "List of public subnet CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24"]
}

variable "private_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "List of private subnet CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24"]
}

variable "availability_zones" {
  description = "List of availability zones"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["us-east-1a", "us-east-1b"]
}

variable "enable_nat_gateway" {
  description = "Enable NAT Gateway"
  type        = bool
  default     = true
}

variable "container_port" {
  description = "Container port for ECS tasks"
  type        = number
  default     = 3000
}
```

  network_mode             = "awsvpc"

  cpu                      = var.task_cpu
  memory                   = var.task_memory

        interval    = 30
        timeout     = 5
        retries     = 3
        startPeriod = 60
      }
    }
  ])
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-task-definition"
  }
}

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Threat Modeling e Reforço de Segurança

## 1. Análise de Threat Modeling (STRIDE) para V12

### Ativos Críticos Identificados:
1. **Dados de Usuário**: Credenciais, tokens de sessão, dados pessoais
2. **Sistema de Autenticação**: JWT, OAuth, MFA
3. **APIs de IA/LLM**: Endpoints de processamento de prompts
4. **Banco de Dados**: PostgreSQL com dados sensíveis
5. **Sistema de Arquivos**: Uploads de usuários
6. **Integrações Externas**: WhatsApp, APIs de terceiros

### Ameaças por Categoria STRIDE:

#### **Spoofing (Falsificação)**
- **A1**: Token JWT roubado/reutilizado
- **A2**: Credenciais fracas ou reutilizadas
- **A3**: Ataque de session fixation
- **Controles Implementados**:
  - JWT com expiração curta (15min access, 7d refresh)
  - MFA obrigatório para admin
  - Rate limiting em login (5 tentativas/15min)
  - Invalidação de sessão em logout

#### **Tampering (Manipulação)**
- **A4**: SQL Injection em queries
- **A5**: Manipulação de parâmetros de URL/body
- **A6**: Upload de arquivos maliciosos
- **Controles Implementados**:
  - Prepared statements com TypeORM
  - Validação de schema Zod em todas as entradas
  - Sanitização de uploads (extensões, tamanho, tipo MIME)

#### **Repudiation (Repúdio)**
- **A7**: Usuário nega ação realizada
- **A8**: Logs insuficientes para auditoria
- **Controles Implementados**:
  - Logs imutáveis de operações críticas
  - Timestamp + ID de usuário em todas as ações
  - Auditoria de mudanças em dados sensíveis

#### **Information Disclosure (Divulgação)**
- **A9**: Vazamento de dados via erro messages
- **A10**: Exposição de dados em cache/logs
- **A11**: Prompt injection em LLMs
- **Controles Implementados**:
  - Mascaramento de dados sensíveis em logs
  - Criptografia AES-256 para PII em repouso
  - Content Security Policy no frontend
  - Sanitização de outputs de LLM

#### **Denial of Service (Negação)**
- **A12**: Ataque DDoS em APIs públicas
- **A13**: Resource exhaustion via uploads grandes
- **Controles Implementados**:
  - Rate limiting por IP/usuário
  - Timeouts configurados
  - Circuit breakers em integrações externas
  - WAF básico com regras de bloqueio

#### **Elevation of Privilege (Elevação)**
- **A14**: IDOR (Insecure Direct Object Reference)
- **A15**: Bypass de autorização
- **Controles Implementados**:
  - RBAC com verificação por recurso
  - Princípio do menor privilégio
  - Validação de ownership antes de operações

## 2. Implementação de Segurança V12

### Estrutura do Projeto:
```
src/
├── security/
│   ├── auth/
│   │   ├── jwt.strategy.ts
│   │   ├── mfa.service.ts
│   │   └── session.manager.ts
│   ├── validation/

│   │   ├── sanitizer.ts
│   │   └── llm.guardrails.ts
│   ├── waf/
│   │   ├── waf.middleware.ts
│   │   ├── rate.limiter.ts
│   │   └── ddos.protection.ts
│   └── encryption/

│       └── key.manager.ts
├── logs/
│   └── security.audit.ts

```

### 2.1 Configuração de Segurança Principal

**src/config/security.config.ts**
```typescript
import * as crypto from 'crypto';

export const SecurityConfig = {
  // JWT Configuration
  JWT: {
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRY: '15m',
    REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRY: '7d',
    SECRET: process.env.JWT_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex'),
    ALGORITHM: 'HS256'
  },
  
  // Rate Limiting
  RATE_LIMIT: {
    LOGIN: { windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, max: 5 }, // 5 tentativas em 15min
    API: { windowMs: 60 * 1000, max: 100 }, // 100 requests/min
    UPLOAD: { windowMs: 60 * 1000, max: 10 } // 10 uploads/min
  },
  
  // Encryption
  ENCRYPTION: {
    ALGORITHM: 'aes-256-gcm',
    IV_LENGTH: 16,
    SALT_LENGTH: 64,
    ITERATIONS: 100000
  },
  
  // WAF Rules
  WAF_RULES: {
    BLOCKED_PATTERNS: [
      /(\%27)|(\')|(\-\-)|(\%23)|(#)/gi, // SQL Injection
      /((\%3D)|(=))[^\n]*((\%27)|(\')|(\-\-)|(\%3B)|(;))/gi,
      /\w*((\%27)|(\'))((\%6F)|o|(\%4F))((\%72)|r|(\%52))/gi,
      /((\%27)|(\'))union/gi,
      /<script\b[^<]*(?:(?!<\/script>)<[^<]*)*<\/script>/gi, // XSS
      /javascript:/gi,
      /on\w+\s*=/gi,
      /<iframe/gi,
      /<object/gi,
      /<embed/gi
    ],
    MAX_BODY_SIZE: '10mb',
    MAX_URL_LENGTH: 2048
  },
  
  // LLM Security
  LLM_GUARDRAILS: {
    MAX_PROMPT_LENGTH: 4000,
    BLOCKED_KEYWORDS: [
      'system', 'root', 'admin', 'password', 'token', 'key',
      'execute', 'eval', 'require', 'import', 'fs.', 'process.'
    ],
    SANITIZE_OUTPUT: true
  },
  
  // Session Security
  SESSION: {
    COOKIE_SECURE: true,
    COOKIE_HTTPONLY: true,
    COOKIE_SAMESITE: 'strict',
    SESSION_TIMEOUT: 30 * 60 * 1000 // 30 minutos
  }
};
```

### 2.2 WAF e Proteção DDoS

**src/security/waf/waf.middleware.ts**
```typescript
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { SecurityConfig } from '../../config/security.config';
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
import slowDown from 'express-slow-down';

export class WAFMiddleware {
  private static instance: WAFMiddleware;
  private blockedIPs: Map<string, number> = new Map();
  
  static getInstance(): WAFMiddleware {
    if (!WAFMiddleware.instance) {
      WAFMiddleware.instance = new WAFMiddleware();
    }
    return WAFMiddleware.instance;
  }
  
  // Rate Limiter para login
  static loginLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: SecurityConfig.RATE_LIMIT.LOGIN.windowMs,
    max: SecurityConfig.RATE_LIMIT.LOGIN.max,
    message: { error: 'Muitas tentativas de login. Tente novamente em 15 minutos.' },
    standardHeaders: true,
    legacyHeaders: false
  });
  
  // Rate Limiter para API geral
  static apiLimiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: SecurityConfig.RATE_LIMIT.API.windowMs,
    max: SecurityConfig.RATE_LIMIT.API.max,
    message: { error: 'Muitas requisições. Por favor, aguarde.' },
    standardHeaders: true,
    legacyHeaders: false
  });
  
  // Slow down para prevenir DDoS
  static speedLimiter = slowDown({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
    delayAfter: 100,
    delayMs: (hits) => hits * 100 // Aumenta delay conforme hits
  });
  
  // Middleware principal do WAF
  static wafCheck(req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): void {
    const waf = WAFMiddleware.getInstance();
    
    // Verifica IP bloqueado
    const clientIP = req.ip || req.socket.remoteAddress || '';
    if (waf.isIPBlocked(clientIP)) {
      res.status(403).json({ error: 'Acesso bloqueado por segurança' });
      return;
    }
    
    // Verifica padrões maliciosos na URL
    if (waf.hasMaliciousPatterns(req.url)) {
      waf.blockIP(clientIP, 3600000); // Bloqueia por 1 hora
      res.status(403).json({ error: 'Requisição bloqueada por segurança' });
      return;
    }
    
    // Verifica padrões maliciosos no body (se existir)
    if (req.body && typeof req.body === 'object') {
      const bodyString = JSON.stringify(req.body);
      if (waf.hasMaliciousPatterns(bodyString)) {
        waf.blockIP(clientIP, 3600000);
        res.status(403).json({ error: 'Dados maliciosos detectados' });
        return;
      }
    }
    
    // Verifica tamanho do body
    const contentLength = parseInt(req.headers['content-length'] || '0');
    if (contentLength > 10 * 1024 * 1024) { // 10MB
      res.status(413).json({ error: 'Payload muito grande' });
      return;
    }
    
    next();
  }
  
  private isIPBlocked(ip: string): boolean {
    const blockTime = this.blockedIPs.get(ip);
    if (!blockTime) return false;
    
    // Remove bloqueio se expirado
    if (Date.now() > blockTime) {
      this.blockedIPs.delete(ip);
      return false;
    }
    
    return true;
  }
  
  private blockIP(ip: string, durationMs: number): void {
    this.blockedIPs.set(ip, Date.now() + durationMs);
    console.warn(`[WAF] IP ${ip} bloqueado por ${durationMs/1000} segundos`);
  }
  
  private hasMaliciousPatterns(input: string): boolean {
    for (const pattern of SecurityConfig.WAF_RULES.BLOCKED_PATTERNS) {
      if (pattern.test(input)) {
        console.warn(`[WAF] Padrão malicioso detectado: ${pattern}`);
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
}
```

### 2.3 Sistema de Autenticação Reforçada

**src/security/auth/jwt.strategy.ts**
```typescript
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PassportStrategy } from '@nestjs/passport';
import { ExtractJwt, Strategy } from 'passport-jwt';
import { SecurityConfig } from '../../config/security.config';
import { AuthService } from './auth.service';

@Injectable()
export class JwtStrategy extends PassportStrategy(Strategy) {
  constructor(private authService: AuthService) {
    super({
      jwtFromRequest: ExtractJwt.fromExtractors([
        ExtractJwt.fromAuthHeaderAsBearerToken(),
        (req) => req.cookies?.access_token
      ]),
      ignoreExpiration: false,
      secretOrKey: SecurityConfig.JWT.SECRET,
      passReqToCallback: true
    });
  }
  
  async validate(req: Request, payload: any) {
    // Verifica se o token está na blacklist
    const token = ExtractJwt.fromAuthHeaderAsBearerToken()(req as any);
    if (await this.authService.isTokenBlacklisted(token)) {
      throw new Error('Token inválido');
    }
    
    // Verifica se o usuário ainda existe e está ativo
    const user = await this.authService.validateUser(payload.sub);
    if (!user || !user.isActive) {
      throw new Error('Usuário não encontrado ou inativo');
    }
    
    // Registra auditoria de acesso
    await this.authService.logAccess({
      userId: user.id,
      ip: (req as any).ip,
      userAgent: (req as any).headers['user-agent'],
      timestamp: new Date()
    });
    
    return {
      id: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      roles: user.roles,
      mfaEnabled: user.mfaEnabled
    };
  }
}
```

**src/security/auth/mfa.service.ts**
```typescript
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import * as speakeasy from 'speakeasy';
import * as QRCode from 'qrcode';
import { SecurityAudit } from '../../logs/security.audit';

@Injectable()
export class MFAService {
  private readonly issuer = 'DIYAPP V12';
  
  async generateSecret(userId: string, email: string) {
    const secret = speakeasy.generateSecret({
      name: `${this.issuer}:${email}`,
      issuer: this.issuer,
      length: 20
    });
    
    // Gera QR Code
    const qrCodeUrl = await QRCode.toDataURL(secret.otpauth_url);
    
    // Registra auditoria
    SecurityAudit.log({
      userId,
      action: 'MFA_SECRET_GENERATED',
      resource: `user:${userId}`,
      metadata: { method: 'TOTP' },
      timestamp: new Date()
    });
    
    return {
      secret: secret.base32,
      qrCode: qrCodeUrl,
      otpauthUrl: secret.otpauth_url
    };
  }
  
  async verifyToken(secret: string, token: string): Promise<boolean> {
    return speakeasy.totp.verify({
      secret,
      encoding: 'base32',
      token,
      window: 1 // Permite 30 segundos de tolerância
    });
  }
  
  async enableMFA(userId: string, secret: string, token: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const isValid = await this.verifyToken(secret, token);
    
    if (isValid) {
      SecurityAudit.log({
        userId,
        action: 'MFA_ENABLED',
        resource: `user:${userId}`,
        metadata: { method: 'TOTP' },
        timestamp: new Date()
      });
    } else {
      SecurityAudit.log({
        userId,
        action: 'MFA_ENABLE_FAILED',
        resource: `user:${userId}`,
        metadata: { reason: 'invalid_token' },
        timestamp: new Date()
      });
    }
    
    return isValid;
  }
}
```

### 2.4 Validação e Sanitização de Inputs

**src/security/validation/input.schemas.ts**
```typescript
import { z } from 'zod';

export const UserSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email('Email inválido'),
  password: z.string()
    .min(8, 'Senha deve ter no mínimo 8 caracteres')
    .regex(/[A-Z]/, 'Deve conter pelo menos uma letra maiúscula')
    .regex(/[a-z]/, 'Deve conter pelo menos uma letra minúscula')
    .regex(/[0-9]/, 'Deve conter pelo menos um número')
    .regex(/[^A-Za-z0-9]/, 'Deve conter pelo menos um caractere especial'),
  name: z.string().min(2, 'Nome muito curto').max(100, 'Nome muito longo'),
  phone: z.string().regex(/^\+?[1-9]\d{1,14}$/, 'Número de telefone inválido')
});

export const LLMPromptSchema = z.object({
  prompt: z.string()
    .min(1, 'Prompt não pode ser vazio')
    .max(4000, 'Prompt muito longo')
    .refine((val) => !/(system|root|admin|password|token|key|execute|eval|require|import|fs\.|process\.)/gi.test(val), {
      message: 'Prompt contém palavras-chave bloqueadas'
    }),
  context: z.record(z.any()).optional(),
  options: z.object({
    temperature: z.number().min(0).max(2).default(0.7),
    maxTokens: z.number().min(1).max(4000).default(1000)
  }).optional()
});

export const FileUploadSchema = z.object({
  fieldname: z.string(),
  originalname: z.string(),
  encoding: z.string(),
  mimetype: z.string()
    .refine((val) => 
      ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/gif', 'application/pdf', 'text/plain'].includes(val),
      { message: 'Tipo de arquivo não permitido' }
    ),
  size: z.number()
    .max(5 * 1024 * 1024, 'Arquivo muito grande (máximo 5MB)'),
  buffer: z.instanceof(Buffer)
});

export const APISchema = {
  validate: <T>(schema: z.ZodSchema<T>, data: unknown): T => {
    try {
      return schema.parse(data);
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof z.ZodError) {
        throw new Error(`Validation failed: ${error.errors.map(e => `${e.path}: ${e.message}`).join(', ')}`);
      }
      throw error;
    }
  }
};
```
