### `tests/load/scripts/main.js`
```javascript
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep, group } from 'k6';
import { scenarios, thresholds } from '../config/scenarios.js';
import { generateTestData } from '../utils/data-generator.js';

// Configuração base
export const options = {
  scenarios: {
    smoke: scenarios.smoke,
    average: scenarios.average_load,
    stress: scenarios.stress
  },
  thresholds: thresholds,
  discardResponseBodies: false,
  userAgent: 'DIYAPP-k6-load-test/1.0'
};

// URL base da aplicação
const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000';

// Headers comuns
const headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'User-Agent': 'k6-load-test',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
};

// Token de autenticação (se necessário)
let authToken = null;

// Setup: Autenticação inicial
export function setup() {
  console.log('Starting load test setup...');
  
  // Login para obter token
  const loginRes = http.post(`${BASE_URL}/api/auth/login`, JSON.stringify({
    email: __ENV.TEST_USER || 'test@diyapp.com',
    password: __ENV.TEST_PASSWORD || 'test123'
  }), { headers: headers });
  
  if (loginRes.status === 200) {
    authToken = loginRes.json().token;
    headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${authToken}`;
    console.log('Authentication successful');
  } else {
    console.warn('Authentication failed, proceeding without token');
  }
  
  return { authToken };
}

// Funções de teste
export default function (data) {
  // Grupo 1: Testes de navegação básica
  group('Basic Navigation', () => {
    // Home page
    const homeRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/`, { headers });
    check(homeRes, {
      'home page status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'home page loaded within 2s': (r) => r.timings.duration < 2000
    });
    
    // Dashboard
    const dashboardRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/dashboard`, { headers });
    check(dashboardRes, {
      'dashboard status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'dashboard contains user data': (r) => r.body.includes('dashboard')
    });
    
    sleep(1);
  });
  
  // Grupo 2: Testes de API
  group('API Endpoints', () => {
    // GET requests
    const projectsRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/projects`, { headers });
    check(projectsRes, {
      'projects API status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'projects response time < 1s': (r) => r.timings.duration < 1000
    });
    
    // POST request com dados dinâmicos
    const testData = generateTestData();
    const createRes = http.post(`${BASE_URL}/api/projects`, JSON.stringify(testData), { headers });
    check(createRes, {
      'create project status 201': (r) => r.status === 201,
      'project created successfully': (r) => r.json().id !== undefined
    });
    
    // Se criação foi bem-sucedida, testar update e delete
    if (createRes.status === 201) {
      const projectId = createRes.json().id;
      
      // UPDATE
      const updateData = { ...testData, name: `Updated-${testData.name}` };
      const updateRes = http.put(`${BASE_URL}/api/projects/${projectId}`, JSON.stringify(updateData), { headers });
      check(updateRes, {
        'update project status 200': (r) => r.status === 200
      });
      
      // DELETE
      const deleteRes = http.del(`${BASE_URL}/api/projects/${projectId}`, null, { headers });
      check(deleteRes, {
        'delete project status 204': (r) => r.status === 204
      });
    }
    
    sleep(2);
  });
  
  // Grupo 3: Testes de upload e processamento
  group('File Operations', () => {
    // Upload de arquivo pequeno
    const smallFile = open('../fixtures/small-file.txt', 'b');
    const uploadRes = http.post(`${BASE_URL}/api/upload`, {
      file: http.file(smallFile, 'test.txt', 'text/plain')
    }, { headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'multipart/form-data' } });
    
    check(uploadRes, {
      'upload status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'upload response time < 3s': (r) => r.timings.duration < 3000
    });
    
    sleep(1);
  });
  
  // Grupo 4: Testes de busca e filtros
  group('Search Operations', () => {
    const searchRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/search?q=test&limit=10&offset=0`, { headers });
    check(searchRes, {
      'search status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'search returns results': (r) => r.json().results !== undefined
    });
    
    sleep(0.5);
  });
}

// Teardown: Limpeza
export function teardown(data) {
  console.log('Load test teardown...');
  // Limpar dados de teste se necessário
  if (data.authToken) {
    const logoutRes = http.post(`${BASE_URL}/api/auth/logout`, null, {
      headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${data.authToken}` }
    });
    check(logoutRes, { 'logout successful': (r) => r.status === 200 });
  }
}
```

// Gerador de dados de teste
export function generateTestData() {
  const timestamp = Date.now();
  const randomId = Math.random().toString(36).substring(7);
  
  return {
    name: `TestProject-${timestamp}-${randomId}`,
    description: `Automated test project generated at ${new Date().toISOString()}`,
    type: ['web', 'mobile', 'api'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)],
    priority: ['low', 'medium', 'high'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)],
    tags: ['test', 'automation', 'load-test'],
    metadata: {
      generatedBy: 'k6-load-test',
      timestamp: timestamp,
      iteration: __VU ? __VU : 0
    },
    content: {
      sections: Array.from({ length: Math.floor(Math.random() * 5) + 1 }, (_, i) => ({
        title: `Section ${i + 1}`,
        content: `Content for section ${i + 1} generated for load testing.`,
        order: i
      }))
    },
    settings: {
      public: Math.random() > 0.5,
      notifications: true,
      autoSave: true
    }
  };
}

// Gerador de usuários de teste
export function generateUserData() {
  const domains = ['test.com', 'example.org', 'diyapp.io'];
  const domain = domains[Math.floor(Math.random() * domains.length)];
  const randomStr = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 8);
  
  return {
    email: `user_${randomStr}@${domain}`,
    username: `testuser_${randomStr}`,
    password: `TestPass${randomStr}123!`,
    firstName: ['Test', 'Load', 'Performance', 'Stress'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)],
    lastName: ['User', 'Bot', 'Runner', 'Agent'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)],
    role: ['user', 'editor', 'viewer'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)]
  };
}

## 2. Testes de Segurança com OWASP ZAP

### `tests/security/zap-automation.js`
```javascript
const zap = require('zapv2');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const util = require('util');

const execPromise = util.promisify(exec);

class SecurityTester {
  constructor(config) {
    this.config = {
      zapHost: config.zapHost || 'localhost',
      zapPort: config.zapPort || 8080,
      targetUrl: config.targetUrl || 'http://localhost:3000',
      apiKey: config.apiKey || process.env.ZAP_API_KEY,
      reportDir: config.reportDir || './reports',
      scanPolicy: config.scanPolicy || 'Default Policy',
      contextName: config.contextName || 'DIYAPP-Security-Test'
    };
    
    this.zap = new zap({
      apiKey: this.config.apiKey,
      proxy: `http://${this.config.zapHost}:${this.config.zapPort}`
    });
    
    this.ensureDirectories();
  }
  
  ensureDirectories() {
    const dirs = [
      this.config.reportDir,
      `${this.config.reportDir}/scans`,
      `${this.config.reportDir}/policies`,
      `${this.config.reportDir}/exports`
    ];
    
    dirs.forEach(dir => {
      if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) {
        fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
      }
    });
  }
  
  async startZapDaemon() {
    console.log('Starting ZAP daemon...');
    
    try {
      // Verificar se ZAP já está rodando
      await this.zap.core.version();
      console.log('ZAP is already running');
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      console.log('Starting ZAP daemon process...');
      
      // Iniciar ZAP em modo daemon
      const zapCommand = `zap.sh -daemon -host ${this.config.zapHost} -port ${this.config.zapPort} -config api.key=${this.config.apiKey} -config api.addrs.addr.name=.* -config api.addrs.addr.regex=true`;
      
      try {
        const { stdout, stderr } = await execPromise(zapCommand, { 
          detached: true,
          stdio: 'ignore'
        });
        
        // Aguardar ZAP iniciar
        await this.waitForZap(30);
        console.log('ZAP daemon started successfully');
        return true;
      } catch (startError) {
        console.error('Failed to start ZAP daemon:', startError);
        return false;
      }
    }
  }
  
  async waitForZap(maxAttempts = 30) {
    for (let i = 0; i < maxAttempts; i++) {
      try {
        await this.zap.core.version();
        return true;
      } catch (error) {
        if (i === maxAttempts - 1) throw error;
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000));
      }
    }
  }
  
  async createContext() {
    console.log('Creating security context...');
    
    const contextId = await this.zap.context.newContext(this.config.contextName);
    
    // Adicionar URLs ao contexto
    await this.zap.context.includeInContext(this.config.contextName, `${this.config.targetUrl}.*`);
    
    // Configurar autenticação se necessário
    if (this.config.authConfig) {
      await this.setupAuthentication(contextId);
    }
    
    return contextId;
  }
  
  async setupAuthentication(contextId) {
    const { loginUrl, username, password, loggedInRegex } = this.config.authConfig;
    
    // Configurar autenticação baseada em formulário
    const authParams = `loginUrl=${encodeURIComponent(loginUrl)}&loginRequestData=username%3D%7B%25username%25%7D%26password%3D%7B%25password%25%7D`;
    
    await this.zap.authentication.setAuthenticationMethod(
      contextId,
      'formBasedAuthentication',
      authParams
    );
    
    await this.zap.authentication.setLoggedInIndicator(
      contextId,
      loggedInRegex
    );
    
    // Criar usuário para testes
    const userId = await this.zap.users.newUser(contextId, 'security-test-user');
    await this.zap.users.setAuthenticationCredentials(
      contextId,
      userId,
      `username=${username}&password=${password}`
    );
    
    await this.zap.users.setUserEnabled(contextId, userId, true);
    
    return userId;
  }
  
  async runSpider(contextId, userId = null) {
    console.log('Running spider...');
    
    let scanId;
    if (userId) {
      // Spider com autenticação
      scanId = await this.zap.spider.scanAsUser(
        this.config.targetUrl,
        contextId,
        userId,
        5, // maxChildren
        null, // recurse
        'true' // subtree only
      );
    } else {
      // Spider sem autenticação
      scanId = await this.zap.spider.scan(
        this.config.targetUrl,
        5, // maxChildren
        null, // contextId
        null, // subtree only
        null // recurse
      );
    }
    
    // Aguardar spider completar
    await this.wait

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
# AI Ops: Pipeline de MLOps com Observabilidade Estruturada
# Arquitetura: OpenTelemetry + LangSmith + Golden Dataset + Alertas Automáticos

"""
ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO:
├── src/
│   ├── ai_ops/
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── monitoring/
│   │   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   │   ├── cost_tracker.py      # Rastreamento de custo por provedor/feature
│   │   │   ├── quality_monitor.py   # Avaliação golden dataset + drift detection
│   │   │   ├── latency_tracker.py   # Latência P50/P95/P99 por provedor
│   │   │   └── anomaly_detector.py  # Detecção de anomalias de uso
│   │   ├── observability/
│   │   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   │   ├── opentelemetry_setup.py  # Config OpenTelemetry
│   │   │   ├── langsmith_integration.py # Integração LangSmith
│   │   │   └── metrics_exporter.py     # Export para Grafana/Prometheus
│   │   ├── alerts/
│   │   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   │   ├── alert_manager.py    # Gerenciador de alertas
│   │   │   ├── cost_alerts.py      # Alertas de custo >20%
│   │   │   ├── quality_alerts.py   # Alertas de drift ≥10%
│   │   │   └── latency_alerts.py   # Alertas de latência SLO
│   │   ├── reporting/
│   │   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   │   ├── weekly_report.py    # Relatório semanal automático
│   │   │   ├── experiment_tracker.py # Rastreamento de experimentos
│   │   │   └── dashboard_api.py    # API para dashboard
│   │   └── database/
│   │       ├── __init__.py
│   │       ├── models.py           # Modelos SQLAlchemy
│   │       ├── migrations/         # Alembic migrations
│   │       └── queries.py          # Queries otimizadas
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── __init__.py

```python
# src/ai_ops/monitoring/cost_tracker.py
"""
Rastreamento de custo de LLMs em produção por feature e por modelo
"""
import asyncio
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
from dataclasses import dataclass
from decimal import Decimal
import logging

from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from pydantic import BaseModel

from src.ai_ops.database.models import LLMCall, CostAlert
from src.utils.logger_setup import get_logger

logger = get_logger(__name__)

@dataclass
class ProviderPricing:
    """Preços por 1K tokens por provedor"""
    input_price: Decimal
    output_price: Decimal
    
PROVIDER_PRICING = {
    "openai:gpt-4": ProviderPricing(
        input_price=Decimal("0.03"),
        output_price=Decimal("0.06")
    ),
    "openai:gpt-3.5-turbo": ProviderPricing(
        input_price=Decimal("0.0015"),
        output_price=Decimal("0.002")
    ),
    "anthropic:claude-3-opus": ProviderPricing(
        input_price=Decimal("0.015"),
        output_price=Decimal("0.075")
    ),
    "anthropic:claude-3-sonnet": ProviderPricing(
        input_price=Decimal("0.003"),
        output_price=Decimal("0.015")
    ),
    "google:gemini-pro": ProviderPricing(
        input_price=Decimal("0.0005"),
        output_price=Decimal("0.0015")
    ),
}

class CostBreakdown(BaseModel):
    """Breakdown de custo por dimensão"""
    total_cost: Decimal
    by_provider: Dict[str, Decimal]
    by_feature: Dict[str, Decimal]
    by_model: Dict[str, Decimal]
    by_day: Dict[str, Decimal]

class CostTracker:
    """Monitor de custo para LLMs"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_session: Session):
        self.db = db_session
        self.expected_costs = self._load_expected_costs()
        
    def _load_expected_costs(self) -> Dict[str, Decimal]:
        """Carrega custos esperados do banco"""
        # Implementação simplificada
        return {
            "feature:chat": Decimal("100.00"),
            "feature:summarization": Decimal("50.00"),
            "feature:classification": Decimal("30.00"),
        }
    
    def calculate_call_cost(self, call: LLMCall) -> Decimal:
        """Calcula custo de uma chamada individual"""
        provider_key = f"{call.provider}:{call.model}"
        
        if provider_key not in PROVIDER_PRICING:
            logger.warning(f"Preço não encontrado para {provider_key}, usando fallback")
            return Decimal("0.01")  # Fallback seguro
            
        pricing = PROVIDER_PRICING[provider_key]
        
        input_cost = (Decimal(call.input_tokens) / 1000) * pricing.input_price
        output_cost = (Decimal(call.output_tokens) / 1000) * pricing.output_price
        
        return input_cost + output_cost
    
    async def get_daily_cost(self, date: datetime) -> CostBreakdown:
        """Retorna custo do dia especificado"""
        start_date = date.replace(hour=0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)
        end_date = start_date + timedelta(days=1)
        
        calls = self.db.query(LLMCall).filter(
            LLMCall.timestamp >= start_date,
            LLMCall.timestamp < end_date
        ).all()
        
        return self._aggregate_costs(calls)
    
    async def get_weekly_cost(self, start_date: datetime) -> CostBreakdown:
        """Retorna custo da semana"""
        end_date = start_date + timedelta(days=7)
        
        calls = self.db.query(LLMCall).filter(
            LLMCall.timestamp >= start_date,
            LLMCall.timestamp < end_date
        ).all()
        
        return self._aggregate_costs(calls)
    
    def _aggregate_costs(self, calls: List[LLMCall]) -> CostBreakdown:
        """Agrega custos de múltiplas chamadas"""
        total_cost = Decimal("0.00")
        by_provider = {}
        by_feature = {}
        by_model = {}
        by_day = {}
        
        for call in calls:
            cost = self.calculate_call_cost(call)
            total_cost += cost
            
            # Por provedor
            provider_key = call.provider
            by_provider[provider_key] = by_provider.get(provider_key, Decimal("0.00")) + cost
            
            # Por feature
            by_feature[call.feature] = by_feature.get(call.feature, Decimal("0.00")) + cost
            
            # Por modelo
            model_key = f"{call.provider}:{call.model}"
            by_model[model_key] = by_model.get(model_key, Decimal("0.00")) + cost
            
            # Por dia
            day_str = call.timestamp.strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            by_day[day_str] = by_day.get(day_str, Decimal("0.00")) + cost
        
        return CostBreakdown(
            total_cost=total_cost,
            by_provider=by_provider,
            by_feature=by_feature,
            by_model=by_model,
            by_day=by_day
        )
    
    async def check_cost_anomalies(self, period: str = "daily") -> List[Dict]:
        """Verifica anomalias de custo"""
        anomalies = []
        
        if period == "daily":
            today = datetime.now().replace(hour=0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)
            cost_data = await self.get_daily_cost(today)
            
            # Verifica cada feature vs custo esperado
            for feature, actual_cost in cost_data.by_feature.items():
                expected_cost = self.expected_costs.get(f"feature:{feature}", Decimal("0.00"))
                
                if expected_cost > 0:
                    increase_pct = ((actual_cost - expected_cost) / expected_cost) * 100
                    
                    if increase_pct > 20:  # Alerta >20%
                        anomaly = {
                            "type": "cost_increase",
                            "feature": feature,
                            "actual_cost": float(actual_cost),
                            "expected_cost": float(expected_cost),
                            "increase_pct": float(increase_pct),
                            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
                            "severity": "high" if increase_pct > 50 else "medium"
                        }
                        anomalies.append(anomaly)
                        
                        # Salva alerta no banco
                        alert = CostAlert(
                            alert_type="cost_increase",
                            feature=feature,
                            actual_cost=actual_cost,
                            expected_cost=expected_cost,
                            increase_pct=increase_pct,
                            severity=anomaly["severity"],
                            resolved=False
                        )
                        self.db.add(alert)
                        self.db.commit()
        
        return anomalies
    
    async def get_cost_trends(self, days: int = 30) -> Dict:
        """Retorna tendências de custo dos últimos N dias"""
        end_date = datetime.now()
        start_date = end_date - timedelta(days=days)
        
        trends = {
            "total_trend": [],
            "feature_trends": {},
            "provider_trends": {}
        }
        
        current_date = start_date
        while current_date <= end_date:
            daily_cost = await self.get_daily_cost(current_date)
            
            trends["total_trend"].append({
                "date": current_date.strftime("%Y-%m-%d"),
                "cost": float(daily_cost.total_cost)
            })
            
            # Feature trends
            for feature, cost in daily_cost.by_feature.items():
                if feature not in trends["feature_trends"]:
                    trends["feature_trends"][feature] = []
                
                trends["feature_trends"][feature].append({
                    "date": current_date.strftime("%Y-%m-%d"),
                    "cost": float(cost)
                })
            
            # Provider trends
            for provider, cost in daily_cost.by_provider.items():
                if provider not in trends["provider_trends"]:
                    trends["provider_trends"][provider] = []
                
                trends["provider_trends"][provider].append({
                    "date": current_date.strftime("%Y-%m-%d"),
                    "cost": float(cost)
                })
            
            current_date += timedelta(days=1)
        
        return trends
```

```python
# src/ai_ops/monitoring/quality_monitor.py
"""
Monitor de qualidade e detecção de drift (≥10%)
"""
import json
import asyncio
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass
import statistics
import logging

from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from pydantic import BaseModel

from src.ai_ops.database.models import QualityMetric, DriftAlert
from src.utils.logger_setup import get_logger

logger = get_logger(__name__)

@dataclass
class GoldenDatasetItem:
    """Item do golden dataset"""
    id: str
    input_text: str
    expected_output: str
    feature: str
    metadata: Dict[str, Any]



### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]

### `dbt/models/raw/raw_telemetry_events.sql`
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='incremental',
    unique_key='event_id',
    partition_by={
      "field": "event_timestamp",
      "data_type": "timestamp",
      "granularity": "day"
    },
    cluster_by = ["event_type", "user_id"]
) }}

SELECT
  event_id,
  user_id,
  session_id,
  event_type,
  event_name,
  event_properties,
  page_url,
  user_agent,
  ip_address,
  device_type,
  os,
  browser,
  country_code,
  region,
  city,
  event_timestamp,
  ingested_at
FROM {{ source('telemetry_stream', 'events') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
WHERE event_timestamp >= (SELECT MAX(event_timestamp) FROM {{ this }})
{% endif %}
```

### `dbt/models/raw/raw_llm_calls.sql`
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='incremental',
    unique_key='call_id',
    partition_by={
      "field": "call_timestamp",
      "data_type": "timestamp",
      "granularity": "day"
    },
    cluster_by = ["model_name", "feature_name"]
) }}

SELECT
  call_id,
  request_id,
  user_id,
  session_id,
  feature_name,
  model_name,
  provider,
  prompt_tokens,
  completion_tokens,
  total_tokens,
  cost_usd,
  latency_ms,
  success,
  error_code,
  error_message,
  request_metadata,
  response_metadata,
  call_timestamp,
  ingested_at
FROM {{ source('llm_gateway', 'calls') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
WHERE call_timestamp >= (SELECT MAX(call_timestamp) FROM {{ this }})
{% endif %}
```

### `dbt/models/staging/stg_telemetry_events.sql`
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    tags=['staging', 'telemetry']
) }}

WITH source AS (
    SELECT * FROM {{ ref('raw_telemetry_events') }}
),

cleaned AS (
    SELECT
        -- Primary key
        event_id,
        
        -- User identifiers
        user_id,
        NULLIF(TRIM(user_id), '') AS user_id_cleaned,
        session_id,
        
        -- Event details
        event_type,
        LOWER(TRIM(event_type)) AS event_type_normalized,
        event_name,
        LOWER(TRIM(event_name)) AS event_name_normalized,
        
        -- Parse JSON properties
        JSON_EXTRACT_SCALAR(event_properties, '$.feature') AS feature_name,
        JSON_EXTRACT_SCALAR(event_properties, '$.duration_ms') AS duration_ms,
        JSON_EXTRACT_SCALAR(event_properties, '$.element_id') AS element_id,
        
        -- Location
        page_url,
        SPLIT(page_url, '?')[OFFSET(0)] AS page_path,
        
        -- Device info
        user_agent,
        device_type,
        os,
        browser,
        
        -- Geolocation (anonymized)
        CASE 
            WHEN ip_address IS NOT NULL THEN 'REDACTED'
            ELSE NULL 
        END AS ip_address_anon,
        country_code,
        region,
        city,
        
        -- Timestamps
        TIMESTAMP(event_timestamp) AS event_timestamp,
        TIMESTAMP(ingested_at) AS ingested_at,
        
        -- Quality flags
        user_id IS NOT NULL AS has_user_id,
        event_type IS NOT NULL AS has_event_type,
        event_timestamp IS NOT NULL AS has_timestamp
        
    FROM source
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned
```

### `dbt/models/staging/stg_llm_calls.sql`
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    tags=['staging', 'llm']
) }}

WITH source AS (
    SELECT * FROM {{ ref('raw_llm_calls') }}
),

cleaned AS (
    SELECT
        -- Primary key
        call_id,
        
        -- Identifiers
        request_id,
        user_id,
        session_id,
        
        -- Feature and model
        feature_name,
        UPPER(TRIM(feature_name)) AS feature_name_normalized,
        model_name,
        provider,
        
        -- Token usage
        CAST(prompt_tokens AS INT64) AS prompt_tokens,
        CAST(completion_tokens AS INT64) AS completion_tokens,
        CAST(total_tokens AS INT64) AS total_tokens,
        
        -- Cost calculation
        CAST(cost_usd AS FLOAT64) AS cost_usd,
        ROUND(CAST(cost_usd AS FLOAT64), 6) AS cost_usd_rounded,
        
        -- Performance
        CAST(latency_ms AS INT64) AS latency_ms,
        
        -- Status
        CAST(success AS BOOLEAN) AS success,
        error_code,
        error_message,
        
        -- Metadata
        request_metadata,
        response_metadata,
        
        -- Timestamps
        TIMESTAMP(call_timestamp) AS call_timestamp,
        TIMESTAMP(ingested_at) AS ingested_at,
        
        -- Derived fields
        CASE 
            WHEN CAST(success AS BOOLEAN) = true THEN 'SUCCESS'
            WHEN error_code IS NOT NULL THEN 'ERROR'
            ELSE 'UNKNOWN'
        END AS call_status,
        
        -- Quality flags
        call_id IS NOT NULL AS has_call_id,
        model_name IS NOT NULL AS has_model_name,
        total_tokens IS NOT NULL AS has_token_count
        
    FROM source
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned
```

### `dbt/models/marts/product/daily_active_users.sql`
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    tags=['marts', 'product', 'kpi'],
    partition_by={
      "field": "date",
      "data_type": "date",
      "granularity": "day"
    }
) }}

WITH daily_users AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS date,
        user_id_cleaned AS user_id,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS session_count,
        COUNT(*) AS event_count,
        ARRAY_AGG(DISTINCT event_type_normalized IGNORE NULLS) AS event_types,
        MIN(event_timestamp) AS first_event_time,
        MAX(event_timestamp) AS last_event_time
    FROM {{ ref('stg_telemetry_events') }}
    WHERE has_user_id = true
      AND has_timestamp = true
      AND user_id_cleaned IS NOT NULL
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

daily_aggregates AS (
    SELECT
        date,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS active_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS total_sessions,
        SUM(event_count) AS total_events,
        AVG(session_count) AS avg_sessions_per_user,
        AVG(event_count) AS avg_events_per_user,
        -- Engagement metrics
        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN session_count >= 3 THEN user_id END) AS highly_engaged_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN ARRAY_LENGTH(event_types) >= 5 THEN user_id END) AS diverse_activity_users
    FROM daily_users
    CROSS JOIN UNNEST([session_id]) AS session_id
    GROUP BY 1
)

SELECT
    date,
    active_users,
    total_sessions,
    total_events,
    avg_sessions_per_user,
    avg_events_per_user,
    highly_engaged_users,
    diverse_activity_users,
    -- Growth metrics
    active_users - LAG(active_users, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date) AS wau_growth,
    ROUND(SAFE_DIVIDE(highly_engaged_users, active_users), 4) AS engagement_rate,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS calculated_at
FROM daily_aggregates
ORDER BY date DESC
```

### `dbt/models/marts/ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql`
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    tags=['marts', 'ai', 'cost'],
    partition_by={
      "field": "date",
      "data_type": "date",
      "granularity": "day"
    }
) }}

WITH daily_calls AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(call_timestamp) AS date,
        feature_name_normalized AS feature,
        model_name,
        provider,
        COUNT(*) AS call_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN success = true THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS success_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN success = false THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS error_count,
        SUM(prompt_tokens) AS total_prompt_tokens,
        SUM(completion_tokens) AS total_completion_tokens,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS total_tokens,
        SUM(cost_usd_rounded) AS total_cost_usd,
        AVG(latency_ms) AS avg_latency_ms,
        APPROX_QUANTILES(latency_ms, 100)[OFFSET(95)] AS p95_latency_ms,
        APPROX_QUANTILES(latency_ms, 100)[OFFSET(99)] AS p99_latency_ms
    FROM {{ ref('stg_llm_calls') }}
    WHERE has_call_id = true
      AND has_model_name = true
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

feature_summary AS (
    SELECT
        date,
        feature,
        SUM(call_count) AS total_calls,
        SUM(success_count) AS successful_calls,
        SUM(error_count) AS failed_calls,
        SUM(total_cost_usd) AS total_cost,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS total_tokens,
        SAFE_DIVIDE(SUM(total_cost_usd), SUM(total_tokens)) AS cost_per_token,
        SAFE_DIVIDE(SUM(success_count), SUM(call_count)) AS success_rate,
        AVG(avg_latency_ms) AS avg_latency,
        MAX(p95_latency_ms) AS p95_latency,
        MAX(p99_latency_ms) AS p99_latency
    FROM daily_calls
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

cost_trend AS (
    SELECT
        date,
        feature,
        total_calls,
        successful_calls,
        failed_calls,
        total_cost,
        total_tokens,
        cost_per_token,
        success_rate,
        avg_latency,
        p95_latency,
        p99_latency,
        -- Cost efficiency metrics
        total_cost - LAG(total_cost, 7) OVER (PARTITION BY feature ORDER BY date) AS weekly_cost_change,
        SAFE_DIVIDE(total_tokens, total_calls) AS avg_tokens_per_call,
        SAFE_DIVIDE(total_cost, total_calls) AS avg_cost_per_call,
        CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS calculated_at
    FROM feature_summary
)

SELECT * FROM cost_trend
ORDER BY date DESC, total_cost DESC
```

## 2. Testes de Qualidade

### `dbt/tests/schema_tests.yml`
```yaml
version: 2

models:
  - name: raw_telemetry_events
    columns:
      - name: event_id
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: event_timestamp
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: user_id
        tests:
          - not_null
  
  - name: raw_llm_calls
    columns:
      - name: call_id
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: call_timestamp
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: total_tokens
        tests:
          - not_null
  
  - name: stg_telemetry_events
    columns:
      - name: event_id
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: event_timestamp
        tests:
          - not_null
          - relationships:
              to: ref('raw_telemetry_events')
              field: event_timestamp
      - name: user_id_cleaned
        tests:
          - not_null
  
  - name: stg_llm_calls
    columns:
      - name: call_id
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: cost_usd_rounded
        tests:
          - accepted_values:
              values: ['>= 0']
  
  - name: daily_active_users
    columns:
      - name: date
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: active_users
        tests:
          - accepted_values:
              values: ['>= 0']
  
  - name: llm_cost_by_feature
    columns:
      - name: date
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: feature
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: total_cost
        tests:
          - accepted_values:
              values: ['>= 0']
```

### `dbt/tests/data_tests.yml`
```yaml
version: 2

tests:
  - name: test_telemetry_data_freshness
    description: "Ensure telemetry data is fresh (max 1 hour old)"
    model: stg_telemetry_events
    severity: error
    test: |
      SELECT 
        MAX(event_timestamp) as latest_event
      FROM {{ ref('stg_telemetry_events') }}
      WHERE TIMESTAMP_DIFF(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), event_timestamp, HOUR) > 1
  
  - name: test_llm_cost_anomaly
    description: "Detect anomalous LLM cost spikes"
    model: llm_cost_by_feature
    severity: warn
    test: |
      WITH daily_stats AS (
        SELECT
          feature,
          date,
          total_cost,
          AVG(total_cost) OVER (
            PARTITION BY feature 
            ORDER BY date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 7 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING
          ) as avg_7day_cost,
          STDDEV(total_cost) OVER (
            PARTITION BY feature 
            ORDER BY date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 7 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING
          ) as std_7day_cost
        FROM {{ ref('llm_cost_by_feature') }}
      )
      SELECT *
      FROM daily_stats
      WHERE total_cost > avg_7day_cost + (3 * std_7day_cost)
        AND avg_7day_cost IS NOT NULL
  
  - name: test_user_engagement_threshold
    description: "Alert if daily active users drop below threshold"
    model: daily_active_users
    severity: error
    test: |
      SELECT *
      FROM {{ ref('daily_active_users') }}
      WHERE date = CURRENT_DATE() - 1
        AND active_users < 100  -- Minimum expected daily users
```

from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from airflow import DAG
from airflow.operators.python import PythonOperator
from airflow.operators.bash import BashOperator
from airflow.providers.google.cloud.operators.bigquery import (
    BigQueryInsertJobOperator,
    BigQueryCheckOperator
)
from airflow.utils.dates import days_ago

default_args = {
    'owner': 'data_engineering',
    'depends_on_past': False,
    'email_on_failure': True,
    'email_on_retry': False,
    'retries': 3,
    'retry_delay': timedelta(minutes=5),
    'start_date': days_ago(1),
}

dag = DAG(
    'v12_telemetry_pipeline',
    default_args=default_args,
    description='Process V12 telemetry data',
    schedule_interval='*/15 * * * *',  # Every 15 minutes
    catchup=False,
    tags=['v12', 'telemetry', 'product']
)

def check_data_freshness(**context):
    """Check if data is fresh enough for processing"""
    from google.cloud import bigquery
    
    client = bigquery.Client()

## 1. Configuração Principal do Provider (providers.tf)

```hcl
# terraform/providers.tf
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    
    cloudflare = {
      source  = "cloudflare/cloudflare"
      version = "~> 4.0"
    }
    
    datadog = {
      source  = "DataDog/datadog"
      version = "~> 3.0"
    }
  }
  
  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state-v12"
    key            = "terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V12"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

provider "cloudflare" {
  api_token = var.cloudflare_api_token
}

provider "datadog" {
  api_key = var.datadog_api_key
  app_key = var.datadog_app_key
  api_url = "https://api.datadoghq.com/"
}
```

## 2. Módulo VPC (módulo reutilizável)

```hcl
# terraform/modules/vpc/main.tf
resource "aws_vpc" "main" {
  cidr_block           = var.vpc_cidr
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-vpc"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "public" {
  count                   = length(var.public_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id                  = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block              = var.public_subnet_cidrs[count.index]
  availability_zone       = var.availability_zones[count.index % length(var.availability_zones)]
  map_public_ip_on_launch = true
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-public-${count.index}"
    Type = "Public"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "private" {
  count             = length(var.private_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = var.private_subnet_cidrs[count.index]
  availability_zone = var.availability_zones[count.index % length(var.availability_zones)]
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-private-${count.index}"
    Type = "Private"
  }
}

resource "aws_internet_gateway" "main" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-igw"
  }
}

resource "aws_eip" "nat" {
  count = var.enable_nat_gateway ? length(var.public_subnet_cidrs) : 0
  domain = "vpc"
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-nat-eip-${count.index}"
  }
}

resource "aws_nat_gateway" "main" {
  count         = var.enable_nat_gateway ? length(var.public_subnet_cidrs) : 0
  allocation_id = aws_eip.nat[count.index].id
  subnet_id     = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-nat-${count.index}"
  }
  
  depends_on = [aws_internet_gateway.main]
}

resource "aws_route_table" "public" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block = "0.0.0.0/0"
    gateway_id = aws_internet_gateway.main.id
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-public-rt"
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "public" {
  count          = length(var.public_subnet_cidrs)
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.public.id
}

resource "aws_route_table" "private" {
  count  = length(var.private_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  dynamic "route" {
    for_each = var.enable_nat_gateway ? [1] : []
    content {
      cidr_block     = "0.0.0.0/0"
      nat_gateway_id = aws_nat_gateway.main[count.index % length(aws_nat_gateway.main)].id
    }
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-private-rt-${count.index}"
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "private" {
  count          = length(var.private_subnet_cidrs)
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.private[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.private[count.index].id
}

resource "aws_security_group" "vpc_endpoints" {
  name        = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-vpc-endpoints-sg"
  description = "Security group for VPC endpoints"
  vpc_id      = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  ingress {
    from_port   = 443
    to_port     = 443
    protocol    = "tcp"
    cidr_blocks = [var.vpc_cidr]
  }
  
  egress {
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    protocol    = "-1"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-vpc-endpoints-sg"
  }
}

resource "aws_vpc_endpoint" "s3" {
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  service_name      = "com.amazonaws.${var.aws_region}.s3"
  vpc_endpoint_type = "Gateway"
  route_table_ids   = [aws_route_table.public.id]
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-s3-endpoint"
  }
}

resource "aws_vpc_endpoint" "ecr_api" {
  vpc_id              = aws_vpc.main.id
  service_name        = "com.amazonaws.${var.aws_region}.ecr.api"
  vpc_endpoint_type   = "Interface"
  private_dns_enabled = true
  subnet_ids          = aws_subnet.private[*].id
  security_group_ids  = [aws_security_group.vpc_endpoints.id]
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecr-api-endpoint"
  }
}

resource "aws_vpc_endpoint" "ecr_dkr" {
  vpc_id              = aws_vpc.main.id
  service_name        = "com.amazonaws.${var.aws_region}.ecr.dkr"
  vpc_endpoint_type   = "Interface"
  private_dns_enabled = true
  subnet_ids          = aws_subnet.private[*].id
  security_group_ids  = [aws_security_group.vpc_endpoints.id]
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecr-dkr-endpoint"
  }
}

resource "aws_vpc_endpoint" "logs" {
  vpc_id              = aws_vpc.main.id
  service_name        = "com.amazonaws.${var.aws_region}.logs"
  vpc_endpoint_type   = "Interface"
  private_dns_enabled = true
  subnet_ids          = aws_subnet.private[*].id
  security_group_ids  = [aws_security_group.vpc_endpoints.id]
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-logs-endpoint"
  }
}

resource "aws_vpc_endpoint" "secretsmanager" {
  vpc_id              = aws_vpc.main.id
  service_name        = "com.amazonaws.${var.aws_region}.secretsmanager"
  vpc_endpoint_type   = "Interface"
  private_dns_enabled = true
  subnet_ids          = aws_subnet.private[*].id
  security_group_ids  = [aws_security_group.vpc_endpoints.id]
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-secretsmanager-endpoint"
  }
}
```

```hcl
# terraform/modules/vpc/variables.tf
variable "project_name" {
  description = "Name of the project"
  type        = string
}

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name (dev, staging, production)"
  type        = string
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "CIDR block for the VPC"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "public_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "List of public subnet CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24"]
}

variable "private_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "List of private subnet CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24"]
}

variable "availability_zones" {
  description = "List of availability zones"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["us-east-1a", "us-east-1b"]
}

variable "aws_region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "enable_nat_gateway" {
  description = "Enable NAT Gateway for private subnets"
  type        = bool
  default     = true
}
```

## 3. Módulo ECS com Auto-scaling

```hcl
# terraform/modules/ecs/main.tf
resource "aws_ecs_cluster" "main" {
  name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-cluster"
  
  setting {
    name  = "containerInsights"
    value = "enabled"
  }
  
  configuration {
    execute_command_configuration {
      logging = "OVERRIDE"
      
      log_configuration {
        cloud_watch_log_group_name = aws_cloudwatch_log_group.ecs_exec.name
      }
    }
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-cluster"
  }
}

resource "aws_cloudwatch_log_group" "ecs_exec" {
  name              = "/ecs/${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-exec"
  retention_in_days = var.log_retention_days
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-exec-log-group"
  }
}

resource "aws_iam_role" "ecs_task_execution_role" {
  name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-task-execution-role"
  
  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Action = "sts:AssumeRole"
        Effect = "Allow"
        Principal = {
          Service = "ecs-tasks.amazonaws.com"
        }
      }
    ]
  })
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-task-execution-role"
  }
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "ecs_task_execution_role_policy" {
  role       = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_execution_role.name
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/service-role/AmazonECSTaskExecutionRolePolicy"
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy" "ecs_task_execution_custom" {
  name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-task-execution-custom"
  role = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_execution_role.id
  
  policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Effect = "Allow"
        Action = [
          "ecr:GetAuthorizationToken",
          "ecr:BatchCheckLayerAvailability",
          "ecr:GetDownloadUrlForLayer",
          "ecr:BatchGetImage",
          "logs:CreateLogStream",
          "logs:PutLogEvents",
          "secretsmanager:GetSecretValue",
          "ssm:GetParameters"
        ]
        Resource = "*"
      }
    ]
  })
}

resource "aws_iam_role" "ecs_task_role" {
  name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-task-role"
  
  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Action = "sts:AssumeRole"
        Effect = "Allow"
        Principal = {
          Service = "ecs-tasks.amazonaws.com"
        }
      }
    ]
  })
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-task-role"
  }
}

resource "aws_ecs_task_definition" "main" {
  family                   = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-task"
  network_mode             = "awsvpc"
  requires_compatibilities = ["FARGATE"]
  cpu                      = var.task_cpu
  memory                   = var.task_memory
  execution_role_arn       = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_execution_role.arn
  task_role_arn            = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_role.arn
  
  container_definitions = jsonencode([
    {
      name      = var.container_name
      image     = var.container_image
      cpu       = var.task_cpu
      memory    = var.task_memory
      essential = true
      
      portMappings = [
        {
          containerPort = var.container_port
          hostPort      = var.container_port
          protocol      = "tcp"
        }
      ]
      
      environment = var.container_environment
      
      secrets = var.container_secrets
      
      logConfiguration = {
        logDriver = "awslogs"
        options = {
          awslogs-group         = aws_cloudwatch_log_group.ecs.name
          awslogs-region        = var.aws_region
          awslogs-stream-prefix = "ecs"
        }
      }
      
      healthCheck = {
        command     = ["CMD-SHELL", var.health_check_command]
        interval    = 30
        timeout     = 5
        retries     = 3
        startPeriod = 60
      }
    }
  ])
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-task-definition"
  }
}

resource "aws_cloudwatch_log_group" "ecs" {
  name              = "/ecs/${var.project_name}-${var.environment}"
  retention_in_days = var.log_retention_days
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-ecs-log-group"
  }
}

resource "aws_ecs_service" "main" {
  name            = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-service"
  cluster         = aws_ecs_cluster.main.id
  task_definition = aws_ecs_task_definition.main.arn
  desired_count   = var.desired_count
  launch_type     = "FARGATE"
  
  network_configuration {
    subnets          = var.private_subnet_ids
    security_groups  = [aws_security_group.ecs.id]
    assign_public_ip = false
  }
  
  load_balancer {
    target_group_arn = var.target_group_arn
    container_name   = var.container_name
    container_port   = var.container_port
  }


### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Threat Modeling e Hardening de Segurança

## 1. Análise de Threat Modeling STRIDE para V12

### Ativos Críticos Identificados:
1. **Dados de Usuário**: Credenciais, tokens de sessão, dados pessoais
2. **Sistema de Autenticação**: JWT, OAuth, MFA
3. **API Endpoints**: Todos os endpoints REST/GraphQL
4. **Banco de Dados**: PostgreSQL com dados sensíveis
5. **Integrações Externas**: WhatsApp API, serviços de terceiros
6. **Sistema de LLM**: Prompts, contextos, outputs
7. **Arquivos Upload**: Imagens, documentos, mídia

### Matriz de Ameaças STRIDE:

#### S - Spoofing (Falsificação)
- **Ameaça**: Ataque de força bruta em login
- **Controle**: Rate limiting (10 tentativas/hora), MFA obrigatório
- **Ameaça**: Token JWT roubado/reutilizado
- **Controle**: Tokens curtos (15min), refresh tokens rotativos

#### T - Tampering (Manipulação)
- **Ameaça**: Manipulação de dados em trânsito
- **Controle**: TLS 1.3 obrigatório, HSTS headers
- **Ameaça**: SQL Injection
- **Controle**: Prepared statements, ORM com escaping
- **Ameaça**: Manipulação de prompts LLM
- **Controle**: Sanitização de inputs, validação de contexto

#### R - Repudiation (Repúdio)
- **Ameaça**: Negação de ações administrativas
- **Controle**: Logs imutáveis com auditoria completa
- **Ameaça**: Falta de rastreabilidade
- **Controle**: Correlation IDs em todas as requisições

#### I - Information Disclosure (Divulgação)
- **Ameaça**: Vazamento de dados sensíveis em logs
- **Controle**: Máscara de PII em logs
- **Ameaça**: Exposição de dados via API
- **Controle**: Autorização granular por recurso
- **Ameaça**: Vazamento de system prompts LLM
- **Controle**: Prompt engineering resistente a extração

#### D - Denial of Service (Negação)
- **Ameaça**: Ataque DDoS na API
- **Controle**: Rate limiting por IP/usuário, WAF
- **Ameaça**: Exaustão de recursos LLM
- **Controle**: Limite de tokens por usuário/sessão

#### E - Elevation of Privilege (Elevação)
- **Ameaça**: IDOR (Insecure Direct Object Reference)
- **Controle**: Verificação de permissão por recurso
- **Ameaça**: JWT token manipulation
- **Controle**: Assinatura forte (RS256), validação de claims

const securityConfig = {
  // Autenticação
  auth: {
    jwtSecret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'change-in-production',
    jwtExpiration: '15m',
    refreshTokenExpiration: '7d',
    mfaRequired: true,
    maxLoginAttempts: 10,
    lockoutDuration: '30m'
  },
  
  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimiting: {
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
    maxRequests: 100, // limite por IP
    message: 'Too many requests from this IP'
  },
  
  // WAF Rules
  waf: {
    enabled: true,
    blockSQLi: true,
    blockXSS: true,
    blockPathTraversal: true,
    maxRequestBodySize: '1mb'
  },
  
  // CORS
  cors: {
    origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(',') || ['http://localhost:3000'],
    credentials: true,
    maxAge: 86400
  },
  
  // Headers de Segurança
  headers: {
    hsts: {
      maxAge: 31536000,
      includeSubDomains: true,
      preload: true
    },
    csp: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      fontSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameSrc: ["'none'"]
    },
    xssProtection: true,
    noSniff: true,
    frameguard: 'DENY'
  },
  
  // LLM Security
  llm: {
    maxTokensPerRequest: 4096,
    maxContextLength: 8000,
    promptInjectionDetection: true,
    outputSanitization: true,
    systemPromptProtection: true
  },
  
  // Logging & Audit
  audit: {
    enabled: true,
    logSensitiveOperations: true,
    maskPII: true,
    retentionDays: 90
  }
};

module.exports = securityConfig;

### 2.2 Middleware de Headers de Segurança

**src/middleware/security-headers.js**
```javascript
const helmet = require('helmet');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security-config');

function configureSecurityHeaders(app) {
  // Helmet com configurações customizadas
  app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
      directives: securityConfig.headers.csp
    },
    hsts: securityConfig.headers.hsts,
    xssFilter: securityConfig.headers.xssProtection,
    noSniff: securityConfig.headers.noSniff,
    frameguard: { action: securityConfig.headers.frameguard }
  }));
  
  // Headers customizados adicionais
  app.use((req, res, next) => {
    // Prevenir clickjacking
    res.setHeader('X-Frame-Options', 'DENY');
    
    // Referrer Policy
    res.setHeader('Referrer-Policy', 'strict-origin-when-cross-origin');
    
    // Permissions Policy
    res.setHeader('Permissions-Policy', 
      'camera=(), microphone=(), geolocation=(), payment=()');
    
    // X-Content-Type-Options
    res.setHeader('X-Content-Type-Options', 'nosniff');
    
    // Cache-Control para endpoints sensíveis
    if (req.path.includes('/api/auth') || req.path.includes('/api/admin')) {
      res.setHeader('Cache-Control', 'no-store, max-age=0');
    }
    
    next();
  });
}

module.exports = configureSecurityHeaders;
```

### 2.3 WAF (Web Application Firewall)

**src/security/waf/waf.middleware.js**
```javascript
const securityConfig = require('../../config/security-config');

class WAFMiddleware {
  constructor() {
    this.rules = [];
    this.loadRules();
  }

  loadRules() {
    // Regra: SQL Injection
    this.rules.push({
      name: 'SQL Injection',
      pattern: /(\b(SELECT|INSERT|UPDATE|DELETE|DROP|UNION|EXEC|ALTER|CREATE|TRUNCATE)\b|\-\-|\/\*|\*\/|;)/gi,
      action: 'block'
    });

    // Regra: XSS
    this.rules.push({
      name: 'XSS Attack',
      pattern: /(<script|javascript:|onload=|onerror=|onclick=|alert\(|document\.cookie|eval\(|window\.location)/gi,
      action: 'block'
    });

    // Regra: Path Traversal
    this.rules.push({
      name: 'Path Traversal',
      pattern: /(\.\.\/|\.\.\\|\.\.%2f|\.\.%5c)/gi,
      action: 'block'
    });

    // Regra: Command Injection
    this.rules.push({
      name: 'Command Injection',
      pattern: /(\|&|;|\|\||&&|`|\$\(|\n|\r)/gi,
      action: 'block'
    });
  }

  middleware() {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      if (!securityConfig.waf.enabled) {
        return next();
      }

      // Verificar query parameters
      if (req.query) {
        for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(req.query)) {
          if (this.detectAttack(key) || this.detectAttack(value)) {
            return this.blockRequest(req, res, 'Malicious query parameter detected');
          }
        }
      }

      // Verificar body
      if (req.body && typeof req.body === 'object') {
        const bodyString = JSON.stringify(req.body);
        if (this.detectAttack(bodyString)) {
          return this.blockRequest(req, res, 'Malicious request body detected');
        }
      }

      // Verificar headers
      for (const [header, value] of Object.entries(req.headers)) {
        if (this.detectAttack(value)) {
          return this.blockRequest(req, res, 'Malicious header detected');
        }
      }

      // Verificar URL
      if (this.detectAttack(req.url)) {
        return this.blockRequest(req, res, 'Malicious URL detected');
      }

      next();
    };
  }

  detectAttack(input) {
    if (!input || typeof input !== 'string') return false;

    for (const rule of this.rules) {
      if (rule.pattern.test(input)) {
        console.warn(`[WAF] Rule "${rule.name}" triggered: ${input.substring(0, 100)}`);
        return true;
      }
    }

    return false;
  }

  blockRequest(req, res, reason) {
    // Log do incidente
    console.error(`[WAF BLOCKED] ${req.ip} - ${req.method} ${req.url} - Reason: ${reason}`);
    
    // Retornar erro 403
    res.status(403).json({
      error: 'Access Forbidden',
      message: 'Request blocked by security rules',
      requestId: req.id,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }
}

module.exports = new WAFMiddleware();
```

### 2.4 Rate Limiter Avançado

**src/security/auth/rate-limiter.js**
```javascript
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const RedisStore = require('rate-limit-redis');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const securityConfig = require('../../config/security-config');

class RateLimiter {
  constructor() {
    this.redisClient = new Redis({
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: process.env.REDIS_PORT || 6379,
      password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD
    });

    this.limiterConfigs = {
      // Limite geral para API
      api: rateLimit({
        store: new RedisStore({
          client: this.redisClient,
          prefix: 'rl:api:'
        }),
        windowMs: securityConfig.rateLimiting.windowMs,
        max: securityConfig.rateLimiting.maxRequests,
        message: securityConfig.rateLimiting.message,
        standardHeaders: true,
        legacyHeaders: false,
        skipSuccessfulRequests: false
      }),

      // Limite mais restrito para autenticação
      auth: rateLimit({
        store: new RedisStore({
          client: this.redisClient,
          prefix: 'rl:auth:'
        }),
        windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
        max: 10, // 10 tentativas por IP
        message: 'Too many login attempts, please try again later',
        skipSuccessfulRequests: true
      }),

      // Limite para endpoints de criação
      create: rateLimit({
        store: new RedisStore({
          client: this.redisClient,
          prefix: 'rl:create:'
        }),
        windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hora
        max: 50, // 50 criações por hora
        message: 'Too many creation requests'
      }),

      // Limite específico para LLM
      llm: rateLimit({
        store: new RedisStore({
          client: this.redisClient,
          prefix: 'rl:llm:'
        }),
        windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hora
        max: 100, // 100 requests LLM por hora
        message: 'LLM rate limit exceeded'
      })
    };
  }

  getMiddleware(type = 'api') {
    return this.limiterConfigs[type] || this.limiterConfigs.api;
  }

  // Método para resetar limites (apenas admin)
  async resetLimit(key) {
    await this.redisClient.del(`rl:${key}:${req.ip}`);
  }
}

module.exports = new RateLimiter();
```

### 2.5 Sistema de Autenticação Reforçada

**src/security/auth/jwt.strategy.js**
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const securityConfig = require('../../config/security-config');

class JWTStrategy {
  constructor() {
    this.secret = securityConfig.auth.jwtSecret;
    this.algorithm = 'RS256'; // Usar assinatura assimétrica em produção
    
    // Em produção, usar chaves RSA
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
      this.privateKey = process.env.JWT_PRIVATE_KEY;
      this.publicKey = process.env.JWT_PUBLIC_KEY;
    }
  }

  generateAccessToken(user) {
    const payload = {
      sub: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      role: user.role,
      permissions: user.permissions,
      jti: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex') // ID único do token
    };

    const options = {
      expiresIn: securityConfig.auth.jwtExpiration,
      issuer: 'diyapp-v12',
      audience: 'diyapp-users'
    };

    return jwt.sign(payload, this.secret, options);
  }

  generateRefreshToken(user) {
    const payload = {
      sub: user.id,
      jti: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex')
    };

    const options = {
      expiresIn: securityConfig.auth.refreshTokenExpiration,
      issuer: 'diyapp-v12',
      audience: 'diyapp-refresh'
    };

    const token = jwt.sign(payload, this.secret, options);
    
    // Armazenar hash do refresh token no DB
    const hash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(token).digest('hex');
    
    return { token, hash };
  }

  verifyToken(token, type = 'access') {
    try {
      const options = {
        issuer: 'diyapp-v12',
        audience: type === 'access' ? 'diyapp-users' : 'diyapp-refresh'
      };

      return jwt.verify(token, this.secret, options);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Token verification failed: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }

  // Blacklist de tokens (para logout)
  async blacklistToken(token, expiresAt) {
    const ttl = Math.floor((expiresAt - Date.now()) / 1000);
    if (ttl > 0) {
      const hash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(token).digest('hex');
      // Armazenar no Redis
      await redisClient.setex(`blacklist:${hash}`, ttl, '1');
    }
  }

  async isTokenBlacklisted(token) {
    const hash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(token).digest('hex');
    const result = await redisClient.get(`blacklist:${hash}`);
    return result === '1';
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTStrategy();
```

      allowedAttributes: {},
      allowedIframeHostnames: []
    };

    // Padrões maliciosos conhecidos
    this.maliciousPatterns = [
      /<script\b[^<]*(?:(?!<\/script>)<[^<]*)*<\/script>/gi,
      /javascript:/gi,

## 2. Testes de Carga com k6

### `src/load-tests/smoke.js` (Teste de Fumaça)
```javascript
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep } from 'k6';
import { htmlReport } from 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/benc-uk/k6-reporter/main/dist/bundle.js';

export const options = {
  vus: 10,
  duration: '1m',
  thresholds: {
    http_req_duration: ['p(95)<500'], // 95% das requisições < 500ms
    http_req_failed: ['rate<0.01'], // Taxa de falha < 1%
  },
};

export default function () {
  const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'https://diyapp-v12.example.com';
  
  // Teste do endpoint principal
  const res1 = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/health`);
  check(res1, {
    'status is 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'response time < 500ms': (r) => r.timings.duration < 500,
  });
  
  // Teste de autenticação
  const loginPayload = JSON.stringify({
    email: 'test@example.com',
    password: 'test123',
  });
  
  const params = {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
  };
  
  const res2 = http.post(`${BASE_URL}/api/auth/login`, loginPayload, params);
  check(res2, {
    'login status is 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'has auth token': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).token !== undefined,
  });
  
  // Teste de API protegida com token
  if (res2.status === 200) {
    const token = JSON.parse(res2.body).token;
    const headers = {
      'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    };
    
    const res3 = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/user/profile`, { headers });
    check(res3, {
      'profile status is 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    });
  }
  
  sleep(1);
}

export function handleSummary(data) {
  return {
    'reports/load/smoke-report.html': htmlReport(data),
    'stdout': textSummary(data, { indent: ' ', enableColors: true }),
  };
}
```

### `src/load-tests/stress.js` (Teste de Estresse)
```javascript
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep } from 'k6';
import { Rate } from 'k6/metrics';

const errorRate = new Rate('errors');

export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '2m', target: 100 },  // Ramp-up para 100 usuários
    { duration: '5m', target: 100 },  // Estabilidade
    { duration: '2m', target: 300 },  // Ramp-up para 300
    { duration: '5m', target: 300 },  // Pico de carga
    { duration: '2m', target: 100 },  // Ramp-down
    { duration: '2m', target: 0 },    // Recuperação
  ],
  thresholds: {
    http_req_duration: ['p(95)<1000'],
    http_req_failed: ['rate<0.05'],
    errors: ['rate<0.1'],
  },
};

export default function () {
  const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'https://diyapp-v12.example.com';
  
  const endpoints = [
    '/api/health',
    '/api/products',
    '/api/categories',
    '/api/search?q=test',
  ];
  
  const endpoint = endpoints[Math.floor(Math.random() * endpoints.length)];
  const res = http.get(`${BASE_URL}${endpoint}`);
  
  const success = check(res, {
    'status is 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'response time < 2s': (r) => r.timings.duration < 2000,
  });
  
  errorRate.add(!success);
  
  // 30% das requisições são POST
  if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
    const payload = JSON.stringify({
      name: `Product_${Date.now()}`,
      price: Math.random() * 100,
      category: 'test',
    });
    
    const params = {
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    };
    
    const resPost = http.post(`${BASE_URL}/api/products`, payload, params);
    check(resPost, {
      'POST status is 201': (r) => r.status === 201,
    });
  }
  
  sleep(Math.random() * 2 + 1); // Sleep entre 1-3 segundos
}
```

### `src/load-tests/soak.js` (Teste de Resistência - 24h)
```javascript
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep } from 'k6';
import { Trend } from 'k6/metrics';

const responseTimeTrend = new Trend('response_time');

export const options = {
  vus: 50,
  duration: '24h',
  thresholds: {
    http_req_duration: ['p(95)<800'],
    http_req_failed: ['rate<0.02'],
  },
};

export default function () {
  const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'https://diyapp-v12.example.com';
  
  const start = Date.now();
  const res = http.batch([
    ['GET', `${BASE_URL}/api/health`, null, {}],
    ['GET', `${BASE_URL}/api/metrics`, null, {}],
    ['GET', `${BASE_URL}/api/system/status`, null, {}],
  ]);
  
  const end = Date.now();
  responseTimeTrend.add(end - start);
  
  check(res[0], {
    'health status is 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
  });
  
  // A cada hora, faz uma operação mais pesada
  if (Date.now() % 3600000 < 1000) { // Aproximadamente a cada hora
    const heavyRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/reports/daily`);
    check(heavyRes, {
      'report status is 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    });
  }
  
  sleep(30 + Math.random() * 30); // Sleep entre 30-60 segundos
}
```

## 3. Testes de Segurança com OWASP ZAP

### `src/security/zap-scan.js`
```javascript
const zaproxy = require('zaproxy');
const fs = require('fs-extra');
const path = require('path');
const yaml = require('js-yaml');

class SecurityScanner {
  constructor() {
    this.zap = new zaproxy('localhost', 8080, 'http');
    this.reportsDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../reports/security');
    this.config = this.loadConfig();
  }

  loadConfig() {
    const configPath = path.join(__dirname, 'owasp-config/scan-config.yaml');
    return yaml.load(fs.readFileSync(configPath, 'utf8'));
  }

  async startZap() {
    console.log('🚀 Iniciando ZAP...');
    // Em produção, usaríamos Docker ou processo separado
    // Para demonstração, assumimos ZAP já rodando
  }

  async spiderScan(targetUrl) {
    console.log(`🕷️  Iniciando spider scan em: ${targetUrl}`);
    
    const scanId = await this.zap.spider.scan(targetUrl);
    let progress = 0;
    
    while (progress < 100) {
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
      progress = await this.zap.spider.status(scanId);
      console.log(`Spider progresso: ${progress}%`);
    }
    
    const results = await this.zap.spider.results(scanId);
    console.log(`✅ Spider encontrou ${results.length} URLs`);
    return results;
  }

  async activeScan(targetUrl) {
    console.log(`🔍 Iniciando active scan em: ${targetUrl}`);
    
    const scanId = await this.zap.ascan.scan(targetUrl);
    let progress = 0;
    
    while (progress < 100) {
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 5000));
      progress = await this.zap.ascan.status(scanId);
      console.log(`Active scan progresso: ${progress}%`);
    }
    
    const alerts = await this.zap.core.alerts();
    return alerts;
  }

  async runSecurityChecks(targetUrl) {
    console.log('🔒 Executando verificações de segurança...');
    
    const checks = [
      this.checkHeaders(targetUrl),
      this.checkCors(targetUrl),
      this.checkHsts(targetUrl),
      this.checkClickjacking(targetUrl),
    ];
    
    const results = await Promise.all(checks);
    return results.flat();
  }

  async checkHeaders(targetUrl) {
    const issues = [];
    const response = await fetch(targetUrl);
    const headers = response.headers;
    
    const requiredHeaders = {
      'X-Content-Type-Options': 'nosniff',
      'X-Frame-Options': 'DENY',
      'X-XSS-Protection': '1; mode=block',
      'Strict-Transport-Security': 'max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains',
    };
    
    for (const [header, expectedValue] of Object.entries(requiredHeaders)) {
      const actualValue = headers.get(header);
      if (!actualValue || !actualValue.includes(expectedValue)) {
        issues.push({
          risk: 'Medium',
          name: `Missing or incorrect ${header} header`,
          description: `Header ${header} should contain: ${expectedValue}`,
          solution: `Configure server to include: ${header}: ${expectedValue}`,
        });
      }
    }
    
    return issues;
  }

  async generateReport(alerts, customChecks) {
    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-');
    const reportPath = path.join(this.reportsDir, `security-scan-${timestamp}.html`);
    
    const report = `
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>Relatório de Segurança - DIYAPP V12</title>
    <style>
        body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; margin: 40px; }
        .critical { background-color: #ffcccc; padding: 10px; border-left: 5px solid #ff0000; }
        .high { background-color: #ffebcc; padding: 10px; border-left: 5px solid #ff9900; }
        .medium { background-color: #ffffcc; padding: 10px; border-left: 5px solid #ffcc00; }
        .low { background-color: #e6f7ff; padding: 10px; border-left: 5px solid #0066cc; }
        .info { background-color: #f0f0f0; padding: 10px; border-left: 5px solid #666666; }
        .summary { margin-bottom: 30px; padding: 20px; background-color: #f5f5f5; }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <h1>🔒 Relatório de Segurança DIYAPP V12</h1>
    <div class="summary">
        <h2>Resumo</h2>
        <p>Data: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}</p>
        <p>Total de vulnerabilidades: ${alerts.length + customChecks.length}</p>
        <p>Críticas: ${alerts.filter(a => a.risk === 'High').length}</p>
        <p>Médias: ${alerts.filter(a => a.risk === 'Medium').length}</p>
        <p>Baixas: ${alerts.filter(a => a.risk === 'Low').length}</p>
    </div>
    
    <h2>Vulnerabilidades Encontradas</h2>
    ${[...alerts, ...customChecks].map(alert => `
    <div class="${alert.risk.toLowerCase()}">
        <h3>${alert.name} (${alert.risk})</h3>
        <p><strong>Descrição:</strong> ${alert.description}</p>
        <p><strong>Solução:</strong> ${alert.solution}</p>
        ${alert.url ? `<p><strong>URL:</strong> ${alert.url}</p>` : ''}
    </div>
    `).join('')}
</body>
</html>`;
    
    await fs.ensureDir(this.reportsDir);
    await fs.writeFile(reportPath, report);
    console.log(`📊 Relatório gerado: ${reportPath}`);
    
    return reportPath;
  }

  async scan(targetUrl) {
    try {
      await this.startZap();
      
      console.log(`🎯 Iniciando scan de segurança para: ${targetUrl}`);
      
      // Spider scan
      const spiderResults = await this.spiderScan(targetUrl);
      
      // Active scan
      const alerts = await this.activeScan(targetUrl);
      
      // Custom security checks
      const customChecks = await this.runSecurityChecks(targetUrl);
      
      // Generate report
      const reportPath = await this.generateReport(alerts, customChecks);
      
      // Check if critical issues found
      const criticalIssues = alerts.filter(a => a.risk === 'High').length;
      if (criticalIssues > 0) {
        console.error(`❌ ${criticalIssues} vulnerabilidades críticas encontradas!`);
        process.exit(1);
      }
      
      console.log('✅ Scan de segurança concluído com sucesso');
      return {
        success: true,
        reportPath,
        totalIssues: alerts.length + customChecks.length,
        criticalIssues,
      };
      
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('❌ Erro durante scan de segurança:', error);
      process.exit(1);
    }
  }
}

// Execução principal
if (require.main === module) {
  const targetUrl = process.env.TARGET_URL || 'https://diyapp-v12.example.com';
  const scanner = new SecurityScanner();
  scanner.scan(targetUrl);
}

module.exports = SecurityScanner;
```

  strength: "MEDIUM"
