# src/mlops/observability/opentelemetry_setup.py
import os
from opentelemetry import trace
from opentelemetry.sdk.trace import TracerProvider
from opentelemetry.sdk.trace.export import BatchSpanProcessor, ConsoleSpanExporter
from opentelemetry.exporter.otlp.proto.grpc.trace_exporter import OTLPSpanExporter
from opentelemetry.sdk.resources import Resource
from opentelemetry.metrics import set_meter_provider
from opentelemetry.sdk.metrics import MeterProvider
from opentelemetry.sdk.metrics.export import PeriodicExportingMetricReader
from opentelemetry.exporter.otlp.proto.grpc.metric_exporter import OTLPMetricExporter
from opentelemetry.instrumentation.fastapi import FastAPIInstrumentor
from opentelemetry.instrumentation.requests import RequestsInstrumentor
import yaml

class OpenTelemetrySetup:
    def __init__(self, config_path="config/mlops_config.yaml"):
        with open(config_path, 'r') as f:
            self.config = yaml.safe_load(f)
        
        self.resource = Resource.create({
            "service.name": self.config['observability']['opentelemetry']['service_name'],
            "service.version": "1.0.0",
            "deployment.environment": self.config['environment']
        })
        
        self.setup_tracing()
        self.setup_metrics()
        self.setup_instrumentation()
    
    def setup_tracing(self):
        """Setup distributed tracing with OTLP exporter"""
        trace.set_tracer_provider(TracerProvider(resource=self.resource))
        tracer_provider = trace.get_tracer_provider()
        
        if self.config['observability']['opentelemetry']['enabled']:
            otlp_exporter = OTLPSpanExporter(
                endpoint=self.config['observability']['opentelemetry']['endpoint'],
                insecure=True
            )
            span_processor = BatchSpanProcessor(otlp_exporter)
        else:
            span_processor = BatchSpanProcessor(ConsoleSpanExporter())
        
        tracer_provider.add_span_processor(span_processor)
        
        self.tracer = trace.get_tracer(__name__)
        return self.tracer
    
    def setup_metrics(self):
        """Setup metrics collection with OTLP exporter"""
        if self.config['observability']['opentelemetry']['enabled']:
            metric_exporter = OTLPMetricExporter(
                endpoint=self.config['observability']['opentelemetry']['metrics_endpoint'],
                insecure=True
            )
            metric_reader = PeriodicExportingMetricReader(metric_exporter, export_interval_millis=10000)
            meter_provider = MeterProvider(
                resource=self.resource,
                metric_readers=[metric_reader]
            )
            set_meter_provider(meter_provider)
        
        self.meter = trace.get_meter_provider().get_meter(__name__)
        
        # Define key metrics
        self.request_counter = self.meter.create_counter(
            name="llm_requests_total",
            description="Total number of LLM requests",
            unit="1"
        )
        
        self.token_counter = self.meter.create_counter(
            name="llm_tokens_total",
            description="Total tokens consumed",
            unit="1"
        )
        
        self.latency_histogram = self.meter.create_histogram(
            name="llm_request_latency",
            description="LLM request latency in milliseconds",
            unit="ms"
        )
        
        self.cost_counter = self.meter.create_counter(
            name="llm_cost_total",
            description="Total cost of LLM requests",
            unit="USD"
        )
        
        self.error_counter = self.meter.create_counter(
            name="llm_errors_total",
            description="Total number of LLM errors",
            unit="1"
        )
    
    def setup_instrumentation(self):
        """Auto-instrument HTTP clients and frameworks"""
        RequestsInstrumentor().instrument()
    
    def instrument_fastapi(self, app):
        """Instrument FastAPI application"""
        FastAPIInstrumentor.instrument_app(app)
    
    def get_tracer(self):
        return self.tracer
    
    def get_meter(self):
        return self.meter

# src/mlops/observability/structured_logging.py
import structlog
import logging
import sys
import json
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
import yaml

class StructuredLogger:
    def __init__(self, config_path="config/mlops_config.yaml"):
        with open(config_path, 'r') as f:
            self.config = yaml.safe_load(f)
        
        self.setup_logging()
        self.logger = structlog.get_logger()
    
    def setup_logging(self):
        """Configure structured logging with JSON output"""
        log_config = self.config['observability']['logging']
        
        # Configure structlog
        structlog.configure(
            processors=[
                structlog.contextvars.merge_contextvars,
                structlog.processors.add_log_level,
                structlog.processors.StackInfoRenderer(),
                structlog.processors.format_exc_info,
                structlog.processors.TimeStamper(fmt="iso"),
                structlog.processors.JSONRenderer()
            ],
            wrapper_class=structlog.make_filtering_bound_logger(
                getattr(logging, log_config['level'])
            ),
            context_class=dict,
            logger_factory=structlog.WriteLoggerFactory(
                file=open(log_config['output_file'], 'a') if log_config.get('output_file') else sys.stdout
            ),
            cache_logger_on_first_use=True,
        )
    
    def log_request(self, 
                   request_id: str,
                   model: str,
                   provider: str,
                   feature: str,
                   input_tokens: int,
                   output_tokens: int,
                   latency_ms: float,
                   cost_usd: float,
                   success: bool,
                   error_message: Optional[str] = None,
                   metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        """Log LLM request with structured data"""
        log_data = {
            "request_id": request_id,
            "model": model,
            "provider": provider,
            "feature": feature,
            "input_tokens": input_tokens,
            "output_tokens": output_tokens,
            "total_tokens": input_tokens + output_tokens,
            "latency_ms": latency_ms,
            "cost_usd": cost_usd,
            "success": success,
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "metadata": metadata or {}
        }
        
        if error_message:
            log_data["error_message"] = error_message
        
        if success:
            self.logger.info("llm_request_completed", **log_data)
        else:
            self.logger.error("llm_request_failed", **log_data)
        
        return log_data
    
    def log_anomaly(self,
                   anomaly_type: str,
                   severity: str,
                   description: str,
                   feature: str,
                   metric_value: float,
                   threshold: float,
                   metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        """Log detected anomalies"""
        log_data = {
            "anomaly_type": anomaly_type,
            "severity": severity,
            "description": description,
            "feature": feature,
            "metric_value": metric_value,
            "threshold": threshold,
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "metadata": metadata or {}
        }
        
        self.logger.warning("anomaly_detected", **log_data)
        return log_data
    
    def log_quality_metric(self,
                          feature: str,
                          metric_name: str,
                          metric_value: float,
                          baseline_value: float,
                          dataset_size: int,
                          metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        """Log quality metrics from golden dataset evaluation"""
        log_data = {
            "feature": feature,
            "metric_name": metric_name,
            "metric_value": metric_value,
            "baseline_value": baseline_value,
            "deviation_percent": abs((metric_value - baseline_value) / baseline_value * 100) if baseline_value != 0 else 0,
            "dataset_size": dataset_size,
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "metadata": metadata or {}
        }
        
        self.logger.info("quality_metric_evaluated", **log_data)
        return log_data

# src/mlops/monitoring/cost_tracker.py
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import pandas as pd
from dataclasses import dataclass
import yaml

@dataclass
class CostRecord:
    timestamp: datetime
    request_id: str
    model: str
    provider: str
    feature: str
    input_tokens: int
    output_tokens: int
    cost_usd: float
    user_id: Optional[str] = None
    session_id: Optional[str] = None

class CostTracker:
    def __init__(self, config_path="config/mlops_config.yaml"):
        with open(config_path, 'r') as f:
            self.config = yaml.safe_load(f)
        
        self.provider_rates = self.config['monitoring']['cost_tracking']['providers']
        self.cost_records: List[CostRecord] = []
        
    def calculate_cost(self, provider: str, model: str, input_tokens: int, output_tokens: int) -> float:
        """Calculate cost based on provider rates"""
        try:
            rate_per_token = self.provider_rates[provider]['models'][model]
            total_tokens = input_tokens + output_tokens
            return total_tokens * rate_per_token / 1000  # Convert to cost per token
        except KeyError:
            # Fallback to default rate if model not found
            return (input_tokens + output_tokens) * 0.001 / 1000
    
    def record_request(self,
                      request_id: str,
                      model: str,
                      provider: str,
                      feature: str,
                      input_tokens: int,
                      output_tokens: int,
                      user_id: Optional[str] = None,
                      session_id: Optional[str] = None) -> CostRecord:
        """Record a new request and calculate its cost"""
        cost = self.calculate_cost(provider, model, input_tokens, output_tokens)
        
        record = CostRecord(
            timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),
            request_id=request_id,
            model=model,
            provider=provider,
            feature=feature,
            input_tokens=input_tokens,
            output_tokens=output_tokens,
            cost_usd=cost,
            user_id=user_id,
            session_id=session_id
        )
        
        self.cost_records.append(record)
        return record
    
    def get_daily_cost(self, date: Optional[datetime] = None) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Get total cost for a specific day"""
        if date is None:
            date = datetime.utcnow().date()
        
        daily_records = [
            r for r in self.cost_records 
            if r.timestamp.date() == date
        ]
        
        return self._aggregate_costs(daily_records)
    
    def get_weekly_cost(self, week_start: Optional[datetime] = None) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Get total cost for a week"""
        if week_start is None:
            week_start = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(days=datetime.utcnow().weekday())
        
        week_end = week_start + timedelta(days=7)
        
        weekly_records = [
            r for r in self.cost_records 
            if week_start <= r.timestamp < week_end
        ]
        
        return self._aggreg

## 1. Esquema de Dados - Modelos dbt

### `dbt/dbt_project.yml`
```yaml
name: 'diyapp_v12_telemetry'
version: '1.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: 'diyapp_v12'

model-paths: ["models"]
analysis-paths: ["analyses"]
test-paths: ["tests"]
seed-paths: ["data"]
macro-paths: ["macros"]
snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_v12_telemetry:
    materialized: table
    raw:
      materialized: incremental
      schema: raw
      tags: ['raw', 'incremental']
    staging:
      materialized: view
      schema: staging
      tags: ['staging', 'view']
    marts:
      materialized: table
      schema: marts
      tags: ['marts', 'table']
    product:
      materialized: table
      schema: product_marts
      tags: ['product', 'marts']
    ai:
      materialized: table
      schema: ai_marts
      tags: ['ai', 'marts']
    ops:
      materialized: table
      schema: ops_marts
      tags: ['ops', 'marts']

seeds:
  diyapp_v12_telemetry:
    enabled: true
    schema: reference
    tags: ['seed', 'reference']
```

### `dbt/models/raw/raw__events.sql`
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='incremental',
        unique_key='event_id',
        partition_by={
            "field": "event_timestamp",
            "data_type": "timestamp",
            "granularity": "day"
        },
        cluster_by=['event_type', 'squad_id']
    )
}}

SELECT
    -- Event identification
    CAST(event_id AS STRING) AS event_id,
    CAST(session_id AS STRING) AS session_id,
    CAST(user_id AS STRING) AS user_id,
    CAST(squad_id AS STRING) AS squad_id,
    
    -- Event metadata
    CAST(event_type AS STRING) AS event_type,
    CAST(event_name AS STRING) AS event_name,
    CAST(feature_name AS STRING) AS feature_name,
    
    -- Event data
    SAFE.PARSE_JSON(event_properties) AS event_properties,
    SAFE.PARSE_JSON(user_properties) AS user_properties,
    
    -- Technical context
    CAST(app_version AS STRING) AS app_version,
    CAST(platform AS STRING) AS platform,
    CAST(os_version AS STRING) AS os_version,
    CAST(device_model AS STRING) AS device_model,
    
    -- Location data (if available)
    CAST(country_code AS STRING) AS country_code,
    CAST(region AS STRING) AS region,
    CAST(city AS STRING) AS city,
    
    -- Timestamps
    TIMESTAMP(event_timestamp) AS event_timestamp,
    TIMESTAMP(client_event_time) AS client_event_time,
    TIMESTAMP(server_received_at) AS server_received_at,
    
    -- Source tracking
    CAST(source_system AS STRING) AS source_system,
    CAST(ingestion_batch_id AS STRING) AS ingestion_batch_id,
    TIMESTAMP(ingestion_timestamp) AS ingestion_timestamp
    
FROM {{ source('diyapp_events', 'raw_events') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
WHERE TIMESTAMP(event_timestamp) > (
    SELECT MAX(event_timestamp) 
    FROM {{ this }}
)
{% endif %}

-- Data quality tests are defined in schema.yml
```

### `dbt/models/raw/raw__llm_calls.sql`
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='incremental',
        unique_key='llm_call_id',
        partition_by={
            "field": "call_timestamp",
            "data_type": "timestamp",
            "granularity": "hour"
        },
        cluster_by=['model_provider', 'model_name', 'feature_name']
    )
}}

SELECT
    -- Call identification
    CAST(llm_call_id AS STRING) AS llm_call_id,
    CAST(request_id AS STRING) AS request_id,
    CAST(correlation_id AS STRING) AS correlation_id,
    
    -- Model information
    CAST(model_provider AS STRING) AS model_provider,
    CAST(model_name AS STRING) AS model_name,
    CAST(model_version AS STRING) AS model_version,
    
    -- Feature context
    CAST(feature_name AS STRING) AS feature_name,
    CAST(squad_id AS STRING) AS squad_id,
    CAST(user_id AS STRING) AS user_id,
    
    -- Token usage
    CAST(input_tokens AS INT64) AS input_tokens,
    CAST(output_tokens AS INT64) AS output_tokens,
    CAST(total_tokens AS INT64) AS total_tokens,
    
    -- Cost data
    CAST(input_token_cost AS NUMERIC) AS input_token_cost,
    CAST(output_token_cost AS NUMERIC) AS output_token_cost,
    CAST(total_cost_usd AS NUMERIC) AS total_cost_usd,
    
    -- Performance metrics
    CAST(latency_ms AS INT64) AS latency_ms,
    CAST(time_to_first_token_ms AS INT64) AS time_to_first_token_ms,
    
    -- Request/Response metadata
    SAFE.PARSE_JSON(request_metadata) AS request_metadata,
    SAFE.PARSE_JSON(response_metadata) AS response_metadata,
    
    -- Status
    CAST(status_code AS INT64) AS status_code,
    CAST(is_success AS BOOLEAN) AS is_success,
    CAST(error_message AS STRING) AS error_message,
    
    -- Timestamps
    TIMESTAMP(call_timestamp) AS call_timestamp,
    TIMESTAMP(request_start_time) AS request_start_time,
    TIMESTAMP(response_end_time) AS response_end_time,
    
    -- Source tracking
    CAST(source_system AS STRING) AS source_system,
    CAST(ingestion_batch_id AS STRING) AS ingestion_batch_id,
    TIMESTAMP(ingestion_timestamp) AS ingestion_timestamp
    
FROM {{ source('llm_gateway', 'raw_llm_calls') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
WHERE TIMESTAMP(call_timestamp) > (
    SELECT MAX(call_timestamp) 
    FROM {{ this }}
)
{% endif %}
```

### `dbt/models/raw/raw__errors.sql`
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='incremental',
        unique_key='error_id',
        partition_by={
            "field": "error_timestamp",
            "data_type": "timestamp",
            "granularity": "day"
        },
        cluster_by=['error_level', 'error_type', 'component_name']
    )
}}

SELECT
    -- Error identification
    CAST(error_id AS STRING) AS error_id,
    CAST(error_code AS STRING) AS error_code,
    CAST(error_type AS STRING) AS error_type,
    
    -- Error details
    CAST(error_message AS STRING) AS error_message,
    CAST(error_stack_trace AS STRING) AS error_stack_trace,
    
    -- Context
    CAST(component_name AS STRING) AS component_name,
    CAST(feature_name AS STRING) AS feature_name,
    CAST(squad_id AS STRING) AS squad_id,
    CAST(user_id AS STRING) AS user_id,
    
    -- Severity
    CAST(error_level AS STRING) AS error_level,
    CAST(is_fatal AS BOOLEAN) AS is_fatal,
    CAST(affects_user_experience AS BOOLEAN) AS affects_user_experience,
    
    -- Technical context
    CAST(app_version AS STRING) AS app_version,
    CAST(environment AS STRING) AS environment,
    CAST(hostname AS STRING) AS hostname,
    
    -- Request context (if applicable)
    CAST(request_id AS STRING) AS request_id,
    CAST(session_id AS STRING) AS session_id,
    SAFE.PARSE_JSON(request_metadata) AS request_metadata,
    
    -- Resolution tracking
    CAST(is_resolved AS BOOLEAN) AS is_resolved,
    CAST(resolution_notes AS STRING) AS resolution_notes,
    TIMESTAMP(resolved_at) AS resolved_at,
    
    -- Timestamps
    TIMESTAMP(error_timestamp) AS error_timestamp,
    TIMESTAMP(detected_at) AS detected_at,
    
    -- Source tracking
    CAST(source_system AS STRING) AS source_system,
    CAST(ingestion_batch_id AS STRING) AS ingestion_batch_id,
    TIMESTAMP(ingestion_timestamp) AS ingestion_timestamp
    
FROM {{ source('error_tracking', 'raw_errors') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
WHERE TIMESTAMP(error_timestamp) > (
    SELECT MAX(error_timestamp) 
    FROM {{ this }}
)
{% endif %}
```

### `dbt/models/staging/stg__events.sql`
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        tags=['staging', 'events']
    )
}}

WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT * FROM {{ ref('raw__events') }}
),

cleaned_events AS (
    SELECT
        -- Event identification (validated)
        event_id,
        session_id,
        COALESCE(user_id, 'anonymous') AS user_id,
        squad_id,
        
        -- Event metadata (standardized)
        LOWER(event_type) AS event_type,
        INITCAP(event_name) AS event_name,
        INITCAP(feature_name) AS feature_name,
        
        -- Event data (cleaned)
        event_properties,
        user_properties,
        
        -- Technical context (validated)
        app_version,
        LOWER(platform) AS platform,
        os_version,
        device_model,
        
        -- Location data
        UPPER(country_code) AS country_code,
        region,
        city,
        
        -- Timestamps (validated)
        event_timestamp,
        client_event_time,
        server_received_at,
        
        -- Derived fields
        TIMESTAMP_DIFF(server_received_at, event_timestamp, SECOND) AS client_server_lag_seconds,
        
        -- Source tracking
        source_system,
        ingestion_batch_id,
        ingestion_timestamp
        
    FROM raw_events
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND event_id IS NOT NULL
      AND event_type IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned_events
```

### `dbt/models/staging/stg__llm_calls.sql`
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        tags=['staging', 'llm_calls']
    )
}}

WITH raw_llm_calls AS (
    SELECT * FROM {{ ref('raw__llm_calls') }}
),

cleaned_llm_calls AS (
    SELECT
        -- Call identification
        llm_call_id,
        request_id,
        correlation_id,
        
        -- Model information (standardized)
        LOWER(model_provider) AS model_provider,
        model_name,
        model_version,
        
        -- Feature context
        INITCAP(feature_name) AS feature_name,
        squad_id,
        COALESCE(user_id, 'system') AS user_id,
        
        -- Token usage (validated)
        GREATEST(0, input_tokens) AS input_tokens,
        GREATEST(0, output_tokens) AS output_tokens,
        GREATEST(0, total_tokens) AS total_tokens,
        
        -- Cost data (calculated if missing)
        COALESCE(input_token_cost, 
            CASE 
                WHEN model_provider = 'openai' THEN input_tokens * 0.0015 / 1000
                WHEN model_provider = 'anthropic' THEN input_tokens * 0.0025 / 1000
                ELSE 0 
            END) AS input_token_cost,
            
        COALESCE(output_token_cost,
            CASE
                WHEN model_provider = 'openai' THEN output_tokens * 0.0020 / 1000
                WHEN model_provider = 'anthropic' THEN output_tokens * 0.0075 / 1000
                ELSE 0
            END) AS output_token_cost,
            
        COALESCE(total_cost_usd, 
            COALESCE(input_token_cost, 0) + COALESCE(output_token_cost, 0)) AS total_cost_usd,
        
        -- Performance metrics (validated)
        GREATEST(0, latency_ms) AS latency_ms,
        GREATEST(0, time_to_first_token_ms) AS time_to_first_token_ms,
        
        -- Request/Response metadata
        request_metadata,
        response_metadata,
        
        -- Status (standardized)
        status_code,
        COALESCE(is_success, status_code BETWEEN 200 AND 299) AS is_success,
        error_message,
        
        -- Timestamps
        call_timestamp,
        request_start_time,
        response_end_time,
        
        -- Derived fields
        TIMESTAMP_DIFF(response_end_time, request_start_time, MILLISECOND) AS calculated_latency_ms,
        
        -- Source tracking
        source_system,
        ingestion_batch_id,
        ingestion_timestamp
        
    FROM raw_llm_calls
    WHERE call_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND llm_call_id IS NOT NULL
      AND model_provider IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned_llm_calls
```

### `dbt/models/marts/product/daily_active_users.sql`
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        tags=['product', 'marts', 'kpi'],
        partition_by={
            "field": "event_date",
            "data_type": "date",
            "granularity": "day"
        },
        cluster_by=['squad_id', 'platform']
    )
}}

WITH daily_events AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS event_date,
        squad_id,
        user_id,
        platform,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS session_count,
        COUNT(*) AS event_count,
        COUNT(DISTINCT feature_name) AS features_used_count
    FROM {{ ref('stg__events') }}
    WHERE event_type IN ('session_start', 'feature_used', 'interaction')
      AND user_id != 'anonymous'
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

daily_active_users AS (
    SELECT
        event_date,
        squad_id,
        platform,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS active_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN session_count >= 3 THEN user_id END) AS engaged_users,
        SUM(session_count) AS total_sessions,
        SUM(event_count) AS total_events,
        AVG(features_used_count) AS avg_features_per_user,
        
        -- Retention metrics (compared to previous day)
        LAG(COUNT(DISTINCT user_id)) OVER (
            PARTITION BY squad_id, platform 
            ORDER BY event_date
        ) AS previous_day_active_users,
        
        -- WAU/MAU ratio components
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) * 1.0 / NULLIF(
            COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) OVER (
                PARTITION BY squad_id, platform, DATE_TRUNC(event_date, WEEK)
            ), 0
        ) AS daily_to_weekly_ratio
        
    FROM daily_events
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
)

SELECT
    event_date,
    squad_id,
    platform,
    active_users,
    engaged_users,
    total_sessions,
    total_events,
    avg_features_per_user,
    previous_day_active_users,
    
    -- Retention rate
    CASE 
        WHEN previous_day_active_users > 0 
        THEN active_users * 1.0 / previous_day_active_users 
        ELSE NULL 
    END AS day_over

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]

## 1. Módulo de Networking (modules/networking/)

### modules/networking/main.tf
```terraform
# Networking Module - VPC, Subnets, Security Groups
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
  }
}

resource "aws_vpc" "main" {
  cidr_block           = var.vpc_cidr
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-vpc"
  })
}

resource "aws_internet_gateway" "main" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-igw"
  })
}

# Public Subnets
resource "aws_subnet" "public" {
  count                   = length(var.public_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id                  = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block              = var.public_subnet_cidrs[count.index]
  availability_zone       = var.availability_zones[count.index % length(var.availability_zones)]
  map_public_ip_on_launch = true

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-public-subnet-${count.index + 1}"
  })
}

# Private Subnets
resource "aws_subnet" "private" {
  count             = length(var.private_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = var.private_subnet_cidrs[count.index]
  availability_zone = var.availability_zones[count.index % length(var.availability_zones)]

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-private-subnet-${count.index + 1}"
  })
}

# Route Tables
resource "aws_route_table" "public" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id

  route {
    cidr_block = "0.0.0.0/0"
    gateway_id = aws_internet_gateway.main.id
  }

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-public-rt"
  })
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "public" {
  count          = length(aws_subnet.public)
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.public.id
}

# NAT Gateway for private subnets
resource "aws_eip" "nat" {
  count = var.enable_nat_gateway ? 1 : 0
  domain = "vpc"

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-nat-eip"
  })
}

resource "aws_nat_gateway" "main" {
  count         = var.enable_nat_gateway ? 1 : 0
  allocation_id = aws_eip.nat[0].id
  subnet_id     = aws_subnet.public[0].id

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-nat-gw"
  })

  depends_on = [aws_internet_gateway.main]
}

resource "aws_route_table" "private" {
  count  = var.enable_nat_gateway ? 1 : 0
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id

  route {
    cidr_block     = "0.0.0.0/0"
    nat_gateway_id = aws_nat_gateway.main[0].id
  }

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-private-rt"
  })
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "private" {
  count          = var.enable_nat_gateway ? length(aws_subnet.private) : 0
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.private[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.private[0].id
}

# Security Groups
resource "aws_security_group" "app" {
  name        = "${var.environment}-app-sg"
  description = "Security group for application instances"
  vpc_id      = aws_vpc.main.id

  ingress {
    description = "HTTP from ALB"
    from_port   = 80
    to_port     = 80
    protocol    = "tcp"
    security_groups = [aws_security_group.alb.id]
  }

  ingress {
    description = "HTTPS from ALB"
    from_port   = 443
    to_port     = 443
    protocol    = "tcp"
    security_groups = [aws_security_group.alb.id]
  }

  ingress {
    description = "SSH from bastion"
    from_port   = 22
    to_port     = 22
    protocol    = "tcp"
    security_groups = var.bastion_security_group_id != "" ? [var.bastion_security_group_id] : []
  }

  egress {
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    protocol    = "-1"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-app-sg"
  })
}

resource "aws_security_group" "alb" {
  name        = "${var.environment}-alb-sg"
  description = "Security group for ALB"
  vpc_id      = aws_vpc.main.id

  ingress {
    description = "HTTP from anywhere"
    from_port   = 80
    to_port     = 80
    protocol    = "tcp"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  ingress {
    description = "HTTPS from anywhere"
    from_port   = 443
    to_port     = 443
    protocol    = "tcp"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  egress {
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    protocol    = "-1"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-alb-sg"
  })
}

resource "aws_security_group" "database" {
  name        = "${var.environment}-database-sg"
  description = "Security group for database"
  vpc_id      = aws_vpc.main.id

  ingress {
    description = "PostgreSQL from app"
    from_port   = 5432
    to_port     = 5432
    protocol    = "tcp"
    security_groups = [aws_security_group.app.id]
  }

  ingress {
    description = "Redis from app"
    from_port   = 6379
    to_port     = 6379
    protocol    = "tcp"
    security_groups = [aws_security_group.app.id]
  }

  egress {
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    protocol    = "-1"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-database-sg"
  })
}
```

### modules/networking/variables.tf
```terraform
variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name (dev, staging, production)"
  type        = string
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "CIDR block for VPC"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "public_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "List of public subnet CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24"]
}

variable "private_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "List of private subnet CIDR blocks"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.10.0/24", "10.0.20.0/24"]
}

variable "availability_zones" {
  description = "List of availability zones"
  type        = list(string)
}

variable "enable_nat_gateway" {
  description = "Enable NAT Gateway for private subnets"
  type        = bool
  default     = true
}

variable "bastion_security_group_id" {
  description = "Security group ID for bastion host"
  type        = string
  default     = ""
}

variable "tags" {
  description = "Additional tags"
  type        = map(string)
  default     = {}
}
```

### modules/networking/outputs.tf
```terraform
output "vpc_id" {
  description = "VPC ID"
  value       = aws_vpc.main.id
}

output "public_subnet_ids" {
  description = "List of public subnet IDs"
  value       = aws_subnet.public[*].id
}

output "private_subnet_ids" {
  description = "List of private subnet IDs"
  value       = aws_subnet.private[*].id
}

output "app_security_group_id" {
  description = "Application security group ID"
  value       = aws_security_group.app.id
}

output "alb_security_group_id" {
  description = "ALB security group ID"
  value       = aws_security_group.alb.id
}

output "database_security_group_id" {
  description = "Database security group ID"
  value       = aws_security_group.database.id
}
```

## 2. Módulo de Compute (modules/compute/)

### modules/compute/main.tf
```terraform
# Compute Module - ALB, Launch Template, Auto Scaling
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
  }
}

# Application Load Balancer
resource "aws_lb" "main" {
  name               = "${var.environment}-alb"
  internal           = false
  load_balancer_type = "application"
  security_groups    = [var.alb_security_group_id]
  subnets           = var.public_subnet_ids

  enable_deletion_protection = var.environment == "production"

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-alb"
  })
}

resource "aws_lb_target_group" "app" {
  name     = "${var.environment}-app-tg"
  port     = 80
  protocol = "HTTP"
  vpc_id   = var.vpc_id

  health_check {
    enabled             = true
    interval            = 30
    path                = "/health"
    port                = "traffic-port"
    protocol            = "HTTP"
    timeout             = 5
    healthy_threshold   = 2
    unhealthy_threshold = 2
    matcher             = "200"
  }

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-app-tg"
  })
}

resource "aws_lb_listener" "http" {
  load_balancer_arn = aws_lb.main.arn
  port              = "80"
  protocol          = "HTTP"

  default_action {
    type = "redirect"

    redirect {
      port        = "443"
      protocol    = "HTTPS"
      status_code = "HTTP_301"
    }
  }
}

resource "aws_lb_listener" "https" {
  load_balancer_arn = aws_lb.main.arn
  port              = "443"
  protocol          = "HTTPS"
  ssl_policy        = "ELBSecurityPolicy-2016-08"
  certificate_arn   = var.certificate_arn

  default_action {
    type             = "forward"
    target_group_arn = aws_lb_target_group.app.arn
  }
}

# Launch Template
resource "aws_launch_template" "app" {
  name_prefix   = "${var.environment}-app-"
  image_id      = var.ami_id
  instance_type = var.instance_type
  key_name      = var.key_name

  vpc_security_group_ids = [var.app_security_group_id]

  iam_instance_profile {
    name = aws_iam_instance_profile.app.name
  }

  block_device_mappings {
    device_name = "/dev/xvda"

    ebs {
      volume_size = var.root_volume_size
      volume_type = "gp3"
      encrypted   = true
    }
  }

  user_data = base64encode(templatefile("${path.module}/user_data.sh", {
    environment = var.environment
    app_version = var.app_version
  }))

  tag_specifications {
    resource_type = "instance"

    tags = merge(var.tags, {
      Name = "${var.environment}-app-instance"
    })
  }

  tag_specifications {
    resource_type = "volume"

    tags = merge(var.tags, {
      Name = "${var.environment}-app-volume"
    })
  }

  lifecycle {
    create_before_destroy = true
  }
}

# IAM Role for EC2
resource "aws_iam_role" "app" {
  name = "${var.environment}-app-role"

  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Action = "sts:AssumeRole"
        Effect = "Allow"
        Principal = {
          Service = "ec2.amazonaws.com"
        }
      }
    ]
  })

  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "ssm" {
  role       = aws_iam_role.app.name
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonSSMManagedInstanceCore"
}

  role       = aws_iam_role.app.name
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/CloudWatchAgentServerPolicy"
}

resource "aws_iam_instance_profile" "app" {
  name = "${var.environment}-app-profile"
  role = aws_iam_role.app.name
}

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# User data script for application instances
set -e

# Environment variables
export ENVIRONMENT="${environment}"
export APP_VERSION="${app_version}"

# Update system
apt-get update -y
apt-get upgrade -y

# Install dependencies
apt-get install -y \
  docker.io \
  docker-compose \
  nginx \
  awscli \
  jq \
  curl \
  wget

# Configure Docker
usermod -aG docker ubuntu
systemctl enable docker
systemctl start docker

# Create application directory
mkdir -p /opt/diyapp
cd /opt/diyapp

# Create docker-compose.yml
cat > docker-compose.yml << 'EOF'
version: '3.8'
services:
  app:
    image: diyapp:${APP_VERSION}
    restart: always
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=${ENVIRONMENT}
      - APP_VERSION=${APP_VERSION}
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
      - ./config:/app/config
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8080/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    restart: always
    ports:
      - "80:80"
    volumes:
      - ./nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
    depends_on:
      - app
EOF

# Create nginx configuration
cat > nginx.conf << 'EOF'
events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    upstream app_backend {
        server app:8080;
    }

    server {
        listen 80;
        server_name _;

        location /health {
            proxy_pass http://app_backend/health;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            access_log off;
        }

        location / {
            proxy_pass http

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Threat Modeling e Reforço de Segurança

## 1. Análise de Threat Modeling (STRIDE) - V12 Core

### Ativos Críticos Identificados:
1. **Dados de Usuário**: Credenciais, tokens de sessão, dados pessoais
2. **Sistema de Autenticação**: JWT, OAuth, MFA
3. **API Endpoints**: REST/GraphQL endpoints com dados sensíveis
4. **Banco de Dados**: PostgreSQL com PII
5. **Integrações Externas**: WhatsApp API, serviços de terceiros
6. **Sistema de Logs**: Informações de auditoria e debugging
7. **Configurações de Infra**: Secrets, chaves de API, variáveis de ambiente

### Ameaças STRIDE por Componente:

#### A. Sistema de Autenticação (Spoofing, Tampering, Repudiation)
- **S1**: Token JWT roubado/reutilizado
- **S2**: Credenciais fracas sem validação
- **T1**: Manipulação de token JWT no cliente
- **T2**: Ataque de reutilização de token
- **R1**: Usuário nega ação privilegiada sem logs adequados

#### B. API Endpoints (Tampering, Info Disclosure, DoS)
- **T3**: SQL Injection em endpoints de consulta
- **T4**: XSS através de inputs de usuário
- **I1**: Exposição de dados sensíveis em respostas de erro
- **I2**: IDOR (Insecure Direct Object Reference)
- **D1**: Ataque de força bruta em endpoints de login
- **D2**: DDoS através de endpoints públicos

#### C. Banco de Dados (Info Disclosure, Tampering)
- **I3**: PII não criptografado em repouso
- **I4**: Logs de banco com dados sensíveis
- **T5**: Acesso não autorizado via credenciais vazadas

#### D. Integrações WhatsApp (Spoofing, Info Disclosure)
- **S3**: Spoofing de número de WhatsApp
- **I5**: Vazamento de mensagens privadas
- **T6**: Manipulação de webhooks

#### E. Sistema LLM (Prompt Injection, Data Exfiltration)
- **S4**: Prompt injection para extrair system prompt
- **I6**: Exfiltração de dados via respostas do modelo
- **T7**: Manipulação de output para executar código

## 2. Implementação de Controles de Segurança

### Arquitetura de Segurança V12:

```
src/security/
├── auth/
│   ├── jwt-strategy.js
│   ├── mfa-manager.js
│   └── session-monitor.js
├── validation/

│   ├── schema-validator.js
│   └── llm-output-sanitizer.js
├── waf/

│   ├── request-validator.js
│   └── ddos-protection.js
├── encryption/
│   ├── data-encryption.js
│   └── key-rotation.js
└── monitoring/
    ├── security-logger.js
    └── threat-detector.js
```

### 2.1 Sistema de Autenticação Reforçado

**src/security/auth/jwt-strategy.js**
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const { RateLimiterMemory } = require('rate-limiter-flexible');

class JWTSecurityManager {
    constructor() {
        this.jwtSecret = process.env.JWT_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
        this.refreshSecret = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
        
        // Rate limiter para tentativas de login
        this.loginRateLimiter = new RateLimiterMemory({
            points: 5, // 5 tentativas
            duration: 900, // em 15 minutos
            blockDuration: 1800 // Bloqueia por 30 minutos após exceder
        });
        
        // Token blacklist para logout
        this.tokenBlacklist = new Set();
        this.setupCleanupInterval();
    }

    setupCleanupInterval() {
        // Limpa tokens expirados da blacklist a cada hora
        setInterval(() => {
            const now = Date.now();
            for (const [token, expiry] of this.tokenBlacklist.entries()) {
                if (expiry < now) {
                    this.tokenBlacklist.delete(token);
                }
            }
        }, 3600000);
    }

    async generateTokens(user, deviceInfo) {
        const accessToken = jwt.sign(
            {
                userId: user.id,
                role: user.role,
                sessionId: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
                deviceFingerprint: this.generateDeviceFingerprint(deviceInfo)
            },
            this.jwtSecret,
            { 
                expiresIn: '15m', // Access token curto
                algorithm: 'HS256'
            }
        );

        const refreshToken = jwt.sign(
            {
                userId: user.id,
                sessionId: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
                tokenVersion: user.tokenVersion || 0
            },
            this.refreshSecret,
            { 
                expiresIn: '7d',
                algorithm: 'HS256'
            }
        );

        // Registrar sessão
        await this.recordSession(user.id, deviceInfo, accessToken);

        return { accessToken, refreshToken };
    }

    generateDeviceFingerprint(deviceInfo) {
        const data = `${deviceInfo.userAgent}-${deviceInfo.ip}-${deviceInfo.acceptLanguage}`;
        return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(data).digest('hex');
    }

    async verifyAccessToken(token, deviceInfo) {
        // Verificar blacklist
        if (this.tokenBlacklist.has(token)) {
            throw new Error('Token revoked');
        }

        try {
            const decoded = jwt.verify(token, this.jwtSecret, { algorithms: ['HS256'] });
            
            // Verificar fingerprint do dispositivo
            const currentFingerprint = this.generateDeviceFingerprint(deviceInfo);
            if (decoded.deviceFingerprint !== currentFingerprint) {
                // Dispositivo diferente - requer reautenticação
                await this.revokeUserSessions(decoded.userId);
                throw new Error('Device mismatch - reauthentication required');
            }

            return decoded;
        } catch (error) {
            if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
                throw new Error('Token expired');
            }
            throw new Error('Invalid token');
        }
    }

    async revokeToken(token) {
        try {
            const decoded = jwt.decode(token);
            if (decoded && decoded.exp) {
                this.tokenBlacklist.add(token);
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Error revoking token:', error);
        }
    }

    async revokeUserSessions(userId) {
        // Implementar lógica para revogar todas as sessões do usuário
        // Isso invalidaria todos os tokens ativos
        // Atualizar tokenVersion no banco de dados
    }

    async recordSession(userId, deviceInfo, token) {
        // Registrar sessão no banco de dados para auditoria
        const sessionRecord = {
            userId,
            deviceInfo,
            tokenHash: crypto.createHash('sha256').update(token).digest('hex'),
            createdAt: new Date(),
            lastActivity: new Date(),
            isActive: true
        };
        
        // Salvar no banco de dados
        // Implementar limpeza de sessões antigas
    }
}

module.exports = JWTSecurityManager;
```

**src/security/auth/mfa-manager.js**
```javascript
const speakeasy = require('speakeasy');
const QRCode = require('qrcode');
const crypto = require('crypto');

class MFAManager {
    constructor() {
        this.mfaAttempts = new Map();
        this.setupCleanupInterval();
    }

    setupCleanupInterval() {
        // Limpa tentativas MFA antigas a cada 5 minutos
        setInterval(() => {
            const now = Date.now();
            for (const [key, data] of this.mfaAttempts.entries()) {
                if (now - data.timestamp > 300000) { // 5 minutos
                    this.mfaAttempts.delete(key);
                }
            }
        }, 300000);
    }

    generateSecret(userId) {
        const secret = speakeasy.generateSecret({
            name: `DIYAPP:${userId}`,
            length: 20
        });

        return {
            secret: secret.base32,
            otpauthUrl: secret.otpauth_url
        };
    }

    async generateQRCode(otpauthUrl) {
        try {
            return await QRCode.toDataURL(otpauthUrl);
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error('Failed to generate QR code');
        }
    }

    verifyToken(secret, token, userId) {
        const attemptKey = `mfa:${userId}:${token}`;
        
        // Verificar rate limiting
        if (this.mfaAttempts.has(attemptKey)) {
            throw new Error('Too many attempts');
        }

        const verified = speakeasy.totp.verify({
            secret: secret,
            encoding: 'base32',
            token: token,
            window: 1 // Permite 30 segundos de diferença
        });

        if (!verified) {
            // Registrar tentativa falha
            this.mfaAttempts.set(attemptKey, {
                timestamp: Date.now(),
                attempts: (this.mfaAttempts.get(attemptKey)?.attempts || 0) + 1
            });
            
            // Bloquear após 5 tentativas falhas
            const attempts = this.mfaAttempts.get(attemptKey)?.attempts || 0;
            if (attempts >= 5) {
                // Bloquear usuário por 15 minutos
                setTimeout(() => {
                    this.mfaAttempts.delete(attemptKey);
                }, 900000);
                throw new Error('MFA blocked for 15 minutes');
            }
            
            throw new Error('Invalid MFA token');
        }

        // Limpar tentativas após sucesso
        this.mfaAttempts.delete(attemptKey);
        
        return true;
    }

    generateBackupCodes(count = 10) {
        const codes = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
            codes.push({
                code: crypto.randomBytes(4).toString('hex').toUpperCase(),
                used: false,
                createdAt: new Date()
            });
        }
        return codes;
    }
}

module.exports = MFAManager;
```

### 2.2 Sanitização de Inputs e Validação

**src/security/validation/input-sanitizer.js**
```javascript
const xss = require('xss');
const validator = require('validator');

class InputSanitizer {
    constructor() {
        this.xssOptions = {
            whiteList: {}, // Empty object means no HTML allowed
            stripIgnoreTag: true,
            stripIgnoreTagBody: ['script', 'style', 'iframe', 'object', 'embed']
        };
    }

    sanitizeInput(input, type = 'string') {
        if (input === null || input === undefined) {
            return input;
        }

        switch (type) {
            case 'string':
                return this.sanitizeString(input);
            case 'email':
                return this.sanitizeEmail(input);
            case 'url':
                return this.sanitizeURL(input);
            case 'html':
                return this.sanitizeHTML(input);
            case 'number':
                return this.sanitizeNumber(input);
            case 'json':
                return this.sanitizeJSON(input);
            default:
                return this.sanitizeString(input);
        }
    }

    sanitizeString(input) {
        if (typeof input !== 'string') {
            input = String(input);
        }
        
        // Remover null bytes
        input = input.replace(/\0/g, '');
        
        // Remover caracteres de controle (exceto tab, newline, carriage return)
        input = input.replace(/[\x00-\x08\x0B\x0C\x0E-\x1F\x7F]/g, '');
        
        // Trim whitespace
        input = input.trim();
        
        // XSS protection
        input = xss(input, this.xssOptions);
        
        return input;
    }

    sanitizeEmail(email) {
        if (!validator.isEmail(email)) {
            throw new Error('Invalid email format');
        }
        
        // Normalizar email
        email = validator.normalizeEmail(email, {
            all_lowercase: true,
            gmail_remove_dots: false,
            gmail_remove_subaddress: false,
            outlookdotcom_remove_subaddress: false,
            yahoo_remove_subaddress: false,
            icloud_remove_subaddress: false
        });
        
        return email;
    }

    sanitizeURL(url) {
        if (!validator.isURL(url, {
            require_protocol: true,
            protocols: ['http', 'https'],
            require_valid_protocol: true
        })) {
            throw new Error('Invalid URL format');
        }
        
        return url;
    }

    sanitizeHTML(html) {
        // Configuração mais permissiva para HTML, mas ainda segura
        const htmlOptions = {
            whiteList: {
                a: ['href', 'title', 'target'],
                p: [],
                br: [],
                strong: [],
                em: [],
                ul: [],
                ol: [],
                li: [],
                h1: [], h2: [], h3: [], h4: [], h5: [], h6: []
            },
            stripIgnoreTag: true,
            onTagAttr: (tag, name, value) => {
                // Sanitizar atributos específicos
                if (name === 'href') {
                    if (!validator.isURL(value, { require_protocol: true })) {
                        return '';
                    }
                    // Permitir apenas http/https
                    if (!value.startsWith('http://') && !value.startsWith('https://')) {
                        return '';
                    }
                }
                if (name === 'target' && value !== '_blank') {
                    return '';
                }
                return `${name}="${xss.escapeAttrValue(value)}"`;
            }
        };
        
        return xss(html, htmlOptions);
    }

    sanitizeNumber(input) {
        const num = Number(input);
        if (isNaN(num)) {
            throw new Error('Invalid number');
        }
        
        // Prevenir números muito grandes (prevenção de overflow)
        if (!Number.isFinite(num)) {
            throw new Error('Number too large');
        }
        
        return num;
    }

    sanitizeJSON(input) {
        try {
            const parsed = JSON.parse(input);
            
            // Função recursiva para sanitizar objetos JSON
            const sanitizeObject = (obj) => {
                if (Array.isArray(obj)) {
                    return obj.map(item => sanitizeObject(item));
                } else if (obj !== null && typeof obj === 'object') {
                    const sanitized = {};
                    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
                        const sanitizedKey = this.sanitizeString(key);
                        sanitized[sanitizedKey] = sanitizeObject(value);
                    }
                    return sanitized;
                } else if (typeof obj === 'string') {
                    return this.sanitizeString(obj);
                }
                return obj;
            };
            
            return sanitizeObject(parsed);
        } catch (error) {
            throw new Error('Invalid JSON');
        }
    }

    // Validação específica para SQL Injection
    sanitizeSQL(input) {
        if (typeof input !== 'string') {
            return input;
        }
        
        // Lista de palavras-chave SQL perigosas
        const sqlKeywords = [
            'SELECT', 'INSERT', 'UPDATE', 'DELETE', 'DROP', 'UNION', 
            'OR', 'AND', 'WHERE', 'FROM', 'JOIN', 'HAVING', 'GROUP BY',
            'ORDER BY', 'LIMIT', 'OFFSET', '--', '/*', '*/', ';'
        ];
        
        const upperInput = input.toUpperCase();
        for (const keyword of sqlKeywords) {
            // Verificar se a palavra-chave aparece como palavra completa
            const regex = new RegExp(`\\b${keyword}\\b`, 'i');
            if (regex.test(input)) {
                throw new Error(`Potential SQL injection detected: ${keyword}`);
            }
        }
        
        return input;
    }

    // Validação para prevenir NoSQL injection
    sanitizeNoSQL(input) {
        if (typeof input === 'object' && input !== null) {
            const stringified = JSON.stringify(input);
            if (stringified.includes('$where') || 
                stringified.includes('$regex') ||
                stringified.includes('$ne') ||
                stringified.includes('$gt') ||
                stringified.includes('$lt')) {
                throw new Error('Potential NoSQL injection detected');
            }
        }
        return input;
    }
}

module.exports = InputSanitizer;
```

**src/security/validation/schema-validator.js**

const Joi = require('joi');

class SchemaValidator {
    constructor() {
        this.schemas = {
            userRegistration: Joi.object({
                email: Joi.string().email().required().normalize(),
                password: Joi.string()
                    .min(12)
                    .pattern(new RegExp('^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\\d)(?=.*[@$!%*?&])[A-Za-z\\d@$!%*?&]{12,}$'))
                    .required()
                    .messages({
                        'string.pattern.base': 'Password must contain at least one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter, one number and one special character',
                        'string.min': 'Password must be at least 12 characters long'
                    }),
                name: Joi.string().min(2).max(100).required(),
                phone: Joi.string().pattern(/^\+?[1-9]\d{1,14}$/).optional()
            }),

            userLogin: Joi.object({
                email: Joi.string().email().required(),
                password: Joi.string().required(),
                mfaToken: J

## 1. Testes de Carga com k6

### `tests/load/config/scenarios.js`
```javascript
// Configurações de cenários de carga
export const scenarios = {
  // Cenário 1: Carga normal de usuários
  normal_load: {
    executor: 'ramping-vus',
    startVUs: 0,
    stages: [
      { duration: '2m', target: 100 },  // Ramp up para 100 usuários
      { duration: '5m', target: 100 },  // Estabiliza em 100 usuários
      { duration: '2m', target: 0 },    // Ramp down
    ],
    gracefulRampDown: '30s',
    tags: { test_type: 'load' },
  },

  // Cenário 2: Pico de carga
  spike_load: {
    executor: 'ramping-vus',
    startVUs: 0,
    stages: [
      { duration: '1m', target: 500 },  // Spike rápido
      { duration: '2m', target: 500 },  // Mantém pico
      { duration: '1m', target: 0 },    // Retorna rápido
    ],
    tags: { test_type: 'spike' },
  },

  // Cenário 3: Carga sustentada
  endurance_load: {
    executor: 'constant-vus',
    vus: 50,
    duration: '30m',
    tags: { test_type: 'endurance' },
  },

  // Cenário 4: Teste de estresse
  stress_load: {
    executor: 'ramping-vus',
    startVUs: 0,
    stages: [
      { duration: '5m', target: 1000 },
      { duration: '10m', target: 1000 },
      { duration: '5m', target: 0 },
    ],
    tags: { test_type: 'stress' },
  },
};

// Limites de performance
export const thresholds = {
  http_req_duration: ['p(95)<500', 'p(99)<1000'], // 95% < 500ms, 99% < 1000ms
  http_req_failed: ['rate<0.01'],                 // Taxa de erro < 1%
  iteration_duration: ['p(95)<2000'],             // 95% das iterações < 2s
  vus: ['value>0'],                               // Garantir que há VUs ativos
  checks: ['rate>0.99'],                          // 99% dos checks devem passar
};
```

### `tests/load/scripts/main-test.js`
```javascript
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep } from 'k6';
import { scenarios, thresholds } from '../config/scenarios.js';
import { generateTestData } from '../utils/data-generator.js';

// Configuração principal
export const options = {
  scenarios: scenarios,
  thresholds: thresholds,
  discardResponseBodies: false,
  userAgent: 'DIYAPP-k6-load-test/1.0',
};

// URL base da aplicação
const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000';

// Headers comuns
const headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'User-Agent': 'DIYAPP-Test-Suite',
};

// Funções de teste
export function setup() {
  console.log(`Iniciando testes de carga em: ${BASE_URL}`);
  return { testData: generateTestData() };
}

// Teste de health check
export function healthCheck() {
  const url = `${BASE_URL}/api/health`;
  const res = http.get(url, { headers: headers });
  
  check(res, {
    'health check status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'health check response time < 200ms': (r) => r.timings.duration < 200,
    'health check has uptime': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).uptime > 0,
  });
}

// Teste de API principal
export function mainAPI(data) {
  const url = `${BASE_URL}/api/v1/process`;
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    action: 'process',
    data: data.testData.getRandom(),
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  });

  const res = http.post(url, payload, { headers: headers });

  check(res, {
    'API status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'API response time < 800ms': (r) => r.timings.duration < 800,
    'API has valid response': (r) => {
      const body = JSON.parse(r.body);
      return body.success === true && body.id !== undefined;
    },
  });
}

// Teste de consulta
export function queryAPI(data) {
  const queryId = data.testData.getRandomId();
  const url = `${BASE_URL}/api/v1/query/${queryId}`;
  
  const res = http.get(url, { headers: headers });

  check(res, {
    'Query status 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'Query response time < 500ms': (r) => r.timings.duration < 500,
    'Query returns data': (r) => {
      const body = JSON.parse(r.body);
      return body.data !== undefined;
    },
  });
}

// Teste de upload de arquivo
export function uploadTest(data) {
  const url = `${BASE_URL}/api/v1/upload`;
  const fileContent = data.testData.getRandomFile();
  
  const payload = {
    file: http.file(fileContent, 'test-file.txt', 'text/plain'),
    metadata: JSON.stringify({
      name: 'test-file',
      size: fileContent.length,
    }),
  };

  const res = http.post(url, payload, { headers: { ...headers, 'Content-Type': 'multipart/form-data' } });

  check(res, {
    'Upload status 201': (r) => r.status === 201,
    'Upload response time < 1000ms': (r) => r.timings.duration < 1000,
    'Upload returns fileId': (r) => {
      const body = JSON.parse(r.body);
      return body.fileId !== undefined;
    },
  });
}

// Fluxo principal de execução
export default function (data) {
  // Executa health check em 20% das iterações
  if (Math.random() < 0.2) {
    healthCheck();
    sleep(0.5);
  }

  // Executa API principal em 60% das iterações
  if (Math.random() < 0.6) {
    mainAPI(data);
    sleep(1);
  }

  // Executa consulta em 40% das iterações
  if (Math.random() < 0.4) {
    queryAPI(data);
    sleep(0.8);
  }

  // Executa upload em 10% das iterações
  if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
    uploadTest(data);
    sleep(2);
  }
}

export function teardown(data) {
  console.log('Testes de carga finalizados');
  // Aqui poderíamos enviar métricas para um sistema de monitoramento
}
```

### `tests/load/utils/data-generator.js`
```javascript
// Gerador de dados de teste para k6
export class TestDataGenerator {
  constructor() {
    this.users = [];
    this.ids = [];
    this.files = [];
    this.initialize();
  }

  initialize() {
    // Gerar 1000 usuários de teste
    for (let i = 0; i < 1000; i++) {
      this.users.push({
        id: `user_${i}`,
        name: `Test User ${i}`,
        email: `user${i}@test.com`,
        data: {
          value: Math.random() * 1000,
          timestamp: new Date(Date.now() - Math.random() * 1000000000).toISOString(),
        },
      });
      this.ids.push(`id_${i}`);
    }

    // Gerar arquivos de teste
    for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
      const size = Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000) + 100;
      this.files.push(this.generateRandomFile(size));
    }
  }

  generateRandomFile(size) {
    const chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789\n\r\t';
    let content = '';
    for (let i = 0; i < size; i++) {
      content += chars.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length));
    }
    return content;
  }

  getRandom() {
    return this.users[Math.floor(Math.random() * this.users.length)];
  }

  getRandomId() {
    return this.ids[Math.floor(Math.random() * this.ids.length)];
  }

  getRandomFile() {
    return this.files[Math.floor(Math.random() * this.files.length)];
  }
}

export function generateTestData() {
  return new TestDataGenerator();
}
```

## 2. Testes de Segurança com OWASP ZAP

### `tests/security/zap-automation.py`
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Automação de testes de segurança com OWASP ZAP para DIYAPP V12
"""

import time
import json
import requests
from zapv2 import ZAPv2
import sys
import os
from datetime import datetime

class SecurityTester:
    def __init__(self, target_url, zap_api_key='', zap_proxy='http://localhost:8080'):
        """
        Inicializa o cliente ZAP
        
        Args:
            target_url: URL alvo para testes
            zap_api_key: Chave da API do ZAP (opcional)
            zap_proxy: Endereço do proxy ZAP
        """
        self.target_url = target_url
        self.zap = ZAPv2(apikey=zap_api_key, proxies={'http': zap_proxy, 'https': zap_proxy})
        self.scan_id = None
        self.report_dir = 'tests/security/reports'
        
        # Criar diretório de relatórios se não existir
        os.makedirs(self.report_dir, exist_ok=True)
    
    def start_spider(self, max_depth=5):
        """
        Inicia spider para descobrir URLs
        
        Args:
            max_depth: Profundidade máxima de crawling
        """
        print(f"[INFO] Iniciando spider em {self.target_url}")
        
        scan_id = self.zap.spider.scan(
            url=self.target_url,
            maxchildren=max_depth,
            recurse=True,
            subtreeonly=False
        )
        
        # Aguardar spider completar
        while int(self.zap.spider.status(scan_id)) < 100:
            print(f"[INFO] Spider progresso: {self.zap.spider.status(scan_id)}%")
            time.sleep(2)
        
        print("[INFO] Spider completado")
        
        # Listar URLs encontradas
        urls = self.zap.spider.results(scan_id)
        print(f"[INFO] {len(urls)} URLs encontradas")
        
        return urls
    
    def start_active_scan(self, policy='Default Policy'):
        """
        Inicia varredura ativa
        
        Args:
            policy: Política de varredura a ser usada
        """
        print(f"[INFO] Iniciando varredura ativa com política: {policy}")
        
        self.scan_id = self.zap.ascan.scan(
            url=self.target_url,
            recurse=True,
            inscopeonly=True,
            scanpolicyname=policy,
            method=None,
            postdata=True
        )
        
        return self.scan_id
    
    def monitor_scan_progress(self):
        """
        Monitora progresso da varredura ativa
        """
        if not self.scan_id:
            print("[ERRO] Nenhuma varredura ativa em andamento")
            return
        
        while int(self.zap.ascan.status(self.scan_id)) < 100:
            status = self.zap.ascan.status(self.scan_id)
            print(f"[INFO] Varredura ativa progresso: {status}%")
            
            # Mostrar alertas encontrados até agora
            alerts = self.zap.core.alerts(baseurl=self.target_url)
            high_alerts = [a for a in alerts if a['risk'] == 'High']
            if high_alerts:
                print(f"[ALERTA] {len(high_alerts)} alertas de alto risco encontrados")
            
            time.sleep(10)
        
        print("[INFO] Varredura ativa completada")
    
    def run_ajax_spider(self):
        """
        Executa spider AJAX para aplicações modernas
        """
        print("[INFO] Iniciando spider AJAX")
        
        self.zap.ajaxSpider.scan(self.target_url, inscope=True)
        
        # Aguardar spider AJAX completar
        while self.zap.ajaxSpider.status == 'running':
            print(f"[INFO] AJAX Spider status: {self.zap.ajaxSpider.status}")
            time.sleep(5)
        
        print("[INFO] AJAX Spider completado")
    
    def run_full_security_scan(self):
        """
        Executa varredura de segurança completa
        """
        print(f"[INFO] Iniciando varredura de segurança completa em {self.target_url}")
        
        # Passo 1: Spider tradicional
        self.start_spider()
        
        # Passo 2: Spider AJAX (para SPAs)
        self.run_ajax_spider()
        
        # Passo 3: Varredura passiva (aguardar alguns minutos)
        print("[INFO] Aguardando varredura passiva (2 minutos)...")
        time.sleep(120)
        
        # Passo 4: Varredura ativa
        scan_id = self.start_active_scan()
        self.monitor_scan_progress()
        
        # Passo 5: Aguardar processamento pós-varredura
        print("[INFO] Processando resultados...")
        time.sleep(30)
        
        return scan_id
    
    def generate_report(self, format='html'):
        """
        Gera relatório da varredura
        
        Args:
            format: Formato do relatório (html, json, xml, md)
        """
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')
        filename = f"{self.report_dir}/security_scan_{timestamp}"
        
        if format == 'html':
            report = self.zap.core.htmlreport()
            filepath = f"{filename}.html"
            with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(report)
        
        elif format == 'json':
            report = self.zap.core.jsonreport()
            filepath = f"{filename}.json"
            with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                json.dump(json.loads(report), f, indent=2)
        
        elif format == 'xml':
            report = self.zap.core.xmlreport()
            filepath = f"{filename}.xml"
            with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(report)
        
        elif format == 'markdown':
            report = self.zap.core.mdreport()
            filepath = f"{filename}.md"
            with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(report)
        
        print(f"[INFO] Relatório gerado: {filepath}")
        return filepath
    
    def get_alerts_summary(self):
        """
        Retorna resumo dos alertas encontrados
        """
        alerts = self.zap.core.alerts(baseurl=self.target_url)
        
        summary = {
            'total': len(alerts),
            'high': 0,
            'medium': 0,
            'low': 0,
            'informational': 0,
            'alerts_by_type': {}
        }
        
        for alert in alerts:
            risk = alert['risk']
            alert_type = alert['alert']
            
            if risk == 'High':
                summary['high'] += 1
            elif risk == 'Medium':
                summary['medium'] += 1
            elif risk == 'Low':
                summary['low'] += 1
            else:
                summary['informational'] += 1
            
            if
